# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [PolyCrysDiff: Controllable Generation of Three-Dimensional Computable Polycrystalline Material Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11695)
*Chi Chen,Tianle Jiang,Xiaodong Wei,Yanming Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PolyCrysDiff是一种基于条件隐扩散模型（conditional latent diffusion）的框架，能够端到端生成可计算的3D多晶微观结构，在形态、取向分布和空间相关性方面表现优异，并通过晶体塑性有限元模拟验证了生成结构的物理有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维多晶材料的微观结构对其力学和物理性质具有关键影响，但真实可控的微观结构构建仍是巨大挑战。阐明结构-性能关系需要能够生成可计算微观结构的方法。

Method: 提出PolyCrysDiff框架，基于条件隐扩散模型（conditional latent diffusion）实现端到端的3D多晶微观结构生成。通过定性定量评估验证生成质量，并与马尔可夫随机场（Markov random field, MRF）和卷积神经网络（convolutional neural network, CNN）等主流方法进行比较。

Result: PolyCrysDiff能够忠实再现目标晶粒形态、取向分布和3D空间相关性，在晶粒属性（如尺寸和球形度）控制方面达到R²超过0.972，优于MRF和CNN方法。通过晶体塑性有限元方法（crystal plasticity finite element method, CPFEM）模拟验证了生成微观结构的可计算性和物理有效性。

Conclusion: 利用PolyCrysDiff的可控生成能力，系统阐明了晶粒级微观结构特征如何影响多晶材料的力学性能。该发展为加速、数据驱动的多晶材料优化设计迈出了关键一步。

Abstract: The three-dimensional (3D) microstructures of polycrystalline materials exert a critical influence on their mechanical and physical properties. Realistic, controllable construction of these microstructures is a key step toward elucidating structure-property relationships, yet remains a formidable challenge. Herein, we propose PolyCrysDiff, a framework based on conditional latent diffusion that enables the end-to-end generation of computable 3D polycrystalline microstructures. Comprehensive qualitative and quantitative evaluations demonstrate that PolyCrysDiff faithfully reproduces target grain morphologies, orientation distributions, and 3D spatial correlations, while achieving an $R^2$ over 0.972 on grain attributes (e.g., size and sphericity) control, thereby outperforming mainstream approaches such as Markov random field (MRF)- and convolutional neural network (CNN)-based methods. The computability and physical validity of the generated microstructures are verified through a series of crystal plasticity finite element method (CPFEM) simulations. Leveraging PolyCrysDiff's controllable generative capability, we systematically elucidate how grain-level microstructural characteristics affect the mechanical properties of polycrystalline materials. This development is expected to pave a key step toward accelerated, data-driven optimization and design of polycrystalline materials.

</details>


### [2] [A Decade of Generative Adversarial Networks for Porous Material Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11836)
*Ali Sadeghkhani,Brandon Bennett,Masoud Babaei,Arash Rabbani*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了2017年至2026年初发表的96篇同行评议论文，分析了基于生成对抗网络（GANs）的多孔材料图像重建技术的演进与应用，将GAN架构分为六类并评估其在孔隙度精度、渗透率预测和重建体积方面的进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多孔材料的数字化重建在地质储层表征、组织工程和电化学器件设计等领域日益重要。传统方法如微计算机断层扫描和统计重建方法虽已建立基础，但深度学习技术特别是生成对抗网络（Generative Adversarial Networks, GANs）的出现，彻底改变了多孔介质重建能力。

Method: 本文采用系统性综述方法，分析了2017年至2026年初发表的96篇同行评议文章。研究将GAN架构分为六类：Vanilla GANs、多尺度GANs（Multi-Scale GANs）、条件GANs（Conditional GANs）、注意力增强GANs（Attention-Enhanced GANs）、基于风格的GANs（Style-based GANs）和混合架构GANs（Hybrid Architecture GANs）。

Result: 分析显示在孔隙度精度（与原始样品偏差在1%以内）、渗透率预测（平均相对误差降低达79%）和可重建体积（从初始的64³到当前的2,200³体素）方面取得显著进展。研究为基于特定应用需求选择适当的GAN架构提供了全面框架。

Conclusion: 尽管基于GAN的多孔材料重建技术取得了实质性进展，但在计算效率、大规模重建的内存限制以及2D到3D转换中的结构连续性保持方面仍存在持续挑战。该系统性分析为根据具体应用需求选择合适的GAN架构提供了全面指导。

Abstract: Digital reconstruction of porous materials has become increasingly critical for applications ranging from geological reservoir characterization to tissue engineering and electrochemical device design. While traditional methods such as micro-computed tomography and statistical reconstruction approaches have established foundations in this field, the emergence of deep learning techniques, particularly Generative Adversarial Networks (GANs), has revolutionized porous media reconstruction capabilities. This review systematically analyzes 96 peer-reviewed articles published from 2017 to early 2026, examining the evolution and applications of GAN-based approaches for porous material image reconstruction. We categorize GAN architectures into six distinct classes, namely Vanilla GANs, Multi-Scale GANs, Conditional GANs, Attention-Enhanced GANs, Style-based GANs, and Hybrid Architecture GANs. Our analysis reveals substantial progress including improvements in porosity accuracy (within 1% of original samples), permeability prediction (up to 79% reduction in mean relative errors), and achievable reconstruction volumes (from initial $64^3$ to current $2{,}200^3$ voxels). Despite these advances, persistent challenges remain in computational efficiency, memory constraints for large-scale reconstruction, and maintaining structural continuity in 2D-to-3D transformations. This systematic analysis provides a comprehensive framework for selecting appropriate GAN architectures based on specific application requirements.

</details>

# cs.CL [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [MaterialFigBENCH: benchmark dataset with figures for evaluating college-level materials science problem-solving abilities of multimodal large language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11414)
*Michiko Yoshitake,Yuta Suzuki,Ryo Igarashi,Yoshitaka Ushiku,Keisuke Nagato*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MaterialFigBench是一个用于评估多模态大语言模型（multimodal LLMs）在材料科学领域解决需要准确解读图表问题的基准数据集，包含137个自由回答型问题，涵盖相图、应力-应变曲线等关键图表类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准主要依赖文本表示，缺乏对材料科学中图表（如相图、应力-应变曲线、阿伦尼乌斯图等）解读能力的系统评估。这些图表在解决大学级材料科学问题时不可或缺，需要专门的基准来评估多模态LLMs的视觉理解和定量解释能力。

Method: 构建了MaterialFigBench数据集，包含137个改编自标准材料科学教材的自由回答型问题，涵盖晶体结构、力学性能、扩散、相图、相变和材料电子性能等广泛主题。为处理从图像读取数值时不可避免的模糊性，在适当情况下提供了专家定义的答案范围。

Result: 评估了包括通过OpenAI API访问的ChatGPT和GPT模型在内的多个最先进多模态LLMs。结果显示，尽管总体准确率随模型更新而提高，但当前LLMs在材料科学图表的真实视觉理解和定量解释方面仍存在困难。许多情况下，正确答案是通过依赖记忆的领域知识而非读取提供的图像获得的。

Conclusion: MaterialFigBench揭示了多模态LLMs在视觉推理、数值精度和有效数字处理方面的持续弱点，同时也识别了性能有所改善的问题类型。该基准为推进材料科学中的多模态推理能力提供了系统且领域特定的基础，并为指导开发具有更强基于图表理解能力的未来LLMs提供了方向。

Abstract: We present MaterialFigBench, a benchmark dataset designed to evaluate the ability of multimodal large language models (LLMs) to solve university-level materials science problems that require accurate interpretation of figures. Unlike existing benchmarks that primarily rely on textual representations, MaterialFigBench focuses on problems in which figures such as phase diagrams, stress-strain curves, Arrhenius plots, diffraction patterns, and microstructural schematics are indispensable for deriving correct answers. The dataset consists of 137 free-response problems adapted from standard materials science textbooks, covering a broad range of topics including crystal structures, mechanical properties, diffusion, phase diagrams, phase transformations, and electronic properties of materials. To address unavoidable ambiguity in reading numerical values from images, expert-defined answer ranges are provided where appropriate. We evaluate several state-of-the-art multimodal LLMs, including ChatGPT and GPT models accessed via OpenAI APIs, and analyze their performance across problem categories and model versions. The results reveal that, although overall accuracy improves with model updates, current LLMs still struggle with genuine visual understanding and quantitative interpretation of materials science figures. In many cases, correct answers are obtained by relying on memorized domain knowledge rather than by reading the provided images. MaterialFigBench highlights persistent weaknesses in visual reasoning, numerical precision, and significant-digit handling, while also identifying problem types where performance has improved. This benchmark provides a systematic and domain-specific foundation for advancing multimodal reasoning capabilities in materials science and for guiding the development of future LLMs with stronger figure-based understanding.

</details>

### [4] [Le Roy, Lerch and Legendre chi functions and generalised Borel-Le Roy transform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12164)
*Giuseppe Dattoli,Roberto Ricci*

Main category: math.CA

TL;DR: 本文基于修正的指数符号理论（Indicial Umbral Theory, IUT）建立统一框架，研究Le Roy函数、Lerch超越函数和Legendre chi函数等特殊函数的性质与推广，并探讨了Borel-Le Roy变换的作用以及发散级数的重整化技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Le Roy函数近年来因其在分析学中的重要性和在分数阶微分算子应用中的多功能性而受到广泛研究。其他特殊函数如Lerch超越函数和Legendre chi函数在物理统计（玻色-爱因斯坦和费米-狄拉克统计）以及涉及多对数函数和Dirichlet L-级数的纯数学研究中都有应用。

Method: 基于幂级数形式理论的修正指数符号理论（Indicial Umbral Theory, IUT）建立统一框架，在该框架下研究特殊函数的性质与推广。特别地，利用修正的IUT公式纳入Borel-Le Roy变换的作用，并通过适当的求和（resummation）技术探索形式体系向发散级数的扩展。

Result: 提出了基于修正指数符号理论的统一框架，能够系统研究Le Roy函数、Lerch超越函数和Legendre chi函数等特殊函数的性质。该框架成功整合了Borel-Le Roy变换，并建立了向发散级数扩展的形式体系。

Conclusion: 通过基于幂级数形式理论的修正指数符号理论，建立了研究特殊函数的统一框架，该框架不仅能够处理现有函数的性质，还能通过Borel-Le Roy变换和求和技术扩展到发散级数领域。

Abstract: The Le Roy function has been the focus of intensive research in recent years, owing both to its relevance in analysis and its versatility in applications involving fractional differential operators. Other special functions - such as the Lerch transcendent and the Legendre chi function - have found applications ranging from Bose-Einstein and Fermi-Dirac statistics in physics to pure mathematical investigations involving polylogarithms and Dirichlet L-series. In this article, we present a unified framework based on a recent reformulation of Indicial Umbral Theory (IUT) grounded in the formal theory of power series. Within this setting, we study the properties and generalisations of these special functions. In particular, we build upon the revised formulation of IUT to incorporate the role of the Borel-Le Roy transform, and to explore the extension of the formalism to divergent series via appropriate resummation techniques.

</details>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [Dyonic ModMax Black Holes in Kalb-Ramond gravity with a Cloud of Strings as Source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11312)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在弦云（cloud of strings）背景下的Kalb-Ramond引力中，具有ModMax非线性电动力学的双荷（dyonic）黑洞的测地线结构、阴影、热力学和霍金辐射。研究发现三种成分（ModMax电动力学、Kalb-Ramond背景和弦云）的共同存在破坏了渐近平坦性，并通过单一几何因子修改了所有可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索ModMax非线性电动力学、洛伦兹破缺的Kalb-Ramond背景和弦云三者共同作用下的黑洞物理。这些成分的结合破坏了渐近平坦性并引入了全局锥形缺陷，可能产生与标准Reissner-Nordström黑洞可观测区分的现象学。

Method: 研究方法包括解析推导光子球（photon sphere）、临界撞击参数（critical impact parameter）和阴影半径（shadow radius）的表达式。对于大质量测试粒子，确定了最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit）和吸积效率（accretion efficiency）。同时建立了黑洞热力学的第一定律和广义Smarr关系，并计算了谱能量发射率（spectral energy emission rate）。

Result: 研究结果表明，阴影大小同时依赖于非平坦渐近性和双荷的ModMax屏蔽效应。在比热中识别出霍金-佩奇型相变（Hawking-Page-type phase transition），并证明在几何光学极限下，谱能量发射率直接由阴影半径控制。所有可观测量都通过单一几何因子被修改。

Conclusion: 结论表明，ModMax非线性电动力学、Kalb-Ramond背景和弦云三种成分的相互作用产生了一种现象学，在观测上可与标准Reissner-Nordström黑洞区分开来。这为通过黑洞阴影和热力学特征探测这些理论成分提供了可能性。

Abstract: We investigate the geodesic structure, shadow, thermodynamics, and Hawking radiation from a dyonic ModMax black hole in Kalb-Ramond gravity with a cloud of strings. The combined presence of ModMax nonlinear electrodynamics, the Lorentz-violating Kalb-Ramond background, and the string cloud breaks asymptotic flatness and introduces a global conical deficit that modifies all observables through a single geometric prefactor. We derive analytic expressions for the photon sphere, critical impact parameter, and shadow radius, and show that the shadow size depends on both the non-flat asymptotics and the ModMax screening of the dyonic charge. For massive test particles, we determine the innermost stable circular orbit and the accretion efficiency as functions of all model parameters. We also establish the first law of black hole thermodynamics and the generalized Smarr relation for this solution, identify a Hawking-Page-type phase transition in the specific heat, and compute the spectral energy emission rate, which we show is directly governed by the shadow radius in the geometric-optics limit. Our results demonstrate that the interplay of these three ingredients produces a phenomenology observationally distinguishable from standard Reissner-Nordström black holes.

</details>


### [6] [Highly homogeneous and isotropic universes: quasi-dust models and the apparent dark-energy evolution arising from the local gravitational potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11377)
*Leandro G. Gomes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究发展了一类非均匀相对论宇宙学模型，其中包含观测到均匀各向同性空间几何和膨胀的宇宙学观测者，物质行为接近尘埃，并在大尺度上产生有效模型，再现了具有尘埃和运行暗能量项的FLRW行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是发展一类能够包含观测到均匀各向同性但实际非均匀的宇宙学模型，这些模型推广了尘埃FLRW模型，并能够解释大尺度上的暗能量效应作为局部引力势的反作用效应。

Method: 方法基于发展一类非均匀相对论宇宙学模型，其中物质由质量粒子系综组成，其数密度4-矢量守恒，并对局部潮汐力产生粘性响应，通过适当设置当前宇宙中的能量分布来构建模型。

Result: 结果显示这些模型在大尺度上产生有效模型，再现了具有尘埃和运行暗能量项的FLRW行为，有效大尺度状态方程参数原则上可以再现尺度因子的任何多项式，其零阶项为负，光度距离观测暗示大尺度加速，而实际上宇宙在减速。

Conclusion: 结论表明发展了一类能够解释观测到的均匀各向同性但实际非均匀的宇宙学模型，其中暗能量效应作为局部引力势的反作用效应出现，观测到的大尺度加速实际上可能是减速宇宙的表观现象。

Abstract: In this manuscript, we develop a class of inhomogeneous relativistic cosmological models with the following properties: (i) They contain cosmological observers to whom the spatial geometry and the expansion are homogeneous and isotropic; (ii) Matter behaves closely to dust, as it is formed by an ensemble of massive particles whose number density $4$-vector is conserved and reacts viscously to the local tidal forces; (iii) They generalize the dust FLRW model; (iv) They give rise to effective models on large scales that reproduce the FLRW behaviour with dust and a running dark-energy term, which appears as a backreaction effect from the local gravitational potential; (v) By suitably setting the distribution of energy in the current universe, the effective large-scale equation-of-state parameter can reproduce, in principle, any polynomial on the scale factor whose term of order zero is negative; (vi) The luminous distance observations imply an apparent large-scale acceleration, as the deceleration parameter is negative, while in reality the universe is decelerating.

</details>


### [7] [Temperature Fluctuations and quantum corrections near Black Hole Horizon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11386)
*Anamika Avinash Pathak,Swastik Bhattacharya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在欧几里得引力（Euclidean Gravity）框架下研究史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild Black Hole）视界附近温度的空间涨落，发现这些涨落与黑洞的近视界超平移（near-horizon supertranslations）密切相关，并建立了温度修正与超平移之间的多项式泛函关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探究史瓦西黑洞视界附近温度的空间变化涨落，这些涨落在欧几里得引力方法中被考虑。研究试图理解这些温度涨落的物理本质及其与黑洞对称性的关联。

Method: 采用欧几里得引力（Euclidean Gravity）方法分析近视界温度涨落。通过建立温度修正与近视界超平移之间的多项式泛函关系，并计算近视界配分函数（partition function），同时实施微观状态计数以验证结果。

Result: 研究发现温度涨落与近视界超平移密切相关，温度相关的修正项可以表示为近视界超平移的多项式泛函，其中领头阶项正比于近视界超平移荷（supertranslation charge）。微观状态计数在施加超平移对称性约束后得到相同结果。

Conclusion: 近视界配分函数提供了对低能视界物理的直观描述，即对所有可能近视界超平移的求和。这表明近视界物理存在基于替代变量的对偶描述（dual description），这些结果对理解黑洞微观结构具有重要意义。

Abstract: Spatially varying near-horizon fluctuations of temperature of a Schwarzschild Black Hole is considered within the Euclidean Gravity approach. We present evidence that suggests that such fluctuations in temperature are closely related with the near-horizon supertranslations of a Black Hole. This allows one to express the temperature-dependent corrections to the near-horizon part of the Euclidean gravity action or Free energy in terms of polynomial functionals of a near-horizon supertranslation for all orders. The leading order term turns out to be proportional to the near-horizon supertranslation charge. We also show that this same term results from a microscopic state counting of the near-horizon field with the constraint of near-horizon supertranslation symmetry imposed. The constructed near-horizon partition function provides a physically appealing intuitive description of the low-energy part of horizon physics as a sum over all possible near-horizon supertranslations. This suggests a dual description of near-horizon physics in terms of alternate variables. The implications of these results are briefly discussed.

</details>


### [8] [An analogue first law for general closed marginally trapped surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11422)
*Ramon Torres*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文为任意时空中的闭合类光捕获面（closed marginally trapped surfaces）构建了横向第一定律的类比形式，建立了准局域热力学框架，为黑洞热力学提供了基于捕获面而非视界的处理方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞热力学公式主要基于视界（horizon）世界管，但这种方法在某些情况下存在非唯一性或技术复杂性。本文旨在为闭合类光捕获面建立准局域热力学框架，提供更自然的处理方式。

Method: 采用准局域（quasi-local）构造方法，将霍金能量（Hawking energy）作为内能，使用与类光捕获面相关的有效表面引力（effective surface gravity）控制热项，推导出能量变化分为广义热贡献和总功贡献的平衡定律。

Result: 在球对称时空的圆球情况下，该形式主义能够复现预期结果。在半经典平衡和蒸发区域，以及克尔（Kerr）时空的非球对称类光捕获面中，框架仍然适用，表明其在视界处理方法不唯一或技术繁琐的情况下具有优势。

Conclusion: 闭合类光捕获面为真正的准局域黑洞热力学提供了自然舞台，该框架在视界处理方法存在局限性的情况下保持适用性，为黑洞热力学提供了新的研究途径。

Abstract: We formulate an analogue transverse first law for general closed marginally trapped surfaces in arbitrary spacetimes. The construction is intrinsically quasi-local and is attached directly to an individual marginally trapped surface, rather than to a preferred horizon worldtube. Taking the Hawking energy as the internal energy and an invariant effective surface gravity associated with the marginally trapped surface as the quantity controlling the thermal term, we derive a balance law in which the variation of energy splits into a generalized heat contribution and a total work contribution. In this way, the resulting law provides a codimension-two, transverse counterpart to existing horizon-based formulations of black-hole thermodynamics. We show that the formalism reproduces the expected results for round spheres in spherically symmetric spacetimes. We then examine semiclassical equilibrium and evaporating regimes, and extend the analysis to non-spherically symmetric marginally trapped surfaces in Kerr. These examples indicate that the framework remains applicable in situations where a horizon-based treatment is either nonunique or technically cumbersome, and suggest that closed marginally trapped surfaces provide a natural arena for a genuinely quasi-local thermodynamics of black holes.

### [9] [Plasma effects on gravitational lensing and shadow observables of a Kerr-like black hole in a dark matter halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11434)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 等离子体作为黑洞周围的光传播介质，已知会显著改变黑洞阴影的形状和可观测量，这可能影响对事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope）结果的解释。因此需要研究暗物质和等离子体如何影响类克尔（Kerr-like）黑洞的阴影。

Method: 研究分析了在均匀和非均匀等离子体分布下的零测地线（null-geodesics），考察了等离子体对光子轨道的影响如何改变最终的黑洞阴影。同时将理论阴影半径与EHT对M87*和Sgr A*的观测结果进行比较以获得约束条件。

Result: 增加黑洞自旋通常会使阴影半径和形变增大；观测角度减小阴影半径同时减少形变。天体物理上合理的暗物质量对光子轨迹无显著影响。均匀等离子体密度增加会增大阴影半径和形变，而非均匀等离子体则相反。发射率显著依赖于所选等离子体模型，均匀等离子体在强度增加时导致更多发射。

Conclusion: 通过比较理论阴影半径与EHT观测结果，可以推断出理论模型中合理的等离子体分布特性和频率。等离子体模型的选择对黑洞阴影特征和发射率有重要影响，而暗物质在合理范围内对光子轨迹影响不显著。

Abstract: Plasma, as a medium around the black hole for light propagation, is known to visibly alter the shape of its shadow and the observables, which could impact the interpretation of the Event Horizon Telescope results. In this study, we examine how dark matter and non-magnetized, pressureless plasma influence the shadow of a Kerr-like black hole. We analyze the null-geodesics in the presence of both homogeneous and inhomogeneous plasma profiles and show how their influence on photon orbits affects the resulting black hole shadow. Our findings indicate that increasing the black hole's spin generally enlarges both the shadow radius and deformation. Additionally, the viewing angle decreases the shadow radius while reducing deformation as the observer moves farther from the equatorial plane. For this model, astrophysically reasonable amounts of dark matter show no significant impact on the photon trajectories. However, we observe that increasing plasma density increases both the shadow radius and deformation for homogeneous plasma, while it decreases them for inhomogeneous plasma. The emission rate also depends significantly on the model of plasma chosen, with homogeneous plasma causing significantly more emission as plasma strength increases. We also study the constraints obtained from comparing theoretical shadow radii with EHT observations of M87* and Sgr A*, which allows us to infer reasonable plasma distribution properties and frequencies in our theoretical model.

### [10] [Spherically-symmetrical vacuum solution in Freund-Nambu scalar-tensor gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11500)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Scalar--tensor theories of gravity provide a natural extension of general relativity and may predict naked singularities as alternative compact objects. In this work, we investigate a novel exact solution within the Freud--Nambu scalar--tensor gravity framework, generalizing the Janis--Newman--Winicour (JNW) naked singularity spacetime through the introduction of a parameter $q$ coupled to a real scalar field $\varphi$ with mass $μ$. Although the metric remains identical to the JNW solution, the scalar field profile is modified, providing a parametrized deformation of this class of spacetimes. We analyze particle dynamics in this background, including a direct linear coupling between the test particle and the scalar field characterized by the parameter $g_s$. The influence of these parameters on astrophysical observables is studied through the specific angular momentum, the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO), and the radiative efficiency of accretion. We also derive the epicyclic frequencies governing oscillatory motion and explore their implications for quasi-periodic oscillations (QPOs) in black hole binaries. Within the epicyclic resonance model, the upper and lower QPO frequencies depend sensitively on the parameters $n$, $g_s$, and $q$. To constrain the model, we perform a Markov Chain Monte Carlo analysis using twin-peak QPO data from the microquasars XTE~J1550--564 and GRS~1915+105. The resulting black hole masses agree with previous estimates and provide the first observational constraints on the parameters $q$ and $g_s$, indicating that modified gravity effects may leave detectable imprints on strong-field astrophysical phenomena.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究通过分析修正的GTD度量在AdS（Anti-de Sitter）时空中的行为，并在Bardeen AdS黑洞框架下考察不同热力学系综（通过Legendre变换实现）中的表现。研究方法包括对热力学测地线（thermodynamic geodesics）的分析。

Conclusion: 修正的GTD框架在AdS时空和不同热力学系综中均表现出鲁棒性和普适性，为黑洞热力学的微观结构研究提供了更可靠的几何描述工具。

Abstract: Thermodynamic geometry provides a powerful framework for probing the microscopic structure of thermodynamic systems. However, recent work has shown that conventional GTD metrics fail to encode essential physical boundaries of thermodynamic phase space. By modifying the conventional metric structure, three new GTD metrics were previously introduced, which successfully capture these boundaries in regular spacetime. Whether such modified metrics remain viable in different spacetime backgrounds and under changes of thermodynamic ensemble has remained an open question. In this work, I address this issue by investigating the behavior of modified GTD metrics in AdS spacetime and across different thermodynamic ensembles in the framework of Bardeen AdS black hole. An analysis of thermodynamic geodesics demonstrates that the modified GTD metrics consistently respect physical boundaries of the phase space, in contrast to conventional GTD metrics. This behavior is preserved in AdS spacetime and under Legendre transformations, establishing the robustness and universality of the modified GTD framework.

The current accuracy of the scattering waveform obtained by quantum amplitude methods is the one-loop level corresponding to the 3PM order, whereas the 4PM waveform is known up to the 2PN order only as derived within the traditional multipolar-post-Minkowskian formalism. The new results at the 4PM and 5PM orders thus provide a benchmark for future multiloop calculations. The soft limit of the waveform at the leading order in the small-frequency expansion gives the gravitational wave memory, which is evaluated at the 4PM and 5PM orders. A narrow peak on top of a wide plateau in two parameters' distributions indicates a well defined best fit value embedded within a broad region of near-degenerate solutions. This means the data strongly favours one specific parameter value but also permit a wide range with comparable likelihood. Physically, it reflects that the Dark Energy dynamics are locally constrained yet globally insensitive to small parameter variations. An increasing $\log_{10}\left[M(z)/M_{0}\right]$ since $z=3$ signifies that black holes have continuously grown through accretion and mergers within the standard hierarchical formation scenario. Motivation: 研究动机在于评估相对论修正下黑洞的有效引力势，分析中性及带电粒子在各类黑洞时空附近的圆轨道和最内稳定圆轨道（ISCOs），这一现象是纯粹相对论性的。

Method: 采用数学分析和图形化方法研究黑洞的圆轨道和ISCOs，同时处理ISCO的天体物理性质，并推导了无毛猜想（no-hair conjecture）所预测的最一般时空的有效势。

Result: 发现进入ISCO的粒子在不同时空中通过引力辐射过程损失特定能量后最终螺旋进入ISCO；电磁效应显示电荷使圆轨道半径变尖锐，且粒子与黑洞电荷乘积增加会增大ISCO半径。

Conclusion: 成功推导了最一般时空的有效势，验证了无毛猜想的预测，揭示了电荷对圆轨道和ISCO半径的显著影响，为理解黑洞附近粒子动力学提供了重要见解。

Abstract: In this paper we study the effective gravitational potential of Schwarzschild, Kerr, Reissner-Nordström and Kerr-Newman black holes with the relativistic corrections to evaluate the circular orbits and the Innermost Stable Circular Orbits (ISCOs), a purely relativistic phenomenon, of neutral and charged particles in the vicinity of these spacetimes. We study the circular orbits and ISCOs of black holes mathematically and graphically. Moreover, the astrophysical properties of ISCO are also dealt with. We find that the particle entering the ISCO loses a certain amount of energy, in different spacetimes, by gravitational radiative processes, before finally spiraling into ISCO. The electromagnetic effects of different spacetimes show how the charges sharpen the radius of the circular orbits, and the increasing product of particle and black hole charge increases the radius of the ISCO. Most importantly, the effective potential of the most general spacetime, as predicted by the no-hair conjecture, has been derived.

</details>


### [17] [Analytic Singular Slow-roll Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11794)
*V. K. Oikonomou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一类最小耦合标量场理论，能够解析求解哈勃参数和标量场，其暴胀现象学与ACT数据兼容。该宇宙学模型描述了从非奇点有限尺度因子开始，经历慢滚暴胀，最终通过共形异常机制避免压力奇点并实现再加热的演化过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索一类能够解析求解的标量场理论，其暴胀现象学与观测数据兼容，并研究宇宙演化中压力奇点的避免机制。特别关注共形异常（conformal anomaly）在消除经典奇点演化中的作用。

Method: 采用一类最小耦合标量场理论（minimally coupled scalar field theories），能够解析求解哈勃参数（Hubble rate）和标量场。利用Nojiri-Odintsov共形异常机制分析量子效应，并讨论多种可能避免压力奇点的机制。

Result: 该模型暴胀现象学与ACT数据兼容，谱指数（spectral index）在极限情况下趋向于n_S=0.98，张标比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）接近零。宇宙演化从有限尺度因子开始，经历慢滚暴胀（slow-roll inflationary era），共形异常消除了经典压力奇点，同时产生极端粒子创造（extreme particle creation）实现再加热（reheating）。

Conclusion: 该模型提供了一种无需暴胀子（inflaton）振荡或与标准模型粒子多重耦合的再加热机制。共形异常不仅避免了经典奇点，还增强了标量扰动（scalar perturbations），促进了原初黑洞（primordial black holes）形成和次级引力波（secondary gravitational waves）产生。

Abstract: We study a class of minimally coupled scalar field theories which leads to analytic solutions for the Hubble rate and the scalar field. The inflationary phenomenology for this class of models can be studied fully analytically. The resulting phenomenology is compatible with the ACT data and for limiting cases, the spectral index is bluer than the ACT constraints and tends to the value $n_{\mathcal{S}}=0.98$, while in the limiting case, the tensor-to-scalar ratio takes very small values, nearly zero. More importantly, the resulting cosmology describes a Universe that has a finite scale factor at $t=0$, thus non-singular, evolves and expands realizing a slow-roll inflationary era and after that it reaches classically a pressure singularity. Classically, the Universe can pass through this singularity, and a turnaround cosmology is realized with the Universe contracting after the turnaround point. However, before the singularity is realized classically, the quantum phenomena dominate the evolution, avoiding the singularity. Specifically we consider the Nojiri-Odintsov conformal anomaly mechanism and we prove that the conformal anomaly erases the classical singular evolution and at the same time it generates extreme particle creation, which eventually reheats the Universe. Thus in this model the scalar field oscillations and the numerous couplings of the inflaton to the Standard Model particles are not required for reheating. In this context, scalar perturbations are enhanced and thus the formation of primordial black holes and the generation of secondary gravitational waves is enhanced. We also discuss several other mechanisms that may lead to the avoidance of the pressure singularity.

</details>


### [18] [Gravitational baryogenesis beyond the spectator approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11837)
*David S. Pereira,Beatriz A. Fernandes,José Pedro Mimoso*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究重新审视了标准引力重子生成算符 $λ\,\nabla_μR\,J^μ$，将其从旁观者相互作用提升为完整的曲率-物质耦合变分问题，推导了普适场方程并分析了其对弗里德曼方程和引力耦合常数的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准引力重子生成（gravitational-baryogenesis）算符通常被视为旁观者相互作用，但纳入引力作用量后，它定义了真正的曲率-物质耦合变分问题。研究旨在系统分析该算符对引力场方程和宇宙学演化的完整影响。

Method: 通过变分原理处理 $λ\,\nabla_μR\,J^μ$ 算符，推导普适场方程并分离实现依赖的张量项。特别关注矢量密度实现，分析其在平坦FRW度规下的修正弗里德曼方程、Raychaudhuri方程和连续性关系。

Result: 研究发现该理论仅支持部分有效普朗克质量解释 $M_{\rm eff}^2=M_{\rm Pl}^2-2λ\nabla_μJ^μ$，并在重子生成期间产生时间依赖的有效引力耦合。研究量化了旁观者近似受控的条件，并为修正引力理论中的引力重子生成研究提供了基线。

Conclusion: 标准引力重子生成算符作为曲率-物质耦合系统具有丰富物理内涵，其完整处理揭示了旁观者近似之外的新效应，为在标准宇宙学和修正引力框架中的一致实现提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The standard gravitational-baryogenesis operator $λ\,\nabla_μR\,J^μ$, with $λ\equiv ε/M_\ast^{2}$, is usually treated as a spectator interaction that generates an effective chemical potential in a prescribed background. When included in the gravitational action, however, it defines a genuine curvature--matter-coupling variational problem, relevant for the baryon, lepton, and $B\!-\!L$ currents, whether described microscopically by particle-physics operators or macroscopically by a fluid current $J^μ=n_Xu^μ$. Up to a boundary term the interaction is equivalent to $-λR\nabla_μJ^μ$, making its $f(R,{\rm matter})$ character manifest, but the metric equations remain open unless the metric dependence of $J^μ$ is specified. For an arbitrary local realization $J^μ(Ψ,g)$ we derive the universal part of the field equations and isolate the realization-dependent tensor generated by $δ_g J^μ$. In the vector-density realization the explicit $J^α\nabla_αR$ term cancels, but an algebraic term $-λg_{μν}R\nabla_αJ^α$ survives, so the theory admits only a partial effective-Planck-mass interpretation, $M_{\rm eff}^2=M_{\rm Pl}^2-2λ\nabla_μJ^μ$, and a time-dependent effective gravitational coupling during baryogenesis. Specializing to flat FRW with a homogeneous current $J^μ=n_Xu^μ$, we obtain the modified Friedmann and Raychaudhuri equations, the associated continuity relation, and dimensionless diagnostics that quantify when the spectator approximation is controlled. We also discuss the implications for gravitational-baryogenesis studies in modified theories of gravity, providing a consistent GR-side baseline for implementations in both standard cosmology and modified-gravity frameworks.

</details>


### [19] [Screened Simpson-Visser Black Holes with Asymptotically de-Sitter Core](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11921)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Ahmad Al-Badawi,Edilberto O. Silva*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在深入研究屏蔽的辛普森-维瑟正则黑洞解（screened Simpson-Visser regular solution）的物理和观测特性，探索这类正则黑洞的几何结构、热力学行为与观测特征之间的复杂关系。

Method: 研究方法包括：分析黑洞的热力学行为，如霍金温度（Hawking temperature）、吉布斯自由能（Gibbs free energy）和比热（specific heat）；研究时空的测地线结构，包括无质量（光子）和大质量（类时）粒子的运动；考察光子球（photon sphere）、黑洞阴影（black hole shadow）和最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbits, ISCO）；探索黑洞的能量发射率辐射（energy-emission rate radiation）；以及分析黑洞的拓扑方面，包括热力学拓扑和光子球的拓扑性质。

Result: 分析揭示了时空几何（spacetime geometry）、测地线运动（geodesic motion）和黑洞热力学（black hole thermodynamics）之间复杂的相互作用，提供了对这类正则黑洞及其潜在观测后果的深入理解。

Conclusion: 本研究全面展示了屏蔽的辛普森-维瑟正则解的多方面物理特性，为理解这类正则黑洞的几何结构、热力学行为和观测特征之间的内在联系提供了系统框架。

Abstract: In this work, we introduce a screened Simpson-Visser regular solution and perform a comprehensive study of its physical and observational properties. We begin by analyzing the thermodynamic behavior of the black hole, including detailed investigations of the Hawking temperature, Gibbs free energy, and specific heat, which provide insights into its stability and phase structure. Next, we examine the geodesic structure of the spacetime, considering both massless (photon) and massive (timelike) particles. In particular, we study the photon sphere, the corresponding black hole shadow, and the innermost stable circular orbits (ISCO), which are crucial for understanding the motion of matter and light around the black hole. Furthermore, we explore the black hole's energy-emission rate radiation, highlighting the effects of the modified geometry on observational signatures. Finally, we investigate the topological aspects of the black hole, analyzing both the thermodynamic topology and the photon sphere's topological properties. Our analysis demonstrates the intricate interplay between the spacetime geometry, geodesic motion, and black hole thermodynamics, offering a deeper understanding of this class of regular black holes and their potential observational consequences.

### [20] [Assessing the robustness of amortized simulation-based inference to transient noise in gravitational-wave ringdowns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12032)
*Song-Tao Liu,Tian-Yang Sun,Yu-Xin Wang,Yong-Xin Zhang,Shang-Jie Jin,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于摊销神经后验估计的模拟推理方法，用于直接从引力波（GW）环降信号中估计黑洞参数，实现了比传统马尔可夫链方法快数个数量级的推理速度，同时保持了统计一致性和有效的置信度覆盖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波（GW）双星系统发出的信号使人们能够在强场区域对广义相对论进行精确检验。随着当前和下一代引力波探测器的改进，开发无需似然函数的参数推断方法至关重要，特别是在面临非标准噪声、部分数据或不完整信号模型等挑战时，这些情况阻碍了分析似然函数的使用。

Method: 本研究提出了一种摊销模拟推理策略，直接估计环降参数。该方法基于摊销神经后验估计，训练一个神经密度估计器来估计先验范围内所有数据段的后验分布。

Result: 训练后的摊销网络在参数估计方面与成熟的马尔可夫链方法相比，实现了统计一致性并具有有效的置信度覆盖，同时推理速度提高了数个数量级。研究还评估了方法对瞬态噪声污染的鲁棒性，发现毛刺注入的时机对估计偏差有决定性影响，特别是在信息稀疏的信号尾部。

Conclusion: 该研究不仅为环降分析提供了一个高效准确的推理框架，而且为未来引力波天文学在现实噪声环境中开发鲁棒的数据处理流程奠定了基础。研究还发现毛刺强度与估计误差正相关，但在低信噪比时影响有限，质量和自旋参数对噪声最为敏感。

Abstract: Gravitational waves (GW) emitted by binary systems allow us to perform precision tests of general relativity in the strong field regime. Ringdown signals allow for probing black hole mass and spin with high precision in GW astronomy. With improvements in current and next-generation GW detectors, developing likelihood-free parameter inference methods is crucial. This is especially important when facing challenges such as non-standard noise, partial data, or incomplete signal models that prevent the use of analytical likelihood functions. In this work, we propose an amortized simulation-based inference strategy to estimate ringdown parameters directly. Specifically, our method is based on amortized neural posterior estimation, which trains a neural density estimator of the posterior for all data segments within the prior range. The results show that our trained amortized network achieves statistically consistent parameter estimates with valid confidence coverage compared to established Markov-chain methods, while offering inference speeds that are orders of magnitude faster. Furthermore, we evaluate the robustness of the method against transient noise contamination. Our analysis reveals that the timing of glitch injection has a decisive impact on estimation bias, particularly during the tail of a signal with sparse information. Glitch strength is positively correlated with estimation error, but has limited effect at low signal-to-noise ratios. Mass and spin parameters are most sensitive to noise. This study not only provides an efficient and accurate inference framework for ringdown analysis but also lays a foundation for developing robust data-processing pipelines for future GW astronomy in realistic noise environments.

### [21] [Topological field theory plus local Lorentz symmetry is gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12100)
*Maïté Dupuis,Florian Girelli,Oleksandra Hrytseniak,Wolfgang Wieland*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于Weyl旋子值1-形式（Weyl spinor-valued 1-forms）的四维引力新表述，从具有全局SL(2,ℂ)对称性的拓扑场论出发，通过局域化该对称性使引力自然涌现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 四维引力存在多种等价表述（度规、爱因斯坦-嘉当、远平行、McDowell-Mansouri等），每种在量子化方面各有优势。作者旨在提出一种基于Weyl旋子值1-形式的新表述，以编码标架场（frame-field）数据。

Method: 从具有全局SL(2,ℂ)对称性的拓扑场论出发，通过将该对称性提升为局域规范对称性（local gauge symmetry）使引力涌现。分析理论的协变相空间（covariant phase space）、对称性和荷结构，并探讨容许角项（admissible corner terms）的作用及其对边界荷和代数的影响。

Result: 该框架可扩展至包含宇宙学常数（cosmological constant），并可从模型中获取新颖的G→0标度极限。标架场在拓扑层面已存在，使得点粒子可在拓扑理论和引力理论中均匀耦合。通过详细的哈密顿分析阐明了现实条件（reality conditions）的实现。

Conclusion: 该基于Weyl旋子值1-形式的引力表述具有特殊的结构特征，使其特别适用于离散化（discretization）和量子化（quantization）。

Abstract: Four-dimensional gravity admits many equivalent formulations - metric, Einstein-Cartan, teleparallel, McDowell-Mansouri, among others - each offering distinct advantages, particularly, in view of quantization. We propose a new formulation based on Weyl spinor-valued 1-forms, ultimately encoding the frame-field data. Starting from a topological field theory with a global $\mathrm{SL}(2,\mathbb{C})$ symmetry, we show that promoting this symmetry to a local gauge symmetry leads to the emergence of gravity. We analyze the covariant phase space of this theory, its symmetries and charge structure and explore the role of admissible corner terms together with their impact on boundary charges and their algebra. We study several extensions of this framework, including the incorporation of a cosmological constant and a novel $ G \rightarrow 0 $ scaling limit obtained from this model. The presence of the frame field already at the topological level allows point particles to be coupled uniformly in both the topological and gravitational theories. We perform a detailed Hamiltonian analysis of the theory and clarify the implementation of the reality conditions. We argue that this formulation provides structural features that make it particularly well suited for both discretization and quantization.

### [22] [Shifted-geodesic approximation for spinning-body gravitational wave fluxes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12189)
*Lisa V. Drummond,Scott A. Hughes,Viktor Skoupý,Philip Lynch,Gabriel Andres Piovano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于偏移测地线（shifted-geodesic）的框架，用于计算克尔黑洞（Kerr black holes）束缚轨道上旋转测试体的引力波通量。该方法通过微扰轨道频率和运动积分来包含自旋效应，同时保持测地线运动的整体结构，为计算引力辐射提供了一种简单高效的近似方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要一种简单高效的方法来计算克尔黑洞束缚轨道上旋转测试体的引力波通量。由于后绝热修正（post-adiabatic corrections）相对于主导的绝热项是次要的，这种近似方法具有充分的理论依据。振荡性自旋项对通量的贡献通常很小，但对轨道描述的计算成本很高，因此成为自然的目标近似对象。

Method: 采用偏移测地线框架，通过微扰轨道频率和运动积分来包含自旋效应，同时保持测地线运动的整体结构。该方法主要适用于低偏心率、低倾角和较大半正焦弦的轨道，在接近稳定与不稳定轨道之间的分界线时可靠性降低。

Result: 诊断性旋进演化显示，使用偏移测地线近似导致的相位差非常小（约10^{-2}弧度/年），确认了自旋诱导的通量修正可以通过这种简单的测地线轨迹修改来准确包含。该近似为计算旋转体轨道提供了快速便捷的方法，但并非旨在替代更精确的处理。

Conclusion: 偏移测地线近似提供了一种实用替代方案，在优先考虑速度和简单性时特别有用，能够支持LISA任务的参数空间研究和高效的极端质量比旋进/中等质量比旋进（EMRI/IMRI）通量计算。

Abstract: We present a shifted-geodesic framework for computing gravitational-wave fluxes from spinning test bodies moving on bound orbits of Kerr black holes. The method provides a simple and efficient means of evaluating energy and angular momentum fluxes incorporating the leading effect of the smaller body's spin. Because post-adiabatic corrections, including secondary spin contributions, are subdominant to the leading adiabatic terms, this approximation is well justified. In particular, we find that oscillatory spin terms typically contribute very little to fluxes, but their contribution to the description of orbits is computationally expensive, making such terms a natural target for approximation. In our framework, orbital frequencies and integrals of the motion are perturbed to include spin effects, while the trajectory retains the global structure of geodesic motion. This simplifies the computation of gravitational radiation. The shifted-geodesic approximation is most reliable for orbits with lower eccentricity, lower inclination, and larger semi-latus recta. The approximation becomes less reliable as we approach the separatrix between stable and unstable orbits; fortunately, many inspirals spend less time in this region of parameter space. A diagnostic inspiral evolution shows very small dephasing due to use of the shifted-geodesic approximation ($\approx10^{-2}$ radians over 1 year), confirming that spin-induced flux corrections can be accurately included using this simple modification to a geodesic trajectory. This approximation provides a rapid and convenient way to compute spinning-body orbits, but is not intended to replace more accurate treatments. We propose it as a pragmatic alternative when speed and simplicity are prioritized, enabling efficient EMRI/IMRI flux calculations and supporting parameter-space studies for LISA. (Abridged)

</details>

### [23] [Finite-energy solutions to Einstein-scalar field Lichnerowicz equations on complete Riemannian manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09889)
*Bartosz Bieganowski,Pietro d'Avenia,Jacopo Schino*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文研究具有奇异非线性项的椭圆型方程，在系数低正则性条件下，通过建立存在性定理和不存在性结果，完整刻画了非负超解和正解的存在条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有奇异非线性项的椭圆型方程，其中系数允许低正则性。这类问题在非紧流形上具有挑战性，需要处理奇异项并建立适定性理论。

Method: 采用ε-正则化（ε-regularized）问题族，结合山路（mountain pass）论证和极限过程。在处理非紧流形上的奇异项时，Harnack不等式发挥关键作用。

Result: 在谱假设、几何假设和全局可积性条件下，证明了非负有限能量超解（finite-energy supersolution）的存在性。若Ricci曲率非负且B≥0，则获得正有限能量解。同时证明了不存在性结果，表明A的全局可积性条件对非负超解存在是必要的。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了奇异椭圆问题解的存在性理论，完整刻画了系数条件与解存在性的关系。全局可积性条件在精确意义下是必要的，为处理低正则性系数和非紧流形上的奇异问题提供了系统方法。

Abstract: We consider the singular elliptic problem of the form \[ -Δu + V(x)u = \mathcal{B}(x)|u|^{2^*-2}u + \frac{\mathcal{A}(x)}{|u|^{2^*}u}, \qquad u\in H^1(M), \] where the coefficients are allowed to have low regularity. Under natural spectral assumptions on $-Δ+V$, geometric assumptions on the manifold $M$ ensuring the Sobolev embedding $H^1(M)\hookrightarrow L^{2^*}(M)$, and a suitable global integrability/smallness condition involving $\mathcal{A}$, $\mathcal{B}$, and a function $ψ\in H^1(M)$, we prove the existence of a nonnegative finite-energy supersolution. If, in addition, the Ricci curvature is nonnegative and $\mathcal{B}\ge 0$, we obtain a positive finite-energy solution. The proof relies on a family of $\varepsilon$-regularized problems, mountain pass arguments, and a limiting procedure in which Harnack's inequality plays a crucial role in handling the singular term on noncompact manifolds. We also prove a nonexistence result showing that the global integrability condition on $\mathcal{A}$ is, in a precise sense, necessary for the existence of nonnegative supersolutions.

</details>


### [24] [Scattering for Defocusing NLS with Inhomogeneous Nonlinear Damping and Nonlinear Trapping Potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11765)
*David Lafontaine,Boris Shakarov*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文研究了三维空间中具有非线性阻尼和势能的能量次临界散焦非线性薛定谔方程，证明了当阻尼作用在势能诱导浓度效应的区域时，解具有全局存在性、H^1一致有界性，并在临界间区域发生散射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究三维空间中能量次临界（energy-subcritical）散焦非线性薛定谔方程在非线性阻尼和势能作用下的动力学行为，特别关注阻尼空间依赖性对解长期行为的影响。

Method: 通过引入基于位力论证（virial argument）修正的新型能量泛函，同时证明能量的一致有界性和局部能量衰减估计，随后利用相互作用Morawetz估计（interaction Morawetz estimates）升级为散射结果。

Result: 当阻尼作用在势能诱导浓度效应的区域（即势能为负值或非排斥性时），解具有全局存在性和H^1一致有界性，并在临界间（intercritical）区域发生散射。

Conclusion: 即使势能为零，阻尼的空间依赖性也会破坏能量的单调性，因此解在H^1范数下的一致时间控制是非平凡的，代表了该问题的新结果。

Abstract: We investigate an energy-subcritical defocusing nonlinear Schrödinger equation in $\mathbb R^3$ subject to a lower order nonlinear trapping potential and a spatially dependent nonlinear damping: \begin{equation*}
  i\partial_t u + Δu + i a(x) |u|^{2σ_2} u = |u|^{2σ_1} u + V(x)|u|^{2σ_3} u. \end{equation*} We prove that if the damping acts where $V$ induces concentration effects, i.e. where $V$ is either negative or non-repulsive, solutions are global and uniformly bounded in $H^1$, and scatter in the intercritical regime. A primary challenge arises from the spatial dependence of $a(x)$, which breaks the energy's monotonicity. Consequently, a uniform in time control of the $H^1$ norm of a solution is non-trivial and represents a new result even for $V = 0$. We overcome this issue by introducing a novel energy modified by virial argument, showing simultaneously a uniform bound on the energy and local energy decay estimates, which are subsequently upgraded to scattering via interaction Morawetz estimates.

</details>

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [25] [Algorithmic Capture, Computational Complexity, and Inductive Bias of Infinite Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11161)
*Orit Davidovich,Zohar Ringel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究正式定义了"算法捕获"概念，即神经网络泛化到任意问题规模的能力，并证明无限宽度transformer具有对低复杂度算法的归纳偏置，限制其学习高复杂度算法的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于区分真正的算法学习与统计插值，通过定义算法捕获（algorithmic capture）概念来形式化神经网络对算法的掌握能力，即能够泛化到任意问题规模且具有可控误差和最小样本适应。

Method: 方法包括分析无限宽度transformer在惰性（lazy）和丰富（rich）两种机制下的表现，推导这些网络可学习函数的推理时间计算复杂度上界，并研究其在高效多项式时间启发式方案（EPTHS）类中的归纳偏置。

Result: 结果显示，尽管transformer具有通用表达能力，但其对低复杂度算法存在归纳偏置，这有效阻止了它们捕获更高复杂度的算法，同时允许在搜索、复制和排序等简单任务上取得成功。

Conclusion: 结论表明transformer的归纳偏置使其倾向于学习高效多项式时间启发式方案（EPTHS）类中的低复杂度算法，从而限制了其捕获高复杂度算法的能力，这为理解神经网络算法学习能力提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We formally define Algorithmic Capture (i.e., ``grokking'' an algorithm) as the ability of a neural network to generalize to arbitrary problem sizes ($T$) with controllable error and minimal sample adaptation, distinguishing true algorithmic learning from statistical interpolation. By analyzing infinite-width transformers in both the lazy and rich regimes, we derive upper bounds on the inference-time computational complexity of the functions these networks can learn. We show that despite their universal expressivity, transformers possess an inductive bias towards low-complexity algorithms within the Efficient Polynomial Time Heuristic Scheme (EPTHS) class. This bias effectively prevents them from capturing higher-complexity algorithms, while allowing success on simpler tasks like search, copy, and sort.

</details>

### [26] [Pattern formation in driven condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11870)
*Ivana Vasić,Dušan Vudragović,Mihaela Carina Raportaru,Alexandru Nicolin-Żaczek*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该综述回顾了玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BECs）中由外部驱动引发的图案形成研究进展，重点介绍了法拉第不稳定性（Faraday instability）在量子超流体系统中的实现，以及最近观察到的稳定二维方格晶格图案，该图案表现出超固态（supersolid）的某些特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究空间均匀系统在外界驱动下图案形成（pattern formation）的起始机制是多个科学领域的重要课题。玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BECs）因其卓越的实验可控性，为研究图案形成机制提供了理想的量子力学平台。

Method: 该综述回顾了过去二十年的研究进展，从首个预测驱动凝聚体中参数不稳定性（parametric instabilities）和法拉第波（Faraday waves）的理论提案开始，讨论了关键实验和理论突破，最终聚焦于二维受限、周期性驱动BEC中稳定方格晶格图案的观察。

Result: 研究证实了驱动凝聚体中参数共振和图案形成的预测，并实现了稳定的二维方格晶格图案。这种具有叠加密度调制的驱动超流体状态表现出超固态（supersolid）的某些特征。

Conclusion: 周期性驱动的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体为探索非平衡相和图案形成提供了独特平台，近期观察到的稳定图案状态标志着该领域研究的重要进展，揭示了驱动超流体与超固态性质之间的潜在联系。

Abstract: The onset of pattern formation in a spatially homogeneous system subjected to external driving is an important topic in various scientific fields. A celebrated classical example is the Faraday instability, where a vertically oscillated fluid surface undergoes a parametric resonance, giving rise to standing waves that self-organize into regular spatial patterns. Bose-Einstein condensates (BECs) provide an ideal quantum-mechanical platform for studying pattern-forming mechanisms due to their exceptional degree of experimental control. As a compressible state of quantum matter, a condensate responds sensitively to external perturbations, including time-periodic modulation of interactions, trapping potentials, or external fields. These features make BECs particularly well suited for exploring driven nonequilibrium phases and pattern formation. In this chapter, we review the remarkable progress achieved in this field over the past two decades. We begin with the first theoretical proposal predicting parametric instabilities and emergent Faraday waves in driven condensates. We then discuss key experimental and theoretical breakthroughs that confirmed these predictions and refined the understanding of the underlying mechanisms. This line of research has culminated in the recent observation of a stabilized square lattice pattern in a periodically driven BEC confined in a two-dimensional geometry. This driven superfluid state with superposed density modulation was shown to exhibit some features of a supersolid state.

</details>

### [27] [Metasurface Tape for Efficient Millimeter-Wave Power Transfer via Surface-Wave Propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11579)
*Phuc Toan Dang,Kota Suzuki,Yoshiki Ashikaga,Yasushi Tsuchiya,Sendy Phang,Hiroki Wakatsuchi*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种柔性超表面胶带（flexible metasurface tape），用于克服毫米波通信中的自由空间路径损耗问题。通过将电磁能量引导为表面波（surface waves），该设计将功率衰减从球面依赖（r^{-2}）改变为圆形依赖（r^{-1}），在约100 GHz频率下实现了显著的功率传输增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 毫米波技术对于未来高速无线通信至关重要，但其面临严重的自由空间路径损耗（free-space path loss）挑战，即功率密度随距离平方反比衰减（r^{-2}）。这种球面依赖的衰减限制了毫米波系统的有效范围，需要新的解决方案来克服这一瓶颈。

Method: 研究者提出了一种柔性超表面胶带，通过在柔性基底上制造周期性接地贴片阵列（periodic grounded-patch array），将电磁能量引导为表面波。该方法将电磁场限制在亚波长界面，改变了功率衰减规律，首次在约100 GHz频率下进行了数值和实验验证。

Result: 实验结果显示，在95 GHz至105 GHz的宽带宽（约10%）范围内，超表面胶带显著提高了传输功率。相对于自由空间基线，接收功率平均每米改善约40倍（例如在2米距离处增加29 dB）。柔性轻质的特性使其易于安装在不同表面上。

Conclusion: 该超表面胶带为扩展毫米波系统的有效范围提供了有前景的平台，为解决下一代无线网络中的路径损耗瓶颈提供了稳健解决方案。其宽带特性能够适应高速数据率应用所需的宽带调制方案。

Abstract: Millimeter-wave technologies are essential for future high-speed wireless communications. However, a fundamental challenge remains in the form of severe free-space path loss, where the power density decreases inversely with the square of the distance r (i.e., proportional to r^{-2}) as a spherical dependence. To overcome this limitation, we propose a flexible metasurface tape that is designed to guide electromagnetic energy as surface waves. Unlike conventional free-space propagation, this engineered metasurface confines the field to a subwavelength interface, thereby altering the power decay law to a circular dependence (i.e., proportional to r^{-1}). We numerically and experimentally, for the first time, demonstrate this concept using a periodic grounded-patch array fabricated on a flexible substrate and operated at approximately 100 GHz. The measurement results show that the metasurface tape significantly increases the transmitted power, yielding an average rate of improvement of approximately 40 per meter in received power relative to the free-space baseline in our measurement geometry (e.g., 29-dB increase at 2 m). This increase is realized over a broad bandwidth from 95 GHz to 105 GHz (i.e., approximately 10 %), accommodating wideband modulation schemes required for high-data-rate applications. The flexible, lightweight nature of the tape allows it to be easily installed on diverse surfaces. Our demonstration indicates that the metasurface tape is a promising platform for extending the effective range of millimeter-wave systems, thus offering a robust solution to the path-loss bottleneck in next-generation wireless networks.

</details>

Method: 研究方法基于中心特征标（central character）在换位（transposition）上的取值分析。通过这一代数组合方法，作者建立了Hurwitz数的结构特征与渐近行为之间的联系。

Result: 研究发现了特定Hurwitz数的结构特征，并推导出了其在大亏格（large genus）情况下的渐近公式。这些结果揭示了Hurwitz数在极限情况下的数学行为模式。

Conclusion: 该工作通过中心特征标方法成功揭示了Hurwitz数的结构与大亏格渐近性质，为代数组合与渐近分析领域提供了新的理论工具与洞察。

Abstract: In this paper, based on the value of central character on the transposition, we find structure and large genus asymptotics of certain Hurwitz numbers.

### [29] [Upper bound of some character ratios and large genus asymptotic behavior of Hurwitz numbers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11614)
*Xiang Li*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了任意紧致黎曼曲面（compact Riemann surface）上具有固定数量一般轮廓（general profiles）和某些(r,1^{d-r})轮廓的Hurwitz数的大亏格渐近行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文的动机源于文献[3]，旨在将先前关于黎曼球面（Riemann sphere）上Hurwitz数大亏格渐近的结果推广到任意紧致黎曼曲面。先前工作[14]已研究了黎曼球面上具有固定数量一般轮廓和某些(2,1^{d-2})轮廓的Hurwitz数渐近行为。

Method: 作者将文献[14]中针对黎曼球面的方法推广到任意紧致黎曼曲面，研究具有固定数量一般轮廓和某些(r,1^{d-r})轮廓的Hurwitz数的大亏格渐近行为。

Result: 本文成功获得了任意紧致黎曼曲面上Hurwitz数的大亏格渐近公式，这些Hurwitz数具有固定数量的一般轮廓和某些(r,1^{d-r})轮廓，推广了先前黎曼球面上的结果。

Conclusion: 该研究将Hurwitz数的大亏格渐近分析从黎曼球面推广到任意紧致黎曼曲面，扩展了相关渐近理论的应用范围，为更一般的代数几何和拓扑问题提供了渐近工具。

Abstract: In [14] we found the large genus asymptotics of Hurwitz numbers for the Riemann sphere with a fixed number of general profiles and some (2,1^{d-2}) profiles. In this paper, motivated from [3], we generalize these results to Hurwitz numbers of an arbitrary compact Riemann surface with a fixed number of general profiles and some (r,1^{d-r}) profiles.

### [30] [Lectures on Open Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11925)
*Marco Merkli,Ángel Neira*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提供开放量子系统（open quantum systems）数学理论的简明导论，通过耗散Jaynes-Cummings模型展示不可逆动力学如何从幺正系统-环境演化中产生，并介绍主方程（master equation）、完全正定保迹（CPTP）映射、量子动力学半群等核心概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为开放量子系统数学理论提供一个入门指南，该研究领域在量子科学中具有广泛应用，特别是处理受外部噪声影响的系统。作者希望通过具体模型让理论的关键结构自然呈现。

Method: 采用耗散Jaynes-Cummings模型作为具体案例，通过连续模极限（continuous mode limit）、关联函数（correlation functions）和谱密度（spectral density）等概念的引入，自然推导出开放系统的主方程（master equation）形式演化方程。

Result: 通过模型分析展示了不可逆动力学如何从幺正系统-环境演化中产生，为更一般的完全正定保迹（CPTP）映射和量子动力学半群（quantum dynamical semigroups）研究奠定了基础。文中证明Kraus表示定理、膨胀定理和GKSL定理（Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad theorem）。

Conclusion: 该导论性笔记为读者提供了开放量子系统数学理论的结构化入门，通过具体模型和配套练习（附完整解答）帮助读者掌握核心概念，为进一步研究该广泛领域奠定基础。

Abstract: These notes are a short introduction to the mathematical theory of open quantum systems. They are meant to serve as an entry point into a broad research area which has applications across the quantum sciences dealing with systems subjected to external noise. The guiding idea is to let the key structures of the theory emerge from a concrete model. By working through the dissipative Jaynes-Cummings model the reader will dis- cover explicitly how irreversible dynamics arises from a unitary system-reservoir evolution. The notions of the continuous mode limit, correlation functions, spectral density appear in a natural manner and lead to the evolution equation of the open system in form of a master equation. This sets the stage for the more general analysis of completely positive, trace preserving (CPTP) maps and the study of quantum dynamical semigroups. We motivate and prove the Kraus representation theorem, the dilation theorem and the Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad (GKSL) theorem. Working through the exercises (for which full solutions are supplied) will reinforce the ideas introduced in the main text.

</details>


### [31] [Operationalism, Causality, and Quantum Theory: a mostly time symmetric perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12076)
*Lucien Hardy*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本书系统阐述了操作概率理论（operational probabilistic theories），主要采用时间对称视角，包含简单操作和复杂操作两部分内容，建立了操作概率理论、操作量子理论及希尔伯特对象理论的统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 操作概率理论的标准方法通常采用时间向前视角，本书旨在从时间对称视角全面阐述该理论体系，解决传统方法的局限性，为复杂因果结构提供更一般的理论框架。

Method: 本书采用双重结构：第一部分处理简单操作（所有输入在输出之前），第二部分处理复杂操作（配备因果图）。建立了三个理论层次：操作概率理论（基于操作）、操作量子理论（基于算子张量）和希尔伯特对象理论（可加倍生成算子张量）。

Result: 证明了简单情况下时间对称视角与时间向前视角的等价性；展示了物理性操作构建的电路具有0到1的概率且满足因果条件；用复杂操作建模Sorkin不可能测量，证明物理性防止异常信号传递；发展了希尔伯特对象的图表示法及镜像定理。

Conclusion: 本书建立了从时间对称视角全面阐述操作概率理论的完整框架，证明了该视角在简单情况下的等价性，并为复杂因果结构提供了理论工具，特别是通过希尔伯特对象图表示法和时间对称因果膨胀定理的证明。

Abstract: This is a book about operational probabilistic theories. The standard approach in such theories is from a time forward perspective. In this book we mostly take a time symmetric perspective. This presents a branding problem. Is this a niche book merely about time symmetry? No. This is a comprehensive book about operational probabilistic theories, but mostly from a time symmetric perspective. In fact, this book consists of (1) a simple book about simple operations having simple causal structure (where all the inputs are before all the outputs), and (2) a complex book about complex operations that can have complicated causal structure (a complex operation is equipped with a causal diagram). For the simple case we are able to show that the time symmetric perspective is equivalent to the time forward perspective. In each book we set up (A) operational probabilistic theories (OPTs) in terms of operations, (B) Operational Quantum Theory (OQT) in terms of operator tensors which correspond to operations, and (C) the theory of Hilbert objects which can be doubled up to give operator tensors. Operations are required to be physical which guarantees that circuits built out of operations have probabilities between 0 and 1 and that certain causality conditions are met. We prove that when we wire together operations the resulting networks are also physical. We model Sorkin's impossible measurements with complex operations and show that physicality prevents anomalous signalling. We develop diagrammatic notation for Hilbert objects. This includes mirrors for doubling up and mirror theorems. We use this framework to prove time symmetric causal dilation theorems for various causal diagrams.

</details>


### [32] [Unitary imaginary time evolution and ground state preparation using multi-copy protocols](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11208)
*Tal Schwartzman,Torsten V. Zache,Hannes Pichler,H. R. Sadeghpour*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出确定性酉协议（deterministic unitary protocols）用于近似虚时演化（imaginary-time evolution），以实现高效低能态制备。协议采用多系统副本、系统哈密顿量的实时演化以及受控SWAP操作，设计了树形架构和紧凑"hedge"架构两种电路家族，并通过数值模拟验证了中电路后选择（mid-circuit post-selection）的加速效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高效低能态制备（low-energy state preparation）是量子计算和量子模拟的关键目标。量子虚时演化（quantum imaginary-time evolution）通过用虚时动力学替代实时动力学，能够指数抑制高能本征态，但需要有效的实现方法。

Method: 提出确定性酉协议（deterministic unitary protocols）来近似虚时演化，协议需要：1) 系统的多个副本（multiple copies）；2) 在系统哈密顿量下的实时演化（real-time evolution）；3) 受控SWAP操作（controlled-SWAP operations）或更一般的SWAP生成酉操作（SWAP-generated unitaries）。设计了两种具体电路家族：具有可证明多项式深度收敛性的树形架构（tree architecture），以及仅需多项式宽度的紧凑"hedge"架构。

Result: 数值证据表明中电路后选择（mid-circuit post-selection）能够以实际可行的成功概率加速收敛。同时证明在基态制备（ground-state preparation）场景中，电路体积（circuit volume）可以与后电路可观测量估计（post-circuit observable estimation）的测量复杂度（shot complexity）进行权衡。提出了平台特异性实现路径的具体方案。

Conclusion: 这些混合模拟-数字电路（hybrid analog-digital circuits）能够补充现有的态制备方法，特别适用于多副本寄存器和SWAP介导耦合（SWAP-mediated couplings）自然存在的平台，为近期量子计算提供了实用的态制备方案。

Abstract: Efficient low-energy state preparation is a key objective in quantum computation and quantum simulation. Quantum imaginary-time evolution replaces real-time dynamics with imaginary-time dynamics, exponentially suppressing higher-energy eigenstates. We introduce deterministic unitary protocols that approximate imaginary-time evolution for ground-state preparation. The protocols require multiple copies of the system, real-time evolution under the system Hamiltonian, and controlled-SWAP operations (or more general SWAP-generated unitaries). We analyze two concrete circuit families: a tree architecture with provable polynomial-in-depth convergence but rapidly growing width, and a compact "hedge" architecture that achieves comparable accuracy with only polynomial width in a heuristic construction supported by numerics. We provide numerical evidence that mid-circuit post-selection can accelerate convergence with practical success probabilities. Separately, we demonstrate that circuit volume can be traded for the shot complexity of post-circuit observable estimation in the ground-state preparation setting. We outline concrete implementation of platform-specific routes, where multi-copy registers and SWAP-mediated couplings are natural, thereby illustrating how these hybrid analog-digital circuits can complement existing state-preparation methods in the near term.

</details>


### [33] [DysonNet: Constant-Time Local Updates for Neural Quantum States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11189)
*Lucas Winter,Andreas Nunnenkamp*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: DysonNet是一种新型神经量子态（NQS）架构，通过类戴森级数（Dyson series）结构实现局部非线性与全局线性的耦合，显著提升了计算效率和可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统神经量子态（neural quantum states, NQS）存在计算成本高和可解释性有限的问题。本文旨在开发一种既能保持高精度又能显著提升计算效率的新型NQS架构。

Method: 引入DysonNet，这是一类将严格局部非线性通过全局线性层耦合的NQS架构。其结构类似于截断的戴森级数（truncated Dyson series），将局部波函数更新解释为静态杂质散射。采用ABACUS算法实现单自旋翻转更新的O(1)时间复杂度，并使用状态空间模型S4进行实现。

Result: DysonNet在计算局部估计量时比Vision-Transformers快达230倍，实现了训练时间复杂度的渐进O(N²)改进，在面积律相中达到O(N log² N)的总训练复杂度。在一维长程伊辛模型和受挫J₁-J₂链上的基准测试表明，DysonNet在匹配最先进NQS精度的同时消除了主要的局部更新开销。

Conclusion: DysonNet通过物理可解释的散射级数重整化（resumming the scattering series）实现了计算效率的显著提升，为可扩展的NQS架构提供了一条新路径，其中物理可解释性直接促成了计算效率的提升。

Abstract: Neural quantum states (NQS) provide a flexible variational framework for many-body wavefunctions, but suffer from high computational cost and limited interpretability. We introduce DysonNet, a broad class of NQS that couples strictly local nonlinearities through global linear layers. This structure is analogous to a truncated Dyson series which gives an intuitive interpretation of local wavefunction updates as scattering from static impurities. By resumming the scattering series, single-spin-flip updates can be computed in $\mathcal{O}(1)$ time, independent of system size, using an algorithm we call ABACUS. Implementing DysonNet with the state-space model S4, we obtain up to $230\times$ speedups over Vision-Transformers for computing the local estimator. This corresponds to an asymptotic $\mathcal{O}(N^2)$ improvement in training-time scaling, reaching $\mathcal{O}(N \log^2 N)$ total training complexity in area-law phases. Benchmarks on the 1D long-range Ising model and frustrated $J_1$-$J_2$ chains show that DysonNet matches state-of-the-art NQS accuracy while removing the dominant local-update overhead. More broadly, our results suggest a route to scalable NQS architectures where physical interpretability directly enables computational efficiency.

Abstract: Quantum many-body scars are nonthermal states exhibiting persistent revivals in an otherwise ergodic, nonintegrable quantum system. Existing examples of exact quantum scars, however, have not yet been amenable to direct experimental demonstration. Here we show that a minimal model of hardcore bosons hopping on a $π$-flux ladder is sufficient to give rise to an exact scar due to kinetic frustration. The simplicity of this model makes it suitable for multiple existing quantum simulation platforms, which we illustrate with proposals for cold atom Bose-Hubbard simulators and polar molecule or Rydberg atom tweezer arrays. In these platforms, the scar lifetime can be extended by tuning experimentally accessible parameters, like the Hubbard interaction or a Floquet drive. Finally, we introduce a practical heuristic based on the energy distribution of eigenstates for systematically predicting and optimizing quantum many-body scar lifetimes. Amorphous Al$_2$O$_3$ is widely used as a barrier material, but under irradiation, oxygen vacancy (V$_O$) defects are readily generated, introducing noise sources that accelerate qubit decoherence. We systematically investigate the structural characteristics and electronic impact of V$_O$ defects in amorphous Al$_2$O$_3$ using first-principles calculations and \textit{ab initio} molecular dynamics. Using a noise model, we estimate that higher V$_O$ densities lead to shorter qubit coherence times. These findings provide insights for radiation-hard design of superconducting quantum devices.

By implementing stroboscopic evolution of a two-dimensional Heisenberg model on IBM heavy-hex devices, we observe that initially phase-randomized spins spontaneously self-organize into coherent lattice-wide oscillations. This coexistence of globally desynchronized and locally synchronized regions constitutes a quantum analogue of a classical chimera state. Statevector and matrix-product-state simulations reproduce both the symmetry-protected synchronization and the chimera coexistence, demonstrating that these phenomena arise from the intrinsic Floquet many-body dynamics. Our results establish symmetry-protected synchronization and quantum chimera states as experimentally accessible nonequilibrium dynamical phases in programable many-body quantum systems.

Our findings are directly relevant to both optical and superconducting microwave channels, where analog feedforward techniques have been recently implemented.

Abstract: We present a measurement-driven quantum framework for evaluating overlap and Hamiltonian matrix elements in spin-coupled generalized valence bond (SCGVB) wavefunctions. The approach targets a central difficulty of nonorthogonal valence-bond methods: estimating matrix elements between distinct, generally nonorthogonal configuration state functions. Rather than preparing the full wavefunction on quantum hardware, we reformulate the required quantities as vacuum expectation values of Pauli-string operators that can be accessed using shallow, ancilla-free circuits composed of local Clifford rotations and computational-basis measurements. In contrast to Hadamard-test-based matrix-element estimation, this construction avoids ancilla qubits and controlled operations by reducing the problem to local Pauli measurements. This separates the algebraic construction of the SCGVB problem from the measurement task executed on the quantum register and yields a low-depth strategy compatible with near-term architectures. ### [39] [The Constrained Origin of Canonical and Microcanonical Ensembles in Quantum Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12148)
*Loris Di Cairano*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文展示量子理论中正则系综（canonical ensemble）与微正则系综（microcanonical ensemble）并非独立构造，而是源自同一约束量子动力学系统的互补投影。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子理论中，平衡统计力学通常通过正则系综表述，其特殊地位与时间演化的欧几里得延拓相关。微正则系综则常作为独立的光谱构造引入，这种不对称性需要澄清。

Method: 在扩展希尔伯特空间中构建系统，将时间提升为辅助时钟自由度，通过重参数化不变约束算子 $\hat C = \hat P_T + \hat H$ 选择物理态。对应投影子 $δ(\hat C)$ 提供了统一对象。

Result: 在时钟时间表象中，纯虚时钟分离产生欧几里得核与正则配分函数。在共轭时钟能量表象中，同一投影子约化为光谱算子 $δ(\hat H-E)$，从而得到微正则态密度。

Conclusion: 正则与微正则统计无需作为独立构造引入，二者已编码于同一约束量子动力学中。这种不对称性是表象性的而非结构性的。

Abstract: In quantum theory, equilibrium statistical mechanics is usually formulated through the canonical ensemble, whose privileged status is tied to the Euclidean continuation of time evolution. The microcanonical ensemble, by contrast, is commonly introduced as a separate spectral construction. In this work we show that this asymmetry is representational rather than structural. We formulate the system in an extended Hilbert space in which time is promoted to an auxiliary clock degree of freedom and physical states are selected by a reparametrization-invariant constraint operator $\hat C = \hat P_T + \hat H$. The corresponding projector $δ(\hat C)$ provides a single unified object from which both canonical and microcanonical ensembles emerge as complementary projections in the clock sector. In the clock-time representation, a purely imaginary clock separation yields the Euclidean kernel and the canonical partition function. In the conjugate clock-energy representation, the same projector reduces to the spectral operator $δ(\hat H-E)$ and hence to the microcanonical density of states. The main consequence is structural: canonical and microcanonical statistics need not be introduced as independent constructions, since both are already encoded in the same constrained quantum dynamics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过实验发现集成光子处理器上存在"硬件地平线"相变现象，并推导现象学误差模型（phenomenological error model），将静态相干谱失真（static coherent spectral distortion）和动态退相干（dynamic decoherence）的竞争机制解耦。

Result: 重构误差最初遵循预测的统计标度律$\mathcal{O}(M^{-1/2})$，但在由实现的酉群谱失真决定的平台处突然饱和。这一固有噪声平台（intrinsic noise floor）构成了统计积累无法克服的硬性界限。

Conclusion: 在NISQ（noisy intermediate-scale quantum）硬件上影子层析的效用由涉及硬件参数的特定标度律定义，需要主动补偿策略来弥合理论纯度与集成光子学噪声现实之间的差距。

Abstract: The theoretical efficiency of classical shadow tomography is predicated on a perfect Haar-random unitary ensemble, yet this mathematical ideal remains physically unattainable in near-term hardware. Here, we report the experimental discovery of a fundamental accuracy bound on integrated photonic processors: a ``Hardware Horizon'' where the reconstruction error undergoes a sharp phase transition. While the error initially obeys the predicted statistical scaling $\mathcal{O}(M^{-1/2})$, it abruptly saturates at a floor determined by the spectral distortions of the realized unitary group. By deriving a phenomenological error model, we decouple the competing mechanisms of static coherent spectral distortion and dynamic decoherence, demonstrating that this intrinsic noise floor imposes a hard bound that statistical accumulation cannot overcome. These findings establish that the utility of shadow tomography on NISQ (noisy intermediate-scale quantum) hardware is defined by a specific scaling law involving hardware parameters, necessitating active compensation strategies to bridge the gap between theoretical purity and the noisy reality of integrated photonics.

Motivation: 理解孤立量子多体系统如何热化是现代物理学的核心问题。研究旨在探索二维无序海森堡Floquet模型中遍历性（ergodicity）的涌现机制，特别是跨不同长度尺度的行为特征。

Method: 采用IBM Nighthawk超导量子处理器进行数字量子模拟，系统规模可达10×10量子比特。通过将系统粗粒化（coarse-graining）为不同尺寸的空间斑块（spatial patches），并引入基于每个斑块碰撞熵（collision entropy）的测量方法，详细研究遍历行为在不同尺度上的涌现。

Result: 随着海森堡耦合J增加，无噪声系统经历从亚遍历（subergodic）到遍历行为的平滑交叉（smooth crossover），较小斑块首先接近其随机矩阵理论（random-matrix-theory）值，揭示了跨尺度的层次结构。在经典张量网络模拟可靠参数区域（小斑块或小J值），量子模拟与误差缓解结果高度一致；超出该区域，体积律纠缠和收缩复杂性增长导致经典方法成本急剧上升。

Conclusion: 研究结果为量子计算机在量子热化研究中的应用开辟了新方向，展示了量子模拟在探索经典方法难以处理的强纠缠区域中的独特优势。

Abstract: Understanding how isolated quantum many-body systems thermalize remains a central question in modern physics. We study the onset of ergodicity in a two-dimensional disordered Heisenberg Floquet model using digital quantum simulation on IBM's Nighthawk superconducting processor, reaching system sizes of up to $10\times10$ qubits. We probe ergodicity across different length scales by coarse-graining the system into spatial patches of varying sizes and introducing a measure based on the collision entropy of each patch, enabling a detailed study of when ergodic behavior emerges across scales. The high sampling rate of superconducting quantum processing units, together with an optimal sample estimator, allow us to access patches of sizes up to $3\times3$. We observe that as the Heisenberg coupling $J$ increases, the noiseless system undergoes a smooth crossover from subergodic to ergodic behavior, with smaller patches approaching their random-matrix-theory values first, thereby revealing a hierarchy across scales. In the region of parameter space where classical tensor-network simulations are reliable, small patches or small values of $J$, we find excellent agreement with the error-mitigated quantum simulation. Beyond this regime, volume-law entanglement and contraction complexity growth causes the cost of classical methods to rise sharply. Our results open new directions for the use of quantum computers in the study of quantum thermalization.

</details>

### [42] [Reduced Order Model for Broadband Superabsorption of Waves by Metascreens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11962)
*Habib Ammari,Yu Gao,Lara Vrabac*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于亚波长声学谐振器（subwavelength acoustic resonators）周期性排列的薄涂层设计，用于实现低频声波的宽带吸收（broadband absorption）。通过建立降阶模型（reduced order model）和基于梯度的形状优化方法（gradient based shape optimization），实现了高效的宽带吸收设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在解决低频声波的宽带吸收问题，通过设计一种由亚波长声学谐振器周期性排列在反射表面上的薄涂层，实现对低频声波的有效吸收。

Method: 首先研究相关的散射问题（scattering problem）和亚波长共振问题（subwavelength resonance problem），推导出谐振频率和反射系数的解析近似表达式。通过建立阻抗边界条件（impedance boundary condition）的有效宏观描述，并发展基于形状导数（shape derivatives）的梯度优化方法进行宽带吸收设计。

Result: 研究获得了谐振频率和反射系数的解析近似，建立了能够高效评估频带内散射波的降阶模型。数值实验（numerical experiments）验证了所提出设计方法的宽带性能和有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功开发了一种基于亚波长声学谐振器周期性排列的薄涂层设计方法，通过降阶模型和形状优化实现了低频声波的宽带吸收，为声学吸收材料设计提供了有效的理论框架和优化工具。

Abstract: This work presents a new design for broadband absorption of low-frequency acoustic waves using a thin coating made of subwavelength acoustic resonators arranged periodically on a reflective surface. We first study the associated scattering problem and the corresponding subwavelength resonance problem, and then derive analytical approximations for the resonant frequencies and the reflection coefficient in terms of the periodic capacitance matrix in a half-space with a Dirichlet boundary condition. These approximations yield an effective macroscopic description of the coating via an impedance boundary condition and clarify the mechanism of superabsorption through an approximate coupling condition. Moreover, they lead to a reduced order model that enables efficient evaluation of the scattered waves over a frequency band and accelerates broadband absorption design. Building on this reduced order model, we develop a gradient based shape optimization method using shape derivatives of the resonant quantities to achieve broadband absorption. Numerical experiments demonstrate the broadband performance and the effectiveness of the proposed design procedure.

### [43] [UV/IR relations from the worldsheet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11157)
*Christian Aoufia,Ivano Basile,Giorgio Leone,Matteo Lotito*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文推导了弦理论低能有效作用的普适标度关系，将真空能和规范耦合与高阶导数Wilson系数联系起来，这些关系源于世界面的模不变性和共形不变性，并强化了涌现弦猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在建立弦理论中低能有效作用的普适标度关系，这些关系连接真空能（vacuum energy）和规范耦合（gauge couplings）与高阶导数Wilson系数，旨在强化涌现弦猜想（emergent string conjecture）并将UV/IR混合与沼泽地原理（swampland principles）联系起来。

Method: 在弦微扰理论（string perturbation theory）的一圈水平上，利用世界面（worldsheet）的模不变性（modular invariance）和共形不变性（conformal invariance）推导普适参数关系，这些关系独立于具体的低能相（low-energy phase），并在物种极限（species limits）下变得非平凡。

Result: 推导出的标度关系在物种极限下变得非平凡，显著强化了涌现弦猜想，并将UV/IR混合与沼泽地原理联系起来。进一步考虑开弦（open-string）贡献后，这些关系导致参数不等式，重现了全息界限（holographic bounds）并支持磁弱引力猜想（magnetic weak-gravity conjecture）和暗维度情景（dark dimension scenario）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明这些关系可能持续到更高圈水平，暗示了利用对偶性（dualities）研究强耦合的途径，为弦理论中低能有效作用的普适性质提供了重要见解，并连接了多个重要的沼泽地原理。

Abstract: We derive universal scaling relations for the low-energy effective action of string theory, connecting the vacuum energy and gauge couplings to higher-derivative Wilson coefficients. At one-loop in string perturbation theory, these generic parametric relations follow from modular and conformal invariance of the worldsheet, independently of the specific low-energy phase of the theory, and they become non-trivial in species limits. As a result, we substantially strengthen our previous case for the emergent string conjecture and connect UV/IR mixing to swampland principles. We argue that our results persist to higher loops, hinting at a pathway to study strong couplings using dualities. Further accounting for open-string contributions, if any, our results lead to parametric inequalities which reproduce holographic bounds and support the magnetic weak-gravity conjecture and the dark dimension scenario.

### [44] [Alice in Warpland: KK modes, Warped Compactifications and the Swampland](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11163)
*Salvatore Raucci,Ignacio Ruiz,Irene Valenzuela*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了弯曲紧致化（warped compactification）中Kaluza-Klein（KK）塔的渐近行为，发现在强弯曲背景下KK质量衰减率可能违反锐化距离猜想（Sharpened Distance Conjecture）的界限，但该界限恰好与高维势能禁止渐近加速膨胀的条件一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探究弯曲紧致化（warped compactification）到Minkowski空间时Kaluza-Klein（KK）塔的渐近行为，特别关注整体解紧致化极限（overall decompactification limit）下KK质量标度与模空间距离（moduli space distance）的关系。

Method: 方法包括：在余维数一（codimension-one）的弯曲背景下，针对由高维指数势（higher-dimensional exponential potential）驱动的系统，显式求解内部轮廓（internal profiles），并获得KK塔指数质量衰减率$λ_{\rm KK}$关于模空间距离的闭合表达式。

Result: 研究发现弯曲会降低$λ_{\rm KK}$相对于非弯曲情况，使得足够强的弯曲原则上可能违反锐化距离猜想（Sharpened Distance Conjecture）的界限。值得注意的是，当高维势能满足禁止渐近加速膨胀的条件时，该锐化界限恰好被满足，建立了锐化距离猜想与高维强de Sitter条件（Strong de Sitter condition）的直接联系。

Conclusion: 结论表明弯曲紧致化中KK塔的渐近标度行为建立了弦理论中距离猜想（Distance Conjecture）与宇宙学加速膨胀条件之间的深刻联系。对于更高余维数（higher-codimension）的弯曲背景，渐近KK标度保持不变。

Abstract: We investigate the asymptotic behavior of Kaluza-Klein (KK) towers in warped compactifications to Minkowski space. Focusing on the overall decompactification limit, we derive the scaling of KK masses at large KK momentum for scalar fluctuations in lower-dimensional Planck units. In codimension-one warped backgrounds sourced by a higher-dimensional exponential potential, we solve explicitly for the internal profiles and obtain a closed expression for the exponential mass decay rate $λ_{\rm KK}$ of the tower in terms of the moduli space distance. We find that warping reduces $λ_{\rm KK}$ relative to the unwarped case, in such a way that sufficiently strong warping could in principle violate the Sharpened Distance Conjecture bound. Remarkably, this sharpened bound is still satisfied precisely when the higher-dimensional potential obeys the condition forbidding asymptotic accelerated expansion, establishing a direct link between the Sharpened Distance Conjecture and the Strong de Sitter condition in one higher dimension. We also argue that for higher-codimension warped backgrounds the asymptotic KK scaling remains unmodified.

</details>


### [45] [Learning to Unscramble: Simplifying Symbolic Expressions via Self-Supervised Oracle Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11164)
*David Shih*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的自监督机器学习方法，用于复杂数学表达式的符号简化。该方法通过扰乱简单表达式生成训练数据，训练基于Transformer的策略网络，在量子场论中的双对数约化和旋量螺旋度散射振幅简化问题上实现了接近完美的解决率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如强化学习和端到端回归在处理复杂数学表达式简化时存在局限性，需要开发更有效的符号简化技术，特别是在高能物理（high-energy physics）领域，如双对数约化（dilogarithm reduction）和散射振幅（scattering amplitude）简化。

Method: 通过扰乱简单表达式并记录逆操作生成训练数据，创建包含目标状态和明确路径的oracle轨迹。训练一个置换等变（permutation-equivariant）、基于Transformer的策略网络，以逐步预测给定输入表达式的oracle动作。结合对比分组（contrastive grouping）和束搜索（beam search）进行优化。

Result: 训练后的策略网络在广泛的难度范围内实现了接近完美的解决率，显著优于基于强化学习和端到端回归的先前方法。在杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theory）中，对包含200多个初始项的五点胶子树级振幅（5-point gluon tree-level amplitudes）实现了100%的完全简化率。

Conclusion: 该方法为复杂数学表达式的符号简化提供了一种有效的自监督学习框架，在高能物理的具体应用中表现出卓越性能，为相关领域的符号计算问题提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: We present a new self-supervised machine learning approach for symbolic simplification of complex mathematical expressions. Training data is generated by scrambling simple expressions and recording the inverse operations, creating oracle trajectories that provide both goal states and explicit paths to reach them. A permutation-equivariant, transformer-based policy network is then trained on this data step-wise to predict the oracle action given the input expression. We demonstrate this approach on two problems in high-energy physics: dilogarithm reduction and spinor-helicity scattering amplitude simplification. In both cases, our trained policy network achieves near perfect solve rates across a wide range of difficulty levels, substantially outperforming prior approaches based on reinforcement learning and end-to-end regression. When combined with contrastive grouping and beam search, our model achieves a 100\% full simplification rate on a representative selection of 5-point gluon tree-level amplitudes in Yang-Mills theory, including expressions with over 200 initial terms.

</details>

*Naomi Gendler,Elijah Sheridan,Michael Stillman,David H. Wu*
