TL;DR: 该研究探讨了卡拉比-丘（Calabi-Yau）三维流形有效锥（effective cone）中的"空洞"现象——即某些除子类（divisor classes）本身不是有效的（non-effective），并分析了其在环面超曲面卡拉比-丘三维流形系综中的特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于这些除子在弦论（string theory）中非微扰势（non-perturbative potentials）的作用，特别关注卡拉比-丘三维流形有效锥中的除子特性。

Method: 方法包括分析环面超曲面卡拉比-丘三维流形（toric hypersurface Calabi-Yau threefolds）的系综，证明空洞存在的必要和充分条件，并运用极小模型纲领（minimal model program）推导相关结果。

Result: 研究发现存在非全纯除子类（non-holomorphic divisor classes）的"空洞"，证明其存在条件，展示空洞构成半群（semigroups），并提供了表示空洞的四维环（four-cycles）体积的模依赖界限（moduli-dependent bounds）。

Conclusion: 该研究系统刻画了卡拉比-丘流形有效锥中的空洞现象，建立了其数学特性与弦论物理背景的联系，为理解非微扰效应提供了几何基础。

Abstract: Motivated by their role in non-perturbative potentials in string theory, we study divisors in effective cones of Calabi-Yau threefolds. We give examples of geometries for which some divisor classes in the effective cone are not themselves effective: i.e., they have no global sections. We call these non-holomorphic divisor classes "holes," and characterize their behavior in an ensemble of toric hypersurface Calabi-Yau threefolds. We prove some necessary and sufficient conditions for the existence of holes, show consequences of holes that follow from the minimal model program, and demonstrate that a class of holes come in semigroups (with this class conjectured to constitute all holes). Furthermore, we provide moduli-dependent bounds on the volumes of four-cycles representing holes.

### [47] [The phase diagram of the D1-D5 CFT and localized black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11181)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In this paper we analyze the phases that dominate the microcanonical ensemble at various energies in the D1-D5 CFT, which is dual to type II string theory on $AdS_3 \times S^3\times T^4$. We focus on black hole solutions, and on the dependence of the phase structure on the ratio of the size of the torus to the AdS scale; as small localized black holes (with horizon topology $S^8$) grow, they can start to fill the $S^3$ or the $T^4$ or both, and we analyze the general aspects of the transitions between the various phases of uniform and non-uniform black holes, incorporating known solutions and discussing the properties of additional unknown solutions. Some features of the transitions between these phases are similar to higher dimensional AdS spaces, while other features are different. We provide evidence that when the torus is much larger than the AdS radius, there is a large range of energies where the typical states are a novel phase, described by a lattice (in the $T^4$ directions) of black holes with horizon topology $S^5\times S^3$. In this phase the entropy is linear in the energy, with a coefficient that is of order the AdS radius.

### [49] [One-loop mass corrections and decay widths of Type II heavy string states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11343)
*Massimo Bianchi,Maurizio Firrotta,Lorenzo Grimaldi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文系统研究了一环质量修正对（超）弦理论中高自旋态的影响，重点关注第一Regge轨迹态，通过椭圆函数和格点求和推导闭式表达式，并应用$i\varepsilon$正则化处理红外发散积分，计算至N=10能级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在系统研究（超）弦理论中高自旋态的一环质量修正（one-loop mass corrections）。虽然相关振幅的虚部有限（与树图水平下态衰变为两个低质量态的宽度相关），但实部通常存在红外发散（IR-divergent），需要正则化和重整化处理。

Method: 主要关注Type-II弦理论NS-NS扇区中第一Regge轨迹态。基于椭圆函数（elliptic functions）和格点求和（lattice sums）的性质，显式推导了插入点积分的闭式表达式。随后应用弦理论中的$i\varepsilon$-prescription正则化环面模参数（modular parameter of the torus）的红外发散积分。

Result: 计算了至能级N=10的质量修正，并分析了其随N增加的行为。最终推测低自旋态之间存在混合（mixing），并猜想一环质量矩阵可能由某种随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）支配。

Conclusion: 研究为弦理论高自旋态的一环质量修正提供了系统分析框架，揭示了红外发散的正则化方法，并提出了质量矩阵可能遵循随机矩阵理论的猜想，为进一步理解弦谱的量子修正奠定基础。

Abstract: We start a systematic investigation of the one-loop mass corrections to (super-)string massive higher-spin states. While the imaginary part of the relevant amplitudes are finite, being related to the width of the decay of the states into two lower-mass states at tree level, the real part is generally IR-divergent and needs regularization and renormalization. We mostly focus on states of the first Regge trajectory in the NS-NS sector of Type-II string theories. We explicitly derive a closed-form expression for the integral over the insertion point, relying on properties of elliptic functions and lattice sums. We then regularize the IR divergent integral over the modular parameter of the torus, applying the $i\varepsilon$-prescription in string theory. As a result we compute the desired mass corrections up to level $N = 10$ and analyze their behavior at increasing $N$. Finally, we speculate on the existence of mixing among lower-spin states and conjecture that the one-loop mass matrix be governed by some random matrix theory.

Abstract: By employing the gradient flow exact renormalization group (GFERG), we study the renormalization group (RG) flow of a manifestly gauge or BRST invariant non-perturbative ansatz of the 1PI Wilson action in quantum electrodynamics. The gauge invariance of the Wilson action is \emph{exactly\/} preserved under the RG flow. We explicitly solve the GFERG equation in the leading and partially the next to leading orders of the large $N_f$ approximation, where $N_f$ is the number of flavors. ### [52] [Quantum backreaction and stability of topological wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11724)
*Haris Mehulic,Tomislav Prokopec*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探究具有简单几何结构 $M_2 \times S^2$ 的类时拓扑虫洞（timelike topological wormhole）在量子效应下的稳定性。这类虫洞由各向异性流体（anisotropic fluid）经典支持，需要理解量子涨落对其稳定性的影响。

Method: 采用维度正则化（dimensional regularization）方法对最小耦合大质量标量场（minimally coupled, massive scalar field）在虫洞背景上传播产生的真空涨落进行一圈量子反作用计算。通过重整化（renormalization）处理一圈能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor），并识别必要的引力抵消项（gravitational counterterms）。

Result: 求解到 $\hbar$ 线性阶的半经典爱因斯坦方程（semiclassical Einstein equations），发现量子效应根据有限抵消项（finite counterterms）的选择，可诱导负或正的角向压力（angular pressure），分别倾向于破坏或稳定虫洞结构。同时证明经典可穿越虫洞（classically traversable wormhole）在考虑量子反作用后仍保持可穿越性。

Conclusion: 量子效应对虫洞稳定性具有双重影响，取决于有限抵消项的选择。研究指出需要进一步探讨当半经典引力方程自洽求解时，这些结论是否仍然成立，为理解量子引力效应下的虫洞稳定性提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We investigate the quantum stability of a timelike topological wormhole with a simple geometry $M_2 \times S^2$, supported classically by anisotropic fluid. We compute the one-loop quantum backreaction generated by the vacuum fluctuations of a minimally coupled, massive scalar field propagating on the wormhole background. Using dimensional regularization we renormalize the one-loop energy-momentum tensor and identify the necessary gravitational counterterms. We then solve the semiclassical Einstein equations to linear order in $\hbar$ for both time-dependent and static metric {\it Ansätze}. Depending on the choice of finite counterterms, the quantum effects can induce either negative or positive angular pressure, which will tend to destabilize or stablize the wormhole, respectively.
  We also show that a classically traversable wormhole will remain traversable when the quantum backreaction is taken into account. It would be of interest to investigate whether these conclusions remain true when the equations of semiclassical gravity are self-consistently solved.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法采用刚性$E_{11}$模型，其中广义坐标被视为在刚性对称性下惰性（inert），这与E理论（E-theory）的处理方式形成对比。通过系统性地包含广义坐标，检验Sugawara型流代数构造的可行性。

Conclusion: 本文结论表明，虽然刚性$E_{11}$模型中可以实现Sugawara型流代数构造，但$E_{11} \otimes_s l_1$上的双线性形式存在退化问题，这为M理论的流代数表述提出了重要的数学挑战。

Abstract: We examine the proposal of [29] that M-theory may admit a Sugawara-type current algebra formulation based on $E_{11} \otimes_s l_1$. Motivated by the role of generalized coordinates in E-theory, we ask whether current algebra relations of this type can be derived in a setting that includes those coordinates systematically. We show that such a construction can indeed be carried out for a rigid $E_{11}$ model in which the generalized coordinates are treated as inert under the rigid symmetry, in contrast with E-theory. We also argue that the bilinear form entering the Schwinger term requires closer scrutiny, since any natural ad-invariant extension of the $E_{11}$ Cartan-Killing form to $E_{11} \otimes_s l_1$ is degenerate.

### [54] [Soft cutoffs in the covariant phase space of dynamical reference frames](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11966)

Method: 通过引入动力学参考框架（dynamical reference frames, DRFs）并利用涂抹函数及其对应的算子展开，将协变作用量从硬截断推广到软截断形式。通过限制DRFs及其关联的线性MCFs为特定形式，并对涂抹函数施加适当的边界条件来恢复协变性。

Abstract: We construct covariant theories incorporating fluctuating boundaries and soft cutoffs by introducing dynamical reference frames (DRFs). This framework generalizes the covariant action from a hard-cutoff to a soft-cutoff formulation, utilizing smearing functions and their corresponding operator expansions. This generalization initially leads to a loss of diffeomorphism covariance, which is recovered solely by restricting the DRFs, along with both their associated and linear MCFs, to specific forms, and by imposing suitable boundary conditions on the smearing functions. Satisfying these conditions restores covariance in relational spacetime, thereby enabling the consistent definition of subsystems. Within the covariant phase space formalism, we derive the charges of the soft-cutoff theory while explicitly addressing the inherent ambiguities arising from the boundary Lagrangian. We demonstrate that introducing an additional pointwise dependence is essential to resolve these ambiguities and ensure the integrability of the charges, even under fluctuating boundary conditions. Finally, in the context of General Relativity (GR), we establish the conditions under which holographic renormalization results at the asymptotic boundary coincide with the Noether charges derived from our soft-cutoff procedure.

Abstract: We revisit and extend the construction of bulk local states in flat holography, focusing on the induced representation obtained from the flat limit of the AdS highest-weight conditions. In three dimensions we clarify the scaling mismatch between bra and ket states in the flat basis and resolve it by introducing a dual basis, which yields a smooth flat limit and reproduces the correct Green's function. For higher dimensions we construct bulk local states explicitly, both in the momentum basis and in an alternative tilde basis. The flat limit of the AdS$_{d+1}$ construction is shown to be non-uniform in the descendant level and the Riemann-sum treatment over the scaling window $n\sim l$ converts the discrete descendant expansion into the continuum momentum representation, recovering the massive propagator. The tilde basis generalizes seamlessly to any dimension and is related to the three-dimensional flat basis by a sign factor. These results establish the induced representation as the correct algebraic foundation for bulk reconstruction in flat holography and provide a unified framework valid for arbitrary dimension.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于先前研究将量子黑洞描述为模糊球与半填充费米海，本文旨在通过量子隧穿过程解释黑洞的量子衰变机制。核心动机是建立霍金辐射的微观量子力学描述，并确保该过程的幺正性（unitarity）。

Method: 提出模糊球系统向较小系统的隧穿过程描述黑洞量子衰变。由于费米海收缩且哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）守恒费米子数，隧穿振幅为零，除非隧穿路径提供精确数量的零模以吸收多余费米态。引入模糊球上的磁单极子实现这一功能，从而确定隧穿路径。

Result: 计算得到的隧穿率重现了Page关于黑洞半经典衰变率的结果。磁单极子释放的费米态被识别为霍金辐射，其概率分布符合霍金温度下的玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann distribution）。通过实时隧穿过程可确定多体霍金量子的完整波函数，幺正性在量子力学框架下得以显式保持。

Conclusion: 该研究为霍金辐射提供了基于模糊球和费米海的微观量子力学描述，通过引入磁单极子解决隧穿过程中的费米子数守恒问题，成功重现经典结果并确保幺正性。这为理解黑洞量子衰变机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: It was proposed in \cite{Chu:2024qil} that a quantum black hole can be described by a fuzzy sphere together with a half-filled Fermi sea. In this paper we propose that the tunneling of a fuzzy sphere system to a small one describes the quantum decay of black hole by Hawking radiation. Since the Fermi sea shrinks and the quantum mechanical Hamiltonian conserves fermion number, the amplitude of transition naively vanishes unless the tunneling path provides exact number of zero modes to soak up the excess fermi states. We show that a monopole on fuzzy sphere does exactly that. This fixes the tunneling path. The resulting tunneling rate reproduces Page's result for the semi-classical decay rate of black hole. We propose to identify the fermi states released by the monopole as the Hawking radiation. At the level of probability, the Hawking radiation is found to be given by a Boltzmann distribution at the Hawking temperature. One can go beyond the probabilistic description by determining the full wave function of the multi-partite Hawking quanta. This is possible with a real time formulation of the tunneling process. Unitarity is manifest in our quantum mechanics.

</details>

# cond-mat.str-el [[Back]](#toc)

### [60] [Moiré in $Γ$-valley square lattice: Copper- and iron-based superconductor simulation in a single device](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11153)
*Toshikaze Kariyado,Yusuf Wicaksono,Ashvin Vishwanath,Pavel Volkov,Zhu-Xi Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究提出利用Γ能谷（Γ-valley）方形晶格莫尔（moiré）异质结构模拟高温超导体的有效模型，以ZnF₂为例展示了单轨道和双轨道哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）的实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高温超导体（cuprates、铁基和镍酸盐家族）均基于方形晶格，展现丰富的强关联现象，但现有莫尔异质结构主要基于六方晶格。本研究旨在探索利用Γ能谷方形晶格莫尔系统模拟这些高温超导体物理的可能性。

Method: 研究结合了连续哈密顿量建模（continuum Hamiltonian modeling）、第一性原理计算（first-principle calculations）和哈特里-福克平均场理论（Hartree-Fock mean field theory）。特别关注双轨道模型的四分之一填充（quarter-filling）区域。

Result: 在ZnF₂材料中，第一莫尔带实现了单轨道方形晶格哈伯德模型，可模拟铜酸盐物理；第二和第三莫尔带映射到px,py双轨道方形晶格哈伯德模型，与铁基超导体的最小dxz,dyz模型共享物理机制。在双轨道模型的四分之一填充区域发现了稳定的反铁轨道-铁磁绝缘相（antiferro-orbital, ferromagnetic insulating phase）。

Conclusion: Γ能谷方形晶格莫尔系统代表了范德华（van der Waals）异质结构的新一代平台，能够实现有趣的强关联物相，为模拟高温超导体物理提供了重要途径。

Abstract: Novel superconducting phases have been found in various moiré heterostructures based on hexagonal lattices. However, the archetypal high-temperature superconductors (cuprates, iron-based and nickelate families) all share a square lattice foundation. These materials host a rich landscape of correlated phenomena, such as charge and spin stripes, pseudogap behavior, and unconventional metallicity, which continue to challenge our fundamental understanding of strongly correlated electrons. In this work, we investigate the possibility of simulating the effective models governing these high-$T_c$ superconductors using twisted homobilayers of $Γ$-valley square-lattice systems. We develop a universal theoretical framework and carry out a detailed analysis of a promising candidate material ZnF$_2$. We find that the first moiré band realizes a single-orbital square-lattice Hubbard model, widely believed to capture cuprate physics, while the second and third moiré bands map to a $p_x,p_y$ two-orbital square-lattice Hubbard model, which shares common physics to the minimal $d_{xz}, d_{yz}$ models proposed for iron pnictides. Our study combines continuum Hamiltonian modeling, first-principle calculations, and Hartree-Fock mean field theory. The latter focuses on the quarter-filling regime of the two-orbital model and in particular leads to, among others, a stable antiferro-orbital, ferromagnetic insulating phase. These results highlight $Γ$-valley square-lattice moiré systems as a new and important generation of van der Waals heterostructures to realize interesting strongly correlated phases of matter.

</details>


### [61] [Can electronic quantum criticality drive phonon-induced linear-in-temperature resistivity?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11176)
*Haoyu Guo,Debanjan Chowdhury*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了电子量子临界点附近软化的光学声子（optical phonon）能否在低温下产生线性温度依赖的电阻率（$T$-linear resistivity）。研究提出了模型无关的判据，并分析了Ising-nematic量子临界点的具体机制，发现清洁理论中该机制处于或接近边际边界，且声子反馈效应进一步削弱了低温下稳健的$T$-线性输运。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学声子在高温等分配（equipartition）区域自然产生线性温度依赖的电阻率，但其有限能隙（finite gap）阻碍了该机制在极低温下的持续存在。研究旨在探索电子量子临界点（electronic quantum critical point）附近能否通过强烈软化光学声子来消除这一障碍。

Method: 首先推导了模型无关的判据，要求软化的声子必须满足重整化光学能隙（renormalized optical gap）减小且朗道阻尼声子（Landau-damped phonon）获得动力学指数$z_p>d$。然后分析了具体机制：声子非线性耦合到$\vec{Q}=0$量子临界点附近的长波长电子集体模式，并应用于Ising-nematic情况。采用大$N$场论（large-$N$ field theoretic）表述，并考虑了软化声子对电子临界区域的反馈效应。

Result: 在清洁理论中，临界点附近的声子软化得到增强，但由此产生的动力学处于或接近渐进$T$-线性散射的边际边界。将软化声子反馈到电子临界区域进一步削弱了稳健低温$T$-线性输运的趋势。研究结果明确了基于声子解释电子临界性附近奇异金属（strange-metal）输运的潜力与局限性。

Conclusion: 研究既阐明了电子量子临界点附近软化光学声子作为低温$T$-线性电阻率潜在机制的可能性，也揭示了其局限性。提出的模型无关判据和具体机制分析为理解奇异金属输运现象提供了更精确的理论框架。

Abstract: Optical phonons naturally generate linear-in-$T$ resistivity in the high-temperature equipartition regime, but their finite gap prevents this mechanism from surviving to asymptotically low temperatures. Here we analyze whether proximity to an electronic quantum critical point can remove this obstruction by strongly softening an optical phonon. We first derive a model-independent criterion for such softened phonons to control low-temperature transport: besides reducing the renormalized optical gap, the Landau-damped phonon must acquire a dynamical exponent $z_p>d$, where $d$ is the spatial dimension of the phonon, so that a sufficiently large thermally occupied phase space survives as $T\to 0$. We then analyze a concrete mechanism in which the phonon couples nonlinearly to long-wavelength electronic collective modes near a $\vec{Q}=0$ quantum critical point, and apply it to the Ising-nematic case. Within a large-$N$ field theoretic formulation, the phonon softening is enhanced near criticality, but in the clean theory the resulting dynamics lies at or near the marginal boundary for asymptotic $T$-linear scattering. Including feedback from the softened phonon back onto the electronic critical sector further weakens the tendency toward robust low-temperature $T$-linear transport. Our results sharpen both the promise and the limitations of phonon-based explanations of strange-metal transport near electronic criticality.

</details>


### [62] [Crossover to Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev criticality in an infinite-range quantum Heisenberg spin glass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11263)
*Hossein Hosseinabadi,Subir Sachdev,Jamir Marino*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过大N_f展开方法，分析了无限长程量子海森堡模型的平衡动力学，揭示了系统在SYK临界性与自旋玻璃有序之间的动力学交叉行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解具有随机耦合的无限长程量子海森堡模型的平衡动力学，特别是探究量子涨落对自旋玻璃有序温度的影响，以及系统接近SYK临界相时的动力学行为。

Method: 采用大N_f展开方法，其中N_f控制量子涨落的强度，并自洽地包含Luttinger-Ward泛函的1/N_f修正，以此研究系统的动力学行为。

Result: 在大N_f极限下，系统呈现顺磁-自旋玻璃相变，转变温度与N_f无关；小N_f时量子涨落显著抑制有序温度。系统接近SYK相时，费米子和自旋谱密度在宽频域显示临界行为，最低能标下自旋玻璃动力学主导，产生普适的亚欧姆动力学自旋磁化率χ''(ω)∼sgn(ω)√|ω|。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个理解SYK临界性与自旋玻璃有序之间动力学交叉的最小框架，揭示了量子涨落对自旋玻璃转变的显著影响以及系统在SYK相附近的临界动力学特征。

Abstract: We study the equilibrium dynamics of an infinite-range quantum Heisenberg model with random couplings, in which local magnetic moments arise from $\mathcal{N}_f$ flavors of spinful fermions. We employ an expansion in $\mathcal{N}_f$, which controls the strength of quantum fluctuations, and self-consistently include $1/\mathcal{N}_f$ corrections to the Luttinger-Ward functional. In the large-$\mathcal{N}_f$ limit, where quantum fluctuations are weak, the high- and low-temperature phases are respectively paramagnetic and spin glass ordered, with a transition temperature independent of $\mathcal{N}_f$. For small numbers of fermionic flavors, however, quantum fluctuations substantially suppress the ordering temperature. We show that this behavior reflects the proximity of the system to a Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) phase, where both fermionic and spin spectral densities display critical behavior over a broad range of finite frequencies, with the latter exhibiting the scale-invariant form $χ''(ω)\sim \operatorname{sgn}(ω)$. At the lowest energies and temperatures, spin-glass dynamics ultimately take over, producing a universal sub-Ohmic dynamical spin susceptibility $χ''(ω)\sim \operatorname{sgn}(ω)\sqrt{|ω|}$. Our results establish a minimal framework for understanding dynamical crossovers between SYK criticality and spin-glass ordering.

</details>


### [63] [Dimensionality tuning of heavy-fermion states in ultrathin CeSi2 films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11289)
*Yi Wu,Weifan Zhu,Teng Hua,Yuan Fang,Yanan Zhang,Jiawen Zhang,Yanen Huang,Hao Zheng,Shanyin Fu,Xinying Zheng,Zhengtai Liu,Mao Ye,Ye Chen,Tulai Sun,Michael Smidman,Johann Kroha,Chao Cao,Huiqiu Yuan,Frank Steglich,Hai-Qing Lin,Yang Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过分子束外延（MBE）、原位角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）和输运测量，系统研究了重费米子化合物CeSi2薄膜厚度对电子态的影响，揭示了维度调控对晶体电场激发和近藤过程的重要作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 维度调控是改变量子材料电子态的重要方法，但在重费米子（heavy fermion）体系中，这种调控机制及其与输运性质的关系尚未得到充分探索。研究旨在理解强关联4f电子系统中的量子限制效应。

Method: 结合分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）、原位角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）和输运测量，系统研究重费米子化合物CeSi2薄膜厚度对电子态的影响。

Result: 三维厚膜中观察到费米能级（Fermi level, EF）处的色散近藤峰（Kondo peak）和源自晶体电场（crystal electric field, CEF）激发的卫星峰；二维超薄膜中CEF卫星峰显著抑制，而基态近藤峰保持较强但需更低温度形成。磁电阻最大值温度Tmax从厚膜的~100K降至超薄膜的~35K。

Conclusion: 维度驱动降低了近藤过程中的晶体电场激发，这与光谱结果一致。该工作为理解强关联4f电子系统的量子限制效应提供了直接见解，并为探索二维重费米子材料中的涌现现象开辟了新机遇。

Abstract: Dimensionality tuning is an important method to modify the electronic states of quantum materials. However, the mechanism of such tuning in heavy fermion systems and its connection with transport properties remain largely unexplored. Here by combining molecular beam epitaxy (MBE), in-situ angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) and transport measurements, we study the electronic states of the heavy-fermion compound CeSi2 as a function of film thickness. In three dimensional thick films, our measurements reveal a dispersive Kondo peak at the Fermi level (EF) and satellite peaks originating from crystal electric field (CEF) excitations, characteristic of heavy fermion systems. For two-dimensional ultrathin films, the CEF satellites are largely suppressed while the ground-state Kondo peak at EF remains strong, although it develops at lower temperatures. Simultaneously, the maximum temperature Tmax of the magnetic resistivity, \r{ho}m(T), changes from ~100 K in thick films to ~35 K in ultrathin films. This can be attributed to the dimensionality driven reduction of CEF excitations during the Kondo process, in good agreement with spectroscopic results. Our work provides direct insight to understand the quantum confinement effects on strongly correlated 4f-electron systems and opens up new opportunities to explore emergent phenomena in two-dimensional heavy-fermion materials.

</details>


### [64] [Enhanced carrier binding and bond correlations in the Hubbard-Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model with dispersive optical phonons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11373)
*Debshikha Banerjee,Alberto Nocera,Steven Johnston*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究使用密度矩阵重整化群方法，分析了色散光学声子对轻掺杂一维光学Hubbard-SSH模型中电子配对的影响，发现声子色散显著增强了单重态结合能，但并未转化为超导关联增强，而是形成了稳健的键关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH)模型因其在高温超导中的强电子配对潜力而备受关注，但先前研究主要集中于稀掺杂或半填充模型，且使用无色散（Einstein）声子。本研究旨在探索色散光学声子对轻掺杂一维光学Hubbard-SSH模型的影响。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group）方法，研究轻掺杂一维光学Hubbard-SSH模型中色散光学声子的效应，并通过计算多种关联函数来分析系统性质。

Result: 观察到声子色散显著增强了单重态结合能（singlet binding），但通过计算各种关联函数发现，这种增强的结合能并未转化为超导关联的增强，而是在研究参数范围内形成了稳健的键关联（bond correlations）。

Conclusion: 声子色散对这些关联的显著影响表明，在模拟真实量子材料时，需要超越Einstein声子极限，考虑声子色散效应以获得更准确的物理图像。

Abstract: Electron-phonon (e-ph) interactions play a crucial role in determining many properties of materials. In this context, the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model, where atomic motion modulates the electronic hopping, has gained significant attention due to its potential for strong electron pairing in relation to high-Tc superconductivity. Previous studies of the SSH models have addressed many aspects of this problem, but have focused heavily on either dilute or half-filled models with dispersionless (Einstein) phonons. Here, we study the effects of dispersive optical phonons on the lightly doped one-dimensional optical Hubbard-SSH model using the density matrix renormalization group. We observe a significant enhancement in singlet binding driven by phonon dispersion; however, by calculating various correlation functions, we find that the enhanced binding does not translate to increased superconducting correlations but rather robust bond correlations in the studied parameter regime. Nevertheless, the significant impact of phonon dispersion on these correlations highlights the need to go beyond the Einstein phonon limit while modeling realistic quantum materials.

</details>


### [65] [Electronic Coherence Evolution at the Nearly Commensurate Incommensurate CDW Boundary of 1T-TaS2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11405)
*Turgut Yilmaz,Yi Sheng Ng,Menka Jain,Xiao Tong,Thipusa Wongpinij,Pat Photongkam,Anil Rajapitamahuni,Asish K. Kundu,Jin-Cheng Zheng,Elio Vescovo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究使用角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）分析了1T-TaS2中近公度相到非公度相的转变，发现该转变涉及动量依赖的谱权重新分布而非完全带隙打开，挑战了传统的金属-绝缘体转变图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属二硫族化合物（transition metal dichalcogenides）中的电荷密度波（charge density wave）相变涉及晶格、电荷和关联效应的耦合。在1T-TaS2中，虽然公度相和近公度相已被充分表征，但350K附近向非公度相（incommensurate phase）的转变缺乏直接的动量分辨洞察。

Method: 采用温度依赖的角分辨光电子能谱（angle resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）来追踪跨越该相变的电子结构变化，重点关注布里渊区中心（Brillouin zone center）的准粒子谱权重变化。

Result: 观察到布里渊区中心的准粒子谱权重（quasiparticle spectral weight）被抑制，与输运异常（transport anomaly）同时发生，但没有明确证据显示完全带隙（full band gap）打开。该转变涉及动量依赖的谱权重重新分布，与相干性丧失（loss of coherence）一致，重塑了费米面（Fermi surface）但基本保持了导带色散。

Conclusion: 近公度-非公度相变（nearly commensurate incommensurate transition）可能不符合传统的金属-绝缘体转变（metal insulator transition）图像，而是由相干性丧失驱动的电子重构（electronic reconstruction）。该研究为室温附近的电阻率异常提供了新的微观洞察，并可能指导过渡金属二硫族化合物中集体电子开关的设计原则。

Abstract: Transition metal dichalcogenides host a variety of charge density wave phases that couple lattice, charge, and correlation effects. In 1T-TaS2, the commensurate and nearly commensurate states are well characterized, yet the transition near 350 K into the incommensurate phase has lacked direct momentum resolved insight. Here we use temperature dependent angle resolved photoemission spectroscopy to track the electronic structure across this transition. We observe a suppression of quasiparticle spectral weight at the Brillouin zone center, coincident with the transport anomaly, but without clear evidence of a full band gap opening. The transition appears to involve momentum dependent redistribution of spectral weight, consistent with a loss of coherence that reshapes the Fermi surface while leaving conduction dispersions largely intact. These results suggest that the nearly commensurate incommensurate transition may not align with a conventional metal insulator transition picture, but rather as an electronic reconstruction driven by loss of coherence. Our work provides new microscopic insight into the resistivity anomaly near room temperature and may guide design principles for collective electronic switching in Transition metal dichalcogenides.

</details>


### [66] [Bootstrap Embedding for Interacting Electrons in Phonon Coherent-state Mean Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11463)
*Shariful Islam,Joel Bierman,Yuan Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种费米-玻色自举嵌入（fb-BE）框架，用于处理电子-声子耦合系统的基态。该方法将电子相关性的自举嵌入与声子的自洽相干态平均场处理相结合，能够高效处理大型晶格系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要开发一种能够高效处理大型电子-声子耦合系统的计算方法，特别是在强耦合局域化区域，同时保持计算可行性。

Method: 提出费米-玻色自举嵌入（fermi-bose bootstrap embedding, fb-BE）框架，结合了电子相关性的自举嵌入（bootstrap embedding）与声子的自洽相干态平均场（self-consistent coherent-state mean-field）处理。该方法将电子-声子相互作用问题建模为在自洽势场中运动的关联电子系统。

Result: 在一维Hubbard-Holstein模型中验证了方法对片段尺寸和总系统尺寸（最多350个格点）的收敛性。通过有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）外推到无限系统尺寸。与密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）在8格点系统的基准测试显示运行时间有数量级优势。

Conclusion: 该方法在局域化主导的区域（如Mott绝缘相和强耦合小极化子（tiny polaron）区域）表现最佳，其中局域嵌入近似仍然有效。但由于声子的平均场处理，在弱耦合离域区域和Peierls相变处存在局限性，这些区域量子声子涨落和长程动力学关联变得显著。

Abstract: We develop a fermi-bose bootstrap embedding (fb-BE) framework for the ground state of interacting elec- trons coupled to phonon mean field. The method combines bootstrap embedding for correlated electrons with a self-consistent coherent-state mean-field treatment for phonons. This method models the interacting electron-phonon problem as a system of correlated electrons traveling in a self-consistently specified potential landscape, allowing for efficient treatment of large lattice systems. Convergence of the methods for frag- ment size and total system size are demonstrated for one-dimensional Hubbard-Holstein model for up to 350 sites. Finite-size scaling is performed to extrapolate to infinite system size. Benchmarking against density matrix renormalization group for small 8-site system at half- and quarter-filling shows orders-of-magnitude runtime advantage. The comparison further reveals that the method performs best in regimes dominated by localization, such as the Mott insulating phase and the strong-coupling tiny polaron regime, where the local embedding ansatz is still valid. However, due to the mean-field treatment for phonons, we find limitations of our methods in the weakly coupled delocalized region and at the Peierls transition, where quantum phonon fluctuations and long-range kinetic correlations become substantial.

</details>


### [67] [Foliated-Exotic Duality and Anomaly Inflow in Fracton Quantum Field Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11681)
*Shutaro Shimamura*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文将分形子（fracton）量子场论中的叶状-奇异（foliated-exotic）对偶性扩展到具有子系统对称性（subsystem symmetry）反常（'t Hooft anomaly）的理论中，通过反常流入（anomaly inflow）机制结合子系统对称性保护拓扑（SSPT）相，建立了在无能隙理论中的首个叶状-奇异对偶性示例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分形子相（fracton phases）作为具有子系统全局对称性（subsystem global symmetry）的新型物相，其低能有效描述存在奇异量子场论（exotic QFT）和叶状量子场论（foliated QFT）两种表述。论文旨在将叶状-奇异对偶性（foliated-exotic duality）与子系统对称性的反常流入机制相结合，扩展该对偶性的适用范围。

Method: 采用反常流入机制处理子系统对称性的't Hooft反常，通过构建高维子系统对称性保护拓扑（SSPT）相来捕捉反常。将叶状-奇异对偶性扩展到分形子BF理论和φ-理论中，建立场对应关系并构造相应的叶状描述。

Result: 首先在2+1维奇异和叶状BF理论中，建立了ℤ_N × ℤ_N子系统对称性混合反常的SSPT相描述，并扩展了对偶性至SSPT相。其次在2+1维奇异φ-理论中，通过3+1维U(1)×U(1)子系统对称性SSPT相捕捉反常，首次实现了无能隙理论中的叶状-奇异对偶性。

Conclusion: 论文成功将叶状-奇异对偶性与反常流入机制相结合，扩展了对偶性至具有子系统对称性反常的理论体系。特别是在无能隙的φ-理论中首次实现了该对偶性，为分形子量子场论的两种有效描述提供了更完整的对应框架。

Abstract: Fracton phases are new types of phases of matter characterized by subsystem global symmetry, which is a generalized global symmetry whose symmetry operator is partially topological. Their continuum low-energy effective descriptions admit two different formulations: an exotic quantum field theory (QFT) using exotic tensor gauge fields, and a foliated QFT constructed from a foliation structure and foliated gauge fields. For certain fracton QFTs, these two descriptions are equivalent, which is called the foliated-exotic duality. In this dissertation, we extend the foliated-exotic duality by combining it with the anomaly inflow mechanism for 't Hooft anomalies of subsystem symmetries. This dissertation has two main results. First, we discuss the exotic and foliated $BF$ theories in 2+1 dimensions, which exhibit the mixed 't Hooft anomaly of $\mathbb{Z}_N \times \mathbb{Z}_N$ subsystem symmetry. This anomaly is captured by a subsystem symmetry-protected topological (SSPT) phase for $\mathbb{Z}_N \times \mathbb{Z}_N$ subsystem symmetry in one dimension higher. By extending the foliated-exotic duality in the fractonic $BF$ theory to the SSPT phase, we establish the field correspondences in the SSPT phase and construct the foliated description of the SSPT phase. Second, we discuss the exotic $φ$-theory in 2+1 dimensions -- a fractonic gapless scalar field theory, which has the 't Hooft anomaly of $U(1) \times U(1)$ subsystem symmetry. The anomaly is captured by an SSPT phase for $U(1) \times U(1)$ subsystem symmetry in 3+1 dimensions via the anomaly inflow mechanism. Extending the foliated-exotic duality to the $φ$-theory, we establish field correspondences in the $φ$-theory and construct the foliated $φ$-theory that is equivalent to the exotic $φ$-theory. This provides the first example of the foliated-exotic duality in gapless theories.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究单层Fe₃GeTe₂的电子与磁性质，特别是其在顺磁相中的行为，以理解该化合物的部分巡游磁行为（partially itinerant magnetic behavior）及其磁序稳定机制。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论+动力学平均场理论（DFT+DMFT）方法，在顺磁相中研究Fe₃GeTe₂。考虑中等库仑相互作用（U=3-4 eV），分析两种对称不等价铁原子的磁矩差异。

Abstract: We study the electronic and magnetic properties of monolayer Fe$_3$GeTe$_2$ within the DFT+DMFT approach in the paramagnetic phase. We argue that this compound is sufficiently far from the local magnetic moment limit, demonstrating non-linear temperature dependencies of the partial inverse local and uniform magnetic susceptibilities in a broad temperature range. We find that in the regime of moderate Coulomb interactions ($U=3-4$ eV), the iron atoms located above and below the Ge plane carry a substantial local magnetic moment ($μ\gtrsim 4.5 μ_B$), while the iron atom located within the Ge plane does not exhibit any pronounced magnetic moment. At the same time, the RKKY-type exchange interactions between these two symmetry-nonequivalent types of atoms turn out to be crucial for stabilizing long-range ferromagnetic order in Fe$_3$GeTe$_2$. The estimated spin-wave stiffness and Curie temperature are in good agreement with the experimental data, indicating that a dynamical treatment of electron correlations in Fe$_3$GeTe$_2$ is essential to properly describe its partially itinerant magnetic behavior.

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解拓扑在强关联系统中的存在性是一个核心挑战，因为大多数拓扑诊断方法依赖于非相互作用的能带结构。需要发展能够处理相互作用系统的拓扑表征框架。

Method: 从单粒子格林函数构建单粒子约化密度矩阵（one-body reduced density matrix），并利用它定义有效绕数（effective winding number）和量子体积（quantum volume）。以具有Hatsugai-Kohmoto相互作用的Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型作为解析可处理的例子进行验证。

Result: 该方法能够区分三种绝缘相，包括关联Mott态（correlated Mott states），这些相可以直接从单粒子可观测量中识别。结果表明相互作用拓扑可以通过单粒子激发的谱权重分布来解释。

Conclusion: 该框架为诊断关联系统中的拓扑相提供了一种直观且计算上可行的途径，与现代多体模拟技术兼容，并为识别相互作用拓扑材料开辟了道路。

Abstract: Understanding how topology survives in strongly correlated systems remains a central challenge, as most topological diagnostics rely on non-interacting band structures. Here we present a framework to characterize interacting topological phases within an effective single-particle description derived from the single-particle Green's function. Using the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model with Hatsugai-Kohmoto interactions as an analytically tractable example, we construct the one-body reduced density matrix from the Green's function and use it to define an effective winding number together with quantum volume, a measurement of state geometry. These quantities allow us to distinguish three insulating phases including correlated Mott states directly from single-particle observables. Our results show that interacting topology can be interpreted in terms of the spectral weight distribution of single-particle excitations, providing an intuitive and computationally accessible route to diagnose topological phases in correlated systems. This approach is compatible with modern many-body simulation techniques and opens a pathway toward the identification of interacting topological materials.

Abstract: UTe2 is a rare example of a correlated quantum material in which unconventional density wave orders, Kondo physics, spin-triplet pairing, and reentrant superconductivity coexist within the same electronic system. Its superconducting state develops out of a strongly correlated normal phase. The identification and control of competing or intertwined normal-state orders are thus central to elucidating the electronic landscape from which its superconductivity arises. Here, using scanning tunnelling microscopy (STM) in a vector magnetic field, we uncover a previously unreported staggered charge-density-wave (CDW) in high-quality UTe2 crystals and demonstrate its strong directional response to an external magnetic field: the staggered CDW is completely quenched by a modest 1.7 T field aligned with the quasi-one-dimensional uranium chain direction (a-axis), while remaining robust against fields along other crystallographic directions. This pronounced anisotropy is consistent with an orbital-driven mechanism that leads to a field-tuned quantum phase transition. Strikingly and counterintuitively, the same field orientation and strength concomitantly alter the hybridization gap and suppress the 5f Kondo resonance. Modelling indicates that this correlated evolution arises from a switch of the dominant hybridization channel from Te 5p- U 5f to U 6d- U 5f coupling, suggesting an intimate interplay between CDW and the Kondo effect. Our work establishes an effective tuning knob for the intertwined orders in UTe2 and provides evidence for orbital-selective Kondo hybridization, shedding light on its correlated normal state.

### [74] [Stable Topology in Exactly Flat Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12258)
*Yan-Qi Li,Yi-Jie Wang,Pei-Han Lin,Bin Wang,Zhi-Da Song*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种克服传统禁戒定理的方法，通过构建临界拓扑平带（critical topological flat bands, CTFBs），在有限程跳跃模型中实现了同时具有精确平坦性和稳定拓扑性的能带结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑平带（topological flat bands）为实现奇异拓扑相（如分数量子陈绝缘体）提供了理想平台，但由于基本禁戒定理（no-go theorems）的限制，在局域晶格模型中同时实现精确平坦性和稳定拓扑性一直面临挑战。

Method: 通过构建临界拓扑平带（CTFBs），其布洛赫波函数在整个布里渊区连续但在孤立能带接触点非解析，从而放松了精确平坦性与稳定拓扑性共存的固有限制。建立了构造具有特定拓扑不变量的CTFBs及其母哈密顿量的一般原理。

Result: 提供了二维和三维空间中展示陈数（Chern numbers）、强$\mathbb{Z}_2$指标和晶体对称性保护不变量的具体实例。自动化算法识别出超过50,000个鲁棒的、对称性指示的CTFBs。填充这些CTFB会产生具有幂律关联的短程纠缠拓扑态。

Conclusion: 所有填充的CTFB态都允许具有有限键维数的精确张量网络表示，这为探索强关联拓扑物质提供了一个可处理的起点，克服了传统禁戒定理对同时实现精确平坦性和稳定拓扑性的限制。

Abstract: Topological flat bands (FBs) offer an ideal platform for realizing exotic topological phases, such as fractional Chern insulators, yet their realization with both exact flatness and stable topology in local lattice models has been long hindered by fundamental no-go theorems. Here, we overcome this barrier by demonstrating the existence of critical topological FBs (CTFBs) in finite-range hopping models. They saturate the no-go theorems via a unique structure of Bloch wavefunctions: While continuous over the whole Brillouin zone, the wavefunctions are non-analytic at isolated band touching points, thereby relaxing the inherent restrictions on the coexistence of exact flatness and stable topology. We establish a general principle to construct CTFBs, as well as their parent Hamiltonians, that carry desired topological invariants in given space groups. Explicit examples exhibiting Chern numbers, strong $\mathbb{Z}_2$ index, and crystalline-symmetry-protected invariants in two and three dimensions are provided. Furthermore, an automated algorithm identifies more than 50,000 robust, symmetry-indicated CTFBs. Filling such CTFBs yields short-range entangled topological states that exhibit power-law correlations. Crucially, all filled CTFB states admit exact tensor-network representations with finite bond dimensions, providing a tractable starting point for exploring strongly correlated topological matter.

</details>

### [75] [From Phase Prediction to Phase Design: A ReAct Agent Framework for High-Entropy Alloy Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11068)
*Iman Peivaste,Salim Belouettar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的ReAct智能体，用于高效逆向设计高熵合金（HEA）成分，相比传统贝叶斯优化和随机搜索方法，在相结构预测准确性和成分多样性探索方面表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统试错实验和前向机器学习模型难以高效解决高熵合金（high-entropy alloy, HEA）成分的逆向设计问题，需要开发能够自主提出、验证和迭代优化合金成分的新方法。

Method: 构建了一个ReAct（Reasoning + Acting）大语言模型智能体，通过查询基于4,753个实验记录训练、覆盖四种相结构（FCC、BCC、BCC+FCC、BCC+IM）的校准XGBoost代理模型，实现合金成分的自主设计和迭代优化。

Result: 该智能体在FCC、BCC和BCC+FCC相结构的描述符空间重发现率分别达到38%、18%和38%，且其提案比随机搜索更接近实验相流形（2.4-22.8倍）。领域先验知识使智能体从文献密集区域转向成分多样性探索，其推理与经验相分布统计一致（BCC相Spearman相关系数ρ=0.736，p=0.004）。

Conclusion: 大语言模型引导的智能推理为逆向合金设计提供了一种原理清晰、透明且对流形敏感的补充方法，可作为无梯度优化（gradient-free optimisation）的有效替代方案。

Abstract: Discovering high-entropy alloy (HEA) compositions that reliably form a target crystal phase is a high-dimensional inverse design problem that conventional trial-and-error experimentation and forward-only machine learning models cannot efficiently solve. Here we present a ReAct (Reasoning + Acting) LLM agent that autonomously proposes, validates, and iteratively refines HEA compositions by querying a calibrated XGBoost surrogate trained on 4,753 experimental records across four phases (FCC, BCC, BCC+FCC, BCC+IM), achieving 94.66\% accuracy (F1 macro = 0.896). Against Bayesian optimisation (BO) and random search baselines, the full-prompt agent achieves descriptor-space rediscovery rates of 38\%, 18\%, and 38\% for FCC, BCC, and BCC+FCC (Mann--Whitney $p \leq 0.039$), with proposals lying 2.4--22.8$\times$ closer to the experimental phase manifold than random search. An ablation reveals that domain priors shift the agent from landmark-alloy recall toward compositionally diverse exploration -- an uninformed agent scores higher rediscovery by concentrating on literature-dense families, while the full-prompt agent explores underrepresented space (unique ratio 1.0 vs.\ 0.39 for BCC+FCC). These regimes represent distinct criteria: proximity to known literature versus genuine discovery. Spearman analysis confirms agent reasoning is statistically aligned with empirical phase distributions ($ρ= 0.736$, $p = 0.004$ for BCC). This work establishes LLM-guided agentic reasoning as a principled, transparent, and manifold-aware complement to gradient-free optimisation for inverse alloy design.

</details>


### [76] [Exceptional Optical Phonon Coherence in Enriched Cubic Boron Arsenide via Suppression of Three-Phonon Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11256)
*Tong Lin,Fengjiao Pan,Gaihua Ye,Sanjna Sukumaran,Cynthia Nnokwe,Ange Benise Niyikiza,William A. Smith,Stephen B. Bayne,Rui He,Zhifeng Ren,Hanyu Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 立方砷化硼（BAs）因其优异的双极性迁移率和热导率成为下一代电子器件的有前途材料，但高阶非谐散射过程的理论与实验分析仍具挑战。本研究通过高分辨率光谱技术揭示了该材料中区域中心光学声子的超长相干性，并区分了三种退相干机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 立方砷化硼（cubic boron arsenide, BAs）因其出色的双极性迁移率（ambipolar mobility）和热导率成为下一代电子器件的有前途材料，其高热导率主要归因于三声子散射（three-phonon scattering）的抑制。然而，精确解释不同高阶非谐散射（high-order anharmonic scattering）过程在理论和实验上都面临挑战，导致关于BAs中声子寿命和热导率的最终极限问题仍未解决。

Method: 研究采用高分辨率拉曼光谱（high-resolution Raman spectroscopy）和傅里叶变换红外光谱（Fourier transform infrared spectroscopy）技术，通过分析阻尼率（damping rate）的温度依赖性贡献来区分三种退相干机制（decoherence mechanisms）。实验使用同位素纯度高于98%的富集$^{11}$BAs样品。

Result: 研究发现能隙（gap）在宽温度范围内几乎消除了区域中心光学声子（zone-center optical phonons）的三声子散射，导致在低于100K时同位素纯度限制的声子相干性（phonon coherence）创下纪录，品质因子（quality factor）超过$3.7\times 10^3$。对于合成晶体，缺陷散射（defect scattering）对光学声子线宽（linewidth）的贡献与同位素散射（isotope scattering）相比可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 这些结果为BAs中光学声子的内在和外在散射机制提供了关键见解，激励进一步研究以量化非谐效应（anharmonic effects）并实现优越的声子输运（phonon transport）。研究揭示了该材料中声子相干性的极限，为理解其热导率机制提供了重要实验证据。

Abstract: Cubic boron arsenide (BAs) is a promising semiconductor for next-generation electronics due to its outstanding ambipolar mobility and thermal conductivity, the latter of which is attributed to the suppression of three-phonon scattering. However, precisely accounting for different high-order anharmonic scattering processes is challenging from both theory and experiment, so that questions remain open regarding the ultimate limit of phonon lifetime and thermal conductivity in BAs. Here we show that this gap nearly eliminates three-phonon scattering for zone-center optical phonons in a wide temperature range, leading to a record-high, isotope purity-limited phonon coherence with a quality factor above $3.7\times 10^3$ for >98% enriched $^{11}$BAs below 100 K. We discriminate three decoherence mechanisms by their temperature-dependent contribution to the damping rate using high-resolution Raman and Fourier transform infrared spectroscopy. For the as-synthesized crystals, we find that defect scattering has negligible contributions to the linewidth of optical phonons in comparison to isotope scattering. These results provide critical insights into the intrinsic and extrinsic scattering mechanisms of optical phonons in BAs, motivating further studies to quantify anharmonic effects and realize superior phonon transport.

</details>

Conclusion: 该手性自旋交叉材料实现了热可切换的手性光学活性，其机制源于自旋态转变伴随的Fe 3d电子结构重组，且材料中的电荷输运主要受离子迁移控制，这为开发新型手性光电器件提供了材料基础。

Abstract: We demonstrate thermally switchable chiroptical activity in a chiral spin crossover (SCO) material, where circular dichroism is significant in the low spin state but quenched in the high-spin state for both enantiomers. With magnetometry we establish a cooperative transition with hysteresis near room temperature. Fe L3,2 edge Xray absorption directly links the quenching of chirality to a reorganization of Fe 3d electronic structure that accompanies the spin state transition. Moreover, electrical measurements show pronounced I(V) hysteresis and cycling dependent C(V) behavior, indicating transport in this chiral SCO material is dominated by ionic migration rather than mobile electrons or holes.

### [78] [Intrinsic Even-Odd Thickness-Driven Anomalous Hall in Epitaxial MnBi2Te4 Thin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11305)
*Debarghya Mallick,Simon Kim,An-Hsi Chen,Gabriel A. Vázquez-Lizardi,Alessandro R. Mazza,T. Zac Ward,Gyula Eres,Yue Cao,Debangshu Mukherjee,Hu Miao,Liang Wu,Christopher Nelson,Danielle Reifsnyder Hickey,Robert G. Moore,Matthew Brahlek*

TL;DR: 通过分子束外延精确控制MnBi2Te4薄膜的磁学性质，揭示了反常霍尔效应的奇偶层依赖性，为实现拓扑材料中的零场量子反常霍尔效应奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究MnBi2Te4薄膜中磁性的精确控制，旨在理解其本征反常霍尔效应特性，为实现拓扑材料中的零场量子反常霍尔效应（zero-field quantum anomalous Hall effect）提供关键基础。

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）技术进行薄膜合成，通过优化Mn-Bi-Te比例和生长温度实现缺陷最小化和精确层厚控制；结合X射线衍射和反射率进行结构表征，并与磁输运测量（magnetotransport measurements）进行关联分析。

Result: 发现反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）具有显著的奇偶层依赖性：奇数层薄膜在尼尔温度（~25K）以下表现出大磁滞回线，符合非补偿反铁磁性；偶数层薄膜响应极小，符合反铁磁体预期；反常霍尔效应的符号在本质磁性与缺陷相关磁性之间发生反转。

Conclusion: 该工作确定了诱导纯净非补偿铁磁性的关键因素，揭示了MnBi2Te4中本征反常霍尔效应的特性，为在拓扑材料中实现零场量子反常霍尔效应迈出了重要一步。

Abstract: We demonstrate precise control of magnetism in MnBi2Te4 thin films through careful synthesis by molecular beam epitaxy, achieving minimal defects and accurate layer thickness control. By optimizing Mn-Bi-Te ratios and growth temperatures, we minimize detrimental self-doping effects and accurately target integer-layer films. X-ray diffraction and reflectivity provide quantitative measures of film quality and thickness. When these macroscale probes of structure and thickness are integrated with magnetotransport measurements, a striking even-odd layer dependence of the anomalous Hall effect is revealed. Odd-layer films exhibit a large hysteresis up to the Néel temperature (~25K), consistent with non-compensated antiferromagnetism, while even-layer films show minimal response, as expected for an antiferromagnet. The sign of the anomalous Hall effect exhibits a sign reversal for intrinsic magnetism versus magnetism associated with defects. This work identifies critical factors for inducing pure, non-compensated ferromagnetism and reveals the character of the intrinsic anomalous Hall effect in MnBi2Te4, which together is a step towards realizing the zero-field quantum anomalous Hall effect in topological materials.

### [79] [Atomic-Scale Mechanisms of SiO$_2$ Plasma-Enhanced Chemical Vapor Deposition Revealed by Molecular Dynamics with a Machine-Learning Interatomic Potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11416)
*Jaehoon Kim,Minseok Moon,Hyunsung Cho,Hyeon-Deuk Kim,Rokyeon Kim,Gyehyun Park,Seungwu Han,Youngho Kang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过机器学习原子间势能驱动的分子动力学模拟，揭示了等离子体增强化学气相沉积（PECVD）二氧化硅薄膜的原子尺度生长机制，阐明了氧化剂与硅烷比例对薄膜成分、密度和氢含量的影响规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 等离子体增强化学气相沉积（plasma-enhanced chemical vapor deposition, PECVD）二氧化硅薄膜在低温制备中广泛应用，但其原子尺度的生长机制尚未完全阐明。理解这些基本过程对于优化薄膜成分和质量至关重要。

Method: 研究采用机器学习原子间势能（machine-learning interatomic potential）驱动的分子动力学模拟，以硅烷（silane）和N₂O为源气体，系统改变氧化剂与硅烷衍生物种的比例r，分析薄膜生长过程。

Result: Si-O-Si网络主要通过表面Si-H基团氧化形成Si-OH物种，随后相邻Si-OH基团缩合产生H₂O副产物而构建。低r条件下，Si-H与Si-OH基团反应生成H₂也促进网络形成。增加氧化剂供应通过氧化残余Si-H物种促进网络形成，抑制氢掺入并导致Si/O比饱和。硅烷衍生物种的快速化学吸附与预沉积物种的空间位阻导致局部生长和表面粗糙度。高动能等离子体物种可刻蚀SiO₂薄膜，可能限制生长速率并增加高射频功率条件下的表面粗糙度。

Conclusion: 该研究为PECVD生长提供了原子尺度洞察，并为优化薄膜成分和质量提供了指导。揭示了氧化剂比例对薄膜网络形成、氢含量和表面形貌的关键影响机制。

Abstract: Plasma-enhanced chemical vapor deposition (PECVD) of silicon dioxide (SiO$_2$) is widely used for low-temperature fabrication of dielectric thin films, yet its atomic-scale growth mechanisms remain incompletely understood. In this work, we investigate SiO$_2$ PECVD using silane and N$_2$O as source gases via molecular dynamics simulations driven by a machine-learning interatomic potential. By systematically varying the oxidant-to-silane-derived species ratio $r$, we elucidate the evolution of film stoichiometry, density, and hydrogen content. Formation of the Si-O-Si network primarily proceeds via oxidation of surface Si-H groups to form Si-OH species, followed by condensation of neighboring Si-OH groups that produces H$_2$O as the dominant byproduct. At low $r$, H$_2$ formation via reactions between Si-H and Si-OH groups also contributes to the network formation. Increasing oxidant supply promotes the network formation through oxidation of residual Si-H species, suppressing hydrogen incorporation and leading to saturation of the Si/O ratio. Rapid chemisorption of silane-derived species, together with steric hindrance from pre-deposited species, results in localized growth and surface roughness. We further show that high-kinetic-energy plasma species can etch SiO$_2$ films, which potentially limits growth rates and enhances surface roughness under high RF-power conditions. These results provide atomic-scale insight into PECVD growth and guidance for optimizing film composition and quality.

</details>


### [80] [Valley-dependent electron-phonon scattering in thermoelectric semimetal Ta$_2$PdSe$_6$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11496)
*Masayuki Ochi,Hitoshi Mori,Akitoshi Nakano*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过理论计算揭示了准一维过渡金属硫族化合物Ta$_2$PdSe$_6$中电子-声子散射的强谷依赖性，解释了其热电性能中观测到的强电子-空穴不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准一维过渡金属硫族化合物Ta$_2$PdSe$_6$因其载流子寿命中强烈的电子-空穴不对称性而成为有前景的热电半金属材料，但这种强不对称性的微观起源尚不清楚。

Method: 研究通过理论计算分析了Ta$_2$PdSe$_6$中的电子-声子散射（electron-phonon scattering），重点关注PdSe$_4$链中原子位移主导的软声子模式（soft phonon mode）及其与能带的耦合机制。

Result: 发现软声子模式与费米能级（Fermi energy）附近最高价带（valence band）强耦合，导致强电子-声子散射；电子口袋（electron pocket）底部因能带重叠而经历强谷间散射（intervalley scattering），使其自能（self-energy）虚部在费米能级附近急剧变化，而空穴口袋（hole pocket）载流子的自能虚部则呈现温和的能量依赖性。

Conclusion: 研究证实Ta$_2$PdSe$_6$中的电子-声子散射具有强烈的谷依赖性（valley-dependent），这一发现有助于理解该材料中观测到的独特输运性质（transport properties）。

Abstract: Quasi-one-dimensional transition-metal chalcogenide Ta$_2$PdSe$_6$ is a promising thermoelectric semimetal due to the strong electron-hole asymmetry in the carrier lifetime. However, the microscopic origin of such a strong asymmetry remains unclear. In this study, we theoretically investigate electron-phonon scattering in Ta$_2$PdSe$_6$. There is a soft phonon mode mainly consisting of atomic displacements in PdSe$_4$ chains. This soft mode is strongly coupled with the highest valence band at the $Γ$ point, which lies slightly below the Fermi energy, and causes strong electron-phonon scattering. The bottom of the electron pocket energetically overlapped with that band also suffers from strong intervalley scattering, by which the imaginary part of the electron self-energy exhibits a sharp change near the Fermi level. On the other hand, the imaginary part of the self-energy for carriers in the hole pocket shows a moderate energy dependence. Thus, we find that electron-phonon scattering is strongly valley-dependent. Our finding will help us to understand the distinctive transport properties observed in Ta$_2$PdSe$_6$.

### [81] [Meta-generalized gradient approximation made in the Hartree gauge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11517)
*Yan Oueis,Akilan Ramasamy,James W. Furness,Jamin Kidd,Timo Lebeda,Jianwei Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在Hartree规范下构建的元广义梯度近似（meta-GGA）交换能泛函，利用氢原子交换能密度进行规范对齐，为更精确的非局域密度泛函奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在密度泛函理论（DFT）中，交换关联（XC）能量密度的空间定义不唯一，其精确约束只能在特定规范（gauge）下表述，因此很少用于密度泛函近似（DFA）的构建。这限制了基于XC能量密度精确约束的泛函发展。

Method: 提出在Hartree规范下构建元广义梯度近似（meta-generalized gradient approximation）交换能泛函，利用氢原子的交换能密度在核心区和渐近区进行规范对齐（gauge alignment）。该方法在XC能量密度层面构建DFA。

Result: 该方法扩展了机器学习（machine learning）的参考数据集，并为需要规范对齐的更精确非局域密度泛函（nonlocal density functionals）建立了基础。

Conclusion: 通过在XC能量密度层面构建DFA，并利用氢原子进行规范对齐，该方法能够更好地利用精确约束，为发展更准确的密度泛函近似提供了新途径。

Abstract: In density functional theory (DFT), exact constraints, fundamental mathematical properties of the exchange-correlation (XC) energy and its underlying XC hole, along with paradigm systems such as the uniform electron gas and the hydrogen atom have been instrumental in developing exchange- correlation (XC) density functional approximations (DFAs). However, since the spatial XC energy density is not uniquely defined, its exact constraints can only be formulated within a chosen gauge and are therefore seldom utilized in DFA construction. Here, we propose a meta-generalized gradient approximation for the exchange energy, explicitly constructed within the Hartree gauge, using the hydrogen atom's exchange energy density for gauge alignment in core and asymptotic regions. By formulating DFAs at the XC energy density level, this approach expands reference datasets for machine learning and establishes a foundation for more accurate nonlocal density functionals requiring gauge alignment.

</details>


### [82] [Why ice is so slippery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11539)
*Sigbjørn Løland Bore,B. N. J. Persson,Henrik Andersen Sveinsson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过纳米尺度第一性原理模拟结合摩擦热模型，揭示了冰面滑溜性的起源：摩擦加热导致接触面温度升高至熔点附近，而非仅靠初始润滑膜形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 冰的滑溜性起源长期困扰科学界，需要从微观机制到宏观现象的系统性解释，以解决传统纳米尺度模拟无法准确捕捉速度依赖性的问题。

Method: 采用第一性原理（first principles）进行冰-玻璃（非晶二氧化硅）纳米尺度摩擦模拟，并通过摩擦加热模型（frictional heating model）将结果升级至宏观尺度。

Result: 纳米尺度模拟单独无法准确描述冰摩擦的速度依赖性，导致摩擦系数高估；考虑摩擦加热后，接触温度在速度超过0.1 m/s、位移1毫米时即接近熔点，与广泛速度范围内的实验数据高度吻合。

Conclusion: 冰的最终滑溜性取决于摩擦加热效应，支持Bowden和Hughes（1939）的理论但无需涉及熔化过程；初始润滑膜形成可能无需加热，但滑溜性的关键机制是摩擦导致的温度升高。

Abstract: The origin of ice's slipperiness has long puzzled scientists. To resolve this question, we simulate ice- glass (amorphous silica) friction at the nanoscale from first principles and upscale to the macroscale using a frictional heating model. We find that nanoscale simulations alone cannot capture the correct velocity dependence of ice friction, resulting in an overestimated coefficient of friction. By properly accounting for frictional heating, we find a strong increase in contact temperature toward the melting point, even under modest motion of 1 millimeter with velocities above 0.1 m/s, yielding excellent agreement with experimental friction data across a wide range of velocities. While the initial formation of a lubricating film on ice may occur without heating, the ultimate slipperiness of ice hinges on frictional heating, as proposed by Bowden and Hughes in 1939, but without incorporating melting.

Abstract: Antiferromagnetic (AFM) materials are considered as promising building blocks of novel data storage devices, still, detecting and manipulating AFM domains have remained challenging. Here, we demonstrate that the two antiphase domains of the magnetoelectric antiferromagnet LiCoPO$_4$ can be distinguished by their light absorption difference. Using visible and infrared spectroscopy, we observed spontaneous non-reciprocal absorption, also termed as directional dichroism, at the crystal field excitations of Co$^{2+}$ ions coordinated by distorted oxygen octahedra. This absorption contrast is particularly pronounced near the telecommunication wavelength of 1550 nm. These findings allowed us to image the AFM domains in LiCoPO$_4$ using a simple transmission light microscopy setup. Our findings suggest that optical magnetoelectric effects offer promising routes for probing the AFM order parameter in non-centrosymmetric transition metal compounds.

### [84] [High-pressure phase stability and superconductivity in La-Zr-H hydrides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11590)

Abstract: Hydrogen-rich ternary hydrides are promising candidates for high-Tc superconductivity at megabar pressures, yet their chemical space is vast and largely unexplored. Combining evolutionary structure searches with first-principles calculations, we comprehensively investigate the La-Zr-H ternary system in the 150-300 GPa pressure range. Zero-point energy-corrected convex hull analysis identifies multiple stable superconducting phases, including R3m-Zr2H17 at 300 GPa and P6/mmm-LaZr2H24 at 200 GPa, both of which are thermodynamically and dynamically stable and exhibit strong electron-phonon coupling. Solution of the Eliashberg equations predicts high superconducting transition temperatures of Tc = 209 K for R3m-Zr2H17 at 300 GPa and Tc = 202 K for P6/mmm-LaZr2H24 at 200 GPa. In addition to these stable phases, we identify a high-symmetry metastable compound, P6m2-LaZrH18, which lies just 0.027 eV/atom above the convex hull yet remains dynamically stable and exhibits a high predicted Tc of 206 K at 300 GPa. Finally, a random- forest machine learning model, trained on diverse hydrides superconductivity data, reproduces these structure-property trends across predicted structures, enabling to identify potential hydrides with high predicted Tc for targeted follow-up calculations and future high-pressure experiments.

Accuracy and robustness are maintained across the entire heterogeneity spectrum. ### [88] [Shear-Coupled Grain Growth Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11690)
*Caihao Qiu,David J. Srolovitz,Gregory S. Rohrer,Jian Han,Marco Salvalaglio*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过连续介质建模和扩散界面模拟，揭示了晶界剪切耦合（shear coupling）对二维晶粒生长（grain growth）统计特征的影响。研究发现剪切耦合导致更不均匀、非等轴化的微观结构，内部应力（internal stress）显著改变晶粒生长动力学，高应力晶粒收缩更快，低应力晶粒生长更快。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶粒生长（grain growth）是多元晶材料微观结构演变的基本机制，晶界迁移常伴随剪切耦合（shear coupling）现象。近期研究表明，剪切耦合产生的内部应力（internal stress）对微观结构演变和晶粒生长路径具有决定性作用，但对其统计特征的详细表征仍不充分。

Method: 采用结合基本微观机制的晶界迁移连续介质建模（continuum modeling）和扩散界面模拟（diffuse-interface simulations），对存在晶界剪切耦合的二维晶粒生长统计特征进行详细表征。

Result: 引入剪切耦合产生比传统曲率驱动晶粒生长更不均匀、更少等轴化的微观结构，但其拓扑和几何特性与实验和原子尺度观察一致。随着晶粒生长，内部应力松弛；高应力晶粒收缩更快，低应力晶粒生长更快于其他晶粒。

Conclusion: 内部应力作为晶粒生长的固有特征，深刻改变了晶粒生长微观结构和动力学的基本特性，这一发现与实验和原子尺度模拟结果一致，强调了内部应力在晶粒生长过程中的关键作用。

Abstract: Grain growth (GG), driven by grain boundary (GB) migration, is a fundamental mechanism of microstructural evolution in polycrystalline materials. GB migration is frequently accompanied by a relative shear displacement of grains meeting at GBs, a phenomenon known as shear coupling. This coupling induces internal stresses within the microstructure, which recent studies have shown to play a decisive role in dictating the evolution of microstructure and GG pathways. This work provides a detailed characterization of the statistical features of two-dimensional GG in the presence of GB shear coupling through continuum modeling of GB migration that incorporates fundamental microscopic mechanisms and diffuse-interface simulations. We demonstrate that incorporating shear coupling produces a more heterogeneous, less equiaxed microstructure than conventional curvature-driven GG, while yielding topological and geometric properties consistent with experimental and atomistic observations. We further demonstrate that as grain grows, internal stress relaxes. Highly stressed grains shrink faster, and lightly stressed grains grow faster than other grains. These findings demonstrate that internal stress, an intrinsic feature of GG, profoundly changes essential features of GG microstructure and kinetics, consistent with experiments and atomic-scale simulations.

### [89] [Melting of thin silicon films: a molecular dynamics study with two machine learning potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11722)
*Yu. D. Fomin,E. N. Tsiok,V. N. Ryzhov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过分子动力学模拟，使用SNAP和GAP两种机器学习势能函数，分析了硅烯（silicene）和薄硅膜的热稳定性。研究发现硅烯在500 K时结构失稳，分解温度随膜厚增加而升高，在约28层时达到饱和（对应SNAP模型的体相熔点1380 K）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用分子动力学（molecular dynamics）方法，使用两种机器学习势能函数：SNAP（spectral neighbor analysis potential）和GAP（Gaussian approximation potential）。对于SNAP势能函数，研究了从单层硅烯到36层薄膜的系统，分析其热分解行为。

Result: 硅烯在500 K时失去结构稳定性；分解温度随膜厚增加而升高，在约28层时达到饱和，对应SNAP模型的体相熔点1380 K。8层以下的薄膜表现出两相共存（two-phase coexistence）的分解模式，而更厚的薄膜则经历表面熔化（surface melting）后完全坍塌为液态。GAP势能函数虽然对体相硅更准确，但无法描述气相：使用GAP建模的硅烯会分解为一系列小团簇（small clusters）。

Abstract: Thermal stability of silicene and thin silicon films is studied by molecular dynamics using two machine-learning potentials, SNAP and GAP. For SNAP potential, systems ranging from a single silicene layer to films of 36 layers are considered. Silicene is found to lose its structure at 500 K. The decomposition temperature increases with film thikness and reaches saturation at about 28 layers, corresponding to the bulk melting point of the SNAP model (1380 K). Thin films up to 8 layers exibit two-phase coexistence upon decomposition, while thicker films undergo surface melting followed by complete collapse into the liquid state. The GAP potential, although more accurate for bulk silicon, fails to describe the gas phase: silicene modelled with GAP decomposes into a set of small clusters. The results are compared with earlier data for the Stillinger-Weber potential.

### [90] [First-principles insights into the optoelectronic and thermoelectric properties of X3NbY4(X= Cu, Ag, Au; Y=S, Se, Te) sulvanite compounds for energy applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11733)
*Sadeya Sabnam Emo,Md. Sharear Aman,Md. Abdur Rashid,Jaker Hossain*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究采用密度泛函理论（DFT）下的全势线性缀加平面波（FP-LAPW）方法，系统研究了X3NbY4（X=Cu, Ag, Au; Y=S, Se, Te）硫钒矿型硫族化合物的结构、电子、光学和输运性质，发现这些材料在光电子和热电器件中具有应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索X3NbY4硫钒矿型硫族化合物的物理性质，评估其在光电子和热电应用中的潜力。通过系统分析不同元素组合对材料性能的影响，为新型功能材料的设计提供理论指导。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）框架下的全势线性缀加平面波（Full Potential Linear Augmented Plane wave, FP-LAPW）方法进行计算。使用PBE-GGA和TB-mBJ两种泛函进行电子结构分析，并计算了弹性性质、声子色散曲线、光学性质（介电函数、吸收系数、折射率、能量损失函数）以及热电参数（塞贝克系数、热导率、电导率、功率因子和ZT值）。

Result: 结构计算与同族化合物结果一致。电子能带显示间接带隙结构，PBE-GGA泛函下带隙为1.65-0.50 eV，TB-mBJ泛函下为1.80-1.18 eV，确认为半导体材料。态密度分析表明，S-Se-Te和Cu-Ag-Au原子替换导致价带顶（VBM）上移和导带底（CBM）下移，从而减小带隙。弹性计算显示Cu基材料呈脆性，而Ag和Au基材料呈延性。声子色散曲线证实材料动态稳定。光学性质中吸收系数高达10^5 cm^-1，表明在光电子应用中具有吸引力。热电参数分析进一步支持了其在热电器件中的应用潜力。

Conclusion: X3NbY4硫钒矿型硫族化合物在结构、电子、光学和输运性质上表现出优异特性，特别是高吸收系数和可调带隙，使其成为光电子和热电器件的潜在候选材料。不同元素组合可调控材料性能，为功能材料设计提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The structural, electronic, optical and transport properties of X3NbY4(X= Cu, Ag, Au; Y=S, Se, Te) sulvanite chalcogenides materials have been investigated using the Full Potential Linear Augmented Plane wave (FP-LAPW) within the density functional theory (DFT). The calculated structural information of X3NbY4 compounds is consistent with reported results of the same family compounds. The electronic band diagram exhibit indirect type band structures with bandgap value in the range of Eg 1.65- 0.50 eV using PBE-GGA functional and 1.80 eV-1.18 eV using TB-mBJ functional which indicates that these are semiconductor materials. The density of states (DOS) shows that the amount of bandgap decreases owing to move of valence band maximum (VBM) to the high energy level whereas the conduction band minimum (CBM) to the low energy level owing to the replacement of S-S-Te and Cu-Ag-Au atoms. The hybridized orbital by X-d, Nb-d and Y-p atomic orbitals dominate the VBM while hybridized by Nb-d and Y-p atomic orbitals mainly contribute the CBM. The elastic calculations exhibit that Cu-based materials have brittleness nature whereas Ag- and Au-based compounds are ductile nature. Furthermore, the phonon dispersion curves probes that these X3NbY4 compounds are dynamically stable. However, the calculated optical properties: dielectric function, absorption coefficient, refractive index, and energy loss function; specifically, the higher value of absorption coefficient (105 cm-1) indicates that these materials are attractive candidates in optoelectronics applications. Finally, thermoelectric parameters such as Seebeck coefficient, thermal conductivity, electrical conductivity, power factor (P.F) and ZT value of these compounds have also been investigated. Overall, the finding explores that these materials are potential candidates for the applications in optoelectronic and thermoelectric devices.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The cold source field-effect transistor (CSFET) is promising for reducing power dissipation in integrated circuits by engineering the density of states at the injecting source. ### [93] [Origin and Propagation of Spin-orbit Torques in Pt/Co/Cu/NiFe/Capping Multilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11843)
*Yuming Bai,Rulin Tian,Yue Zhang,Tao Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过NiFe厚度依赖的自旋轨道矩（SOT）效率分析，阐明了复杂多层结构中阻尼型（DL）和场型（FL）SOT的起源与传播特性。研究发现DL-SOT主要受界面自旋吸收支配，而FL-SOT表现出更长的自旋退相干长度，揭示了两种转矩在界面自旋输运中的不同机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋轨道矩（spin-orbit torque, SOT）为实现低功耗自旋电子器件提供了有效途径，但复杂多层结构中阻尼型（damping-like, DL）和场型（field-like, FL）SOT的起源与传播机制尚不明确。本研究旨在澄清这些基本问题，为超薄金属异质结构中界面自旋轨道功能的工程化设计提供指导。

Method: 采用Ta/Pt/Co/Cu/NiFe/Cu/Capping多层结构（Capping为Pt、Al和SiO2），利用自旋旋转几何构型使垂直磁化的Pt/Co/Cu堆栈作为自旋源。通过引入样品面积归一化磁矩m = mNiFe/S来区分体相和界面贡献，结合平面霍尔（planar Hall）和极向磁光克尔效应（polar MOKE）测量实现SOT的明确分离。

Result: DL-SOT遵循近似线性的1/m标度关系，表明Cu/NiFe界面存在快速自旋吸收，但在Pt和Al覆盖层样品中当1/m趋近零时表现出有限beta_SOT，揭示了Cu/Pt和Cu/Al界面的额外界面自旋电流贡献。FL-SOT显著偏离1/m标度，展现出约1.7 nm的更长自旋退相干长度，暗示其在NiFe中的扩展传播特性。

Conclusion: 研究阐明了DL和FL转矩在复杂多层结构中的不同起源与传播特性：DL-SOT主要受界面自旋吸收控制，而FL-SOT表现出更长的自旋退相干长度和扩展传播行为。这些发现为设计具有特定界面自旋轨道功能的超薄金属异质结构提供了重要指导原则。

Abstract: Spin-orbit torque (SOT) enables efficient current-driven control of magnetization, offering a promising pathway toward low-power spintronic devices. However, the origin and propagation of both damping-like (DL) and field-like (FL) SOTs in complex multilayers remain unclear. Here, we investigate NiFe thickness-dependent SOT efficiencies in Ta/Pt/Co/Cu/NiFe/Cu/Capping multilayers (x = 15 nm; Capping = Pt, Al, and SiO2). By employing a spin rotation geometry, the perpendicularly magnetized Pt/Co/Cu stacks serve as a spin source introducing unconventional spin polarization orthogonal to the Oersted field, eliminating its contribution and enabling unambiguous separation of SOTs using planar Hall and polar MOKE measurements. To distinguish bulk and interfacial contributions, we introduce a sample-area-normalized moment m = mNiFe/S, accounting for thickness-dependent magnetization and eliminating uncertainties arising from nominal thickness scaling and magnetic dead layers. We find that DL-SOT follows nearly linear 1/m scaling, consistent with rapid spin absorption at the Cu/NiFe interface but exhibits finite beta_SOT when 1/m approaches zero in both Pt- and Al-capped samples, indicating additional interfacial spin-current contributions at Cu/Pt and Cu/Al interfaces. In contrast, SiO2-capped samples show negligible interfacial contributions. Furthermore, FL-SOT deviates markedly from 1/m scaling and exhibits a significantly longer spin dephasing length (about 1.7 nm) compared to DL-SOT, implying extended propagation across NiFe. Comparative capping-layer studies further corroborate this behavior through interface-dependent spin transport. Our findings clarify the origin and distinct propagation characteristics of DL and FL torques, providing guidelines for engineering interfacial spin-orbit functionalities in ultrathin metallic heterostructures.

</details>


### [94] [Emergence of polar monoclinic phase in heterohalogen substituted CsGeX$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11844)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理方法（first-principles methods）研究CsGeX₃材料，在X位点进行2:1构型的异卤素取代。通过软模特征向量（soft mode eigenvectors）沿不同方向的原子位移生成结构，并通过动力学矩阵（dynamical matrix）的能量学确认单斜相。

Result: 异卤素取代导致更强的八面体环境变化，产生室温下的极性单斜相（polar monoclinic phase）。极化沿[101]方向，比原始材料增加10-15%。价带自旋分裂能（spin-splitting energy）为25-250 meV，导带为9-80 meV，并表现出与极化方向耦合的Rashba和持久自旋织构（persistent spin textures）。

Conclusion: CsGeX₃材料的半导体和自旋极化特性，结合其增强的铁电性和自旋织构，使其成为Datta-Das自旋晶体管（Datta-Das spin transistors）的有力候选材料。对称性相关的k·p哈密顿量（k.p Hamiltonian）参数揭示了自旋分裂强度和自旋织构性质。

Abstract: The occurrence of ferroelectricity in inorganic germanium-based halide perovskites has provided an alternative to oxide counterparts. Using first-principles methods, we have studied CsGeX$_3$ materials with heterohalogen substitution at the X site in a 2:1 configuration. Structurally, such variation alters the octahedral environment more strongly than in pristine materials, giving rise to a polar monoclinic phase at room temperature. The occurrence of the monoclinic phase is also confirmed through the energetics of structures generated by the displacements of atoms in accordance with soft mode eigenvectors of the dynamical matrix along various directions. In the chemically tuned phase, the polarization is along [101] and increases by 10-15\% compared to pristine ones. The electronic structure analysis reveals that spin-splitting energy ranges from 25 to 250 meV in the valence band and from 9 to 80 meV in the conduction band in chemically tuned structures. In addition, these structures exhibit Rashba and persistent spin textures, which are coupled to the polarization direction. The parameters of the symmetry-dependent \textbf{k.p } Hamiltonian provide insights into the strength of spin-splitting and the nature of spin-texture. The semiconducting and spin-polarized nature of CsGeX$_3$ materials makes them strong candidates for Datta-Das spin transistors.

### [95] [Symmetry-Driven Floquet Engineering in Multivalley SnS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11878)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用时间、偏振和角度分辨的极紫外光电子能谱（time-, polarization-, and angle-resolved extreme ultraviolet photoemission spectroscopy）、群论分析（group-theory analysis）以及含时密度泛函理论（time-dependent density functional theory）相结合的方法，在块体多谷半导体SnS中研究对称性驱动的Floquet工程。

Result: 材料固有对称性导致平衡能带和光诱导Floquet态均表现出显著的对称性驱动光电子选择定则。通过驱动光偏振与晶体轴相对取向的调控，实现了对Floquet-Bloch态宇称的确定性控制，能够选择性地相对于平衡价带和导带进行宇称反转。对称性驱动的宇称工程还实现了偏振和谷选择性的能带重整化（band renormalization）。

Conclusion: 这些发现推进了对波函数对称性工程指导原则的理解，为使用定制电磁场选择性控制量子材料中电子态的宇称和重整化提供了途径。

Abstract: Coherent interactions between time-periodic electromagnetic fields and materials offer a powerful platform for engineering light-matter hybrid Floquet states with tailored functionalities. In particular, the ability to manipulate the wavefunction symmetry of such Floquet states has recently emerged as a new frontier in the field of nonequilibrium control of quantum materials. Here, we investigate symmetry-driven Floquet engineering in bulk multivalley semiconductor tin sulfide (SnS) using time-, polarization-, and angle-resolved extreme ultraviolet photoemission spectroscopy, group-theory analysis, and time-dependent density functional theory. We demonstrate that the material's inherent symmetry gives rise to pronounced symmetry-driven photoemission selection rules for both equilibrium bands and light-induced Floquet states, which we probed through nonequilibrium linear dichroism in extreme ultraviolet photoemission. By leveraging the interplay between crystal and driving-light symmetry, we establish deterministic control over the parity of Floquet--Bloch states. Indeed, we show that the symmetry of Floquet--Bloch states can be fully controlled by the relative alignment between the drive polarization and the crystal axes, enabling selective parity inversion with respect to the equilibrium valence and conduction bands. Furthermore, we show that symmetry-driven parity engineering allows for polarization- and valley-selective band renormalization. These findings advance the understanding of guiding principles for wavefunction symmetry engineering, providing pathways for selectively controlling both the parity and renormalization of electronic states in quantum materials using tailored electromagnetic fields.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 综合结果表明，通过生物胶结的方解石沉淀会产生各向异性内部应变和明显的亚畴结构。这些特征能够影响键合完整性和宏观尺度上的荷载传递。

Conclusion: 生物胶结过程中形成的方解石具有复杂的内部应变和亚结构特征，这些微观特征对宏观力学性能具有重要影响，为理解生物胶结材料的力学行为提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Bio-cementation uses bacterially induced calcite to bind sand grains, offering a low-carbon approach to soil stabilization. However, the 3D morphology, orientation texture, and internal strain states of individual calcite bonds remain insufficiently characterized. Here, we combine computed micro-tomography, 3D X-ray Diffraction (3DXRD), and Dark-Field X-ray Microscopy (DFXM) to nondestructively characterize grain morphology, crystallographic orientation, and both type II (intergranular) and type III (intragranular) elastic strains in calcite formed at sand-sand contacts during bio-cementation. Tomography establishes the sample morphology and the cemented contact architecture; 3DXRD provides grain-averaged orientation and strain states; and DFXM resolves sub-grain misorientations and localized strain concentrations generated during growth with 100 nm resolution. The combined results show that calcite precipitation through bio-cementation produces anisotropic internal strain and distinct sub-domain structures that can influence bond integrity and load transfer at the macroscopic scale.

With defect parameters obtained from ab initio calculations as input, RASP enables accurate simulation of threshold voltage shifts caused by defects. Abstract: In multiferroics, new physical responses and functionalities emerge when symmetry-distinct order parameters couple. In sub-domain sized devices with achiral geometry, we demonstrate that nonreciprocal transport serves as a symmetry-based probe of the global spin chirality, co-aligned with the strong topological AHE of the system. In Co$_{1/3}$TaS$_2$ the topological Hall state inherits a large resistance anomaly via chiral-nematic coupling, thus our results showcase how hybrid magnetic orders can achieve advanced functionalities by merging symmetry-forbidden material responses.

With the aim of providing insights on how to chemically control spin-phonon relaxation, we here present a full ab initio study of spin-phonon dynamics for three Yb(III) molecules exhibiting minimal chemical differences, yet quantitatively different spin relaxation times. Results show that low-temperature relaxation is governed by Raman processes triggered by a small group of largely delocalized low-energy phonons. Applied pressure reversibly tunes CrNbSe$_5$ between semiconducting and semimetallic states, enabling access to low- and high-carrier electronic regimes through direct modulation of metal-chalcogen bonding. High-pressure single-crystal X-ray diffraction directly resolves the evolution of Cr-Se and Nb-Se bond distances, coordination polyhedra, and connectivity, revealing a fully reversible semimetal-semiconductor-semimetal transition driven by gradual yet cooperative bond rearrangements within a preserved crystallographic symmetry. In contrast to chemical substitution, which irreversibly alters composition and introduces disorder, pressure acts as a clean, continuous control parameter that reshapes the bonding landscape without disrupting structural symmetry. These results establish CrNbSe$_5$ as a model system for electronically driven phase switching via tunable chemical bonding, highlighting iso-symmetric bond reorganization as a powerful design principle for pressure-controlled electronic and spintronic functionalities.

### [104] [Proof-Carrying Materials: Falsifiable Safety Certificates for Machine-Learned Interatomic Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12183)

Method: 提出Proof-Carrying Materials (PCM)框架，包含三个阶段：在成分空间进行对抗性证伪（adversarial falsification）、使用95%置信区间进行自举包络精炼（bootstrap envelope refinement），以及Lean 4形式化认证。该方法对CHGNet、TensorNet和MACE等架构进行审计，并通过独立Quantum ESPRESSO验证。

Result: PCM框架显著提升了材料发现的可靠性：在热电材料筛选案例中，PCM审计的协议发现了62个被单MLIP筛选漏掉的额外稳定材料，将发现率提升了25%。基于PCM发现特征训练的风险模型在未见材料上表现出良好的预测性能（AUC-ROC = 0.938 ± 0.004）。

Conclusion: PCM框架通过系统性的可靠性验证方法，有效解决了MLIPs在材料筛选中缺乏形式化保证的问题，显著提升了稳定材料的发现率，并为跨架构的可靠性评估提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Machine-learned interatomic potentials (MLIPs) are deployed for high-throughput materials screening without formal reliability guarantees. We show that a single MLIP used as a stability filter misses 93% of density functional theory (DFT)-stable materials (recall 0.07) on a 25,000-material benchmark. ### [105] [A blended approach for evolving phase fields using peridynamics: Cyclic loading in quasi-brittle fracture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12210)

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有准脆性材料损伤断裂模型需要同时考虑不可逆塑性变形和随损伤软化的弹性模量效应，传统方法难以统一描述这些复杂耦合行为。

Method: 采用两点历史相关相场（two-point history-dependent phase field）方法，结合牛顿第二定律描述变形演化，通过非局部本构定律实现空间和时间上的非局部性。应变采用弹性应变与不可逆应变的加法分解，应力-应变行为基于强度包络和考虑损伤塑性的卸载定律族描述。

Result: 理论满足能量平衡和热力学第二定律的正能耗散率要求，平直裂纹的断裂能量可直接从模型恢复为能量释放率与裂纹面积的乘积，且该公式与非局部长度尺度无关。数值模拟显示与混凝土三点弯曲试验的滞回和损伤效应具有定量和定性一致性。

Abstract: A field theory is presented for predicting damage and fracture in quasi brittle materials incorporating effects of irreversible (plastic) deformation as well as elastic moduli that soften with damage. The new observation made here is that material degradation models consistent with plastic dissipation can be described by a two-point history-dependent phase field. This approach blends a two-point phase field with the deformation evolving according to Newton's second law by way of a nonlocal constitutive law. Here the nonlocality is in both space and time. The strain is given by an additive decomposition of elastic strain and irreversible strain. The stress-strain behavior is described by a strength envelope and a family of unloading laws based on damage and plasticity with elastic moduli that degrade in coordination with the accumulation of irreversible strain. The material displacement field is uniquely determined by the initial boundary value problem. The theory satisfies energy balance, with positive energy dissipation rate in accordance with the laws of thermodynamics. The fracture energy of flat cracks is recovered directly from the model and is the product of energy release rate and the crack area, moreover this formula is independent of the length scale of non-locality. The formulation delivers a mesh free method for predicting crack patterns and simulations show quantitative and qualitative agreement with experiments, including hysteresis and damage associated with three-point bending tests on concrete and size effects for quasi-brittle materials.
