*Huaiyu Hugo Wang,Ernesto Flores,Jade Stanton,Gal Orenstein,Peter R. Miedaner,Laura Foglia,Maya Martinez,David A. Reis,Roman Mankowsky,Mathias Sander,Henrik Lemke,Serhane Zerdane,Keith A. Nelson,Mariano Trigo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过结合机械应变、超快激光脉冲和X射线散射技术，在钛酸锶（SrTiO₃）中发现了一种新的极性态，其特征是纳米波长的独特极性振动，而非传统的均匀铁电性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子材料中的隐藏相（hidden phases）存在于平衡相图之外，具有变革性潜力，但由于常与已知态相似而难以识别。钛酸锶（SrTiO₃）冷却时表现出铁电性特征却从未形成该有序态，这体现了识别隐藏相的挑战。

Method: 研究结合了机械应变（mechanical strain）、超快激光脉冲（ultrafast laser pulses）和X射线散射（x-ray scattering）技术，通过探测有限动量下的集体激发来识别隐藏相。

Result: 在钛酸锶中发现了一种新的极性态，其特征是纳米波长的独特极性振动，表明应变稳定了一个以纳米尺度极化调制为特征的隐藏态，而非传统的均匀铁电性（homogeneous ferroelectricity）。

Conclusion: 这一发现可能为量子顺电性（quantum paraelectricity）提供替代解释，并证明探测有限动量下的集体激发对于识别量子材料中的隐藏相至关重要。

Abstract: Hidden phases of quantum materials are collective states that exist outside the equilibrium phase diagram and can host exotic properties with transformative potential. However, because they can often mimic known states, identifying them remains challenging. Strontium titanate (SrTiO3) epitomizes this challenge: upon cooling, it displays signatures of ferroelectricity yet never develops this order. We combined mechanical strain with ultrafast laser pulses and x-ray scattering to discover a new polar state in SrTiO3 that is distinct from ferroelectricity. Its signature are distinctive polar vibrations with nanometer wavelengths. This reveals that strain stabilizes a hidden state characterized by a nanoscale polarization modulation rather than conventional homogeneous ferroelectricity. Our findings may offer an alternative explanation for quantum paraelectricity and demonstrate that probing collective excitations at finite momentum is essential for identifying hidden phases in quantum materials.

</details>


### [107] [Emergent Anomalous Hall Effect from Surface States in the Altermagnet MnTe Thin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12259)
*Yufei Zhao,Saswata Mandal,Chao-Xing Liu,Binghai Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过分离体相和表面贡献，解决了MnTe薄膜中反常霍尔效应（AHE）的符号冲突和厚度无关性争议，建立了通过界面设计解释和调控反铁磁薄膜AHE响应的微观框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对原型反铁磁体（altermagnet）MnTe薄膜中反常霍尔效应（AHE）测量结果存在的矛盾现象，包括相反符号和厚度无关的电阻率，需要澄清这些差异的来源。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和基于对称性的有效模型（symmetry-based effective models），分离不同晶体终端（crystal terminations）的体相和表面贡献，并考虑实际界面化学（realistic interfacial chemistry）。

Result: 尽管体相具有特征性的g波费米面（g-wave Fermi surface），但在体相能隙内的表面态获得类铁磁自旋极化，并在实验相关费米能级主导AHE。表面磁化遵循表面自旋亚晶格，但AHE由给定终端的体相Néel序（bulk Néel order）唯一决定。Te覆盖层可相对于InP衬底反转表面AHE符号。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了通过界面设计解释和调控反铁磁薄膜中反常霍尔效应响应的微观框架（microscopic framework），揭示了体相和表面贡献都与微小但有限的垂直轨道磁化密切相关。

Abstract: Transport measurements on thin films of the prototypical altermagnet MnTe have reported conflicting phenomena of anomalous Hall effects (AHE), including opposite signs and thickness-independent resistivity. Here we resolve these discrepancies by separating bulk and surface contributions to the AHE for different crystal terminations. Using first-principles calculations and symmetry-based effective models, we show that although the bulk hosts a characteristic $g$-wave Fermi surface, surface states within the bulk gap acquire a ferromagnet-like spin polarization and dominate the AHE at experimentally relevant Fermi energies. While the surface magnetization follows the surface spin sublattice, the resulting AHE is uniquely determined by the bulk Néel order for a given termination. Both bulk and surface contributions are closely linked to a small but finite out-of-plane orbital magnetization. Incorporating realistic interfacial chemistry further reveals that a Te capping layer can reverse the surface AHE sign relative to that on an InP substrate. Our results establish a microscopic framework for interpreting and engineering AHE responses in altermagnetic thin films through interface design.

### [108] [Very long-term relaxation of harmonic 1D self-gravitating systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11238)
*Kerwann Tep,Jean-Baptiste Fouvry,Christophe Pichon*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 一维自引力系统在简谐势中表现出二次N标度弛豫时间，而在非简并系统中为线性标度，部分简并系统在低N时显示二次标度，高N时过渡到线性标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一维自引力系统在简谐势（harmonic potential）中的弛豫动力学，其中所有粒子具有相同的平均轨道频率，导致朗道（Landau）和巴列斯库-勒纳（Balescu-Lenard）理论失效。该研究旨在理解频率简并（degenerate frequency）系统的弛豫机制。

Method: 使用精确的碰撞驱动一维积分器（exact collision-driven 1D integrator），数值研究一维简谐自引力系统的自洽弛豫（self-consistent relaxation）。通过改变系统简并程度和径向支撑（radial support）来探索不同动力学机制。

Result: 简谐系统的弛豫时间随粒子数N呈二次方增长；部分简并系统在低N时显示二次标度，但在高N时过渡到线性标度；完全非简并但具有有限径向支撑的系统弛豫时间与N呈线性关系，但比例系数比非紧致系统大得多。

Conclusion: 频率简并显著改变一维自引力系统的弛豫动力学，导致弛豫时间标度从线性变为二次方。该研究为理解矮星系中心等密度核（density cores）的动力学提供了新线索。

Abstract: One-dimensional self-gravitating systems admit genuine thermodynamical equilibria. For systems with strictly monotonic orbital frequency profile, the Landau and Balescu-Lenard theories predict a relaxation time scaling linearly with the number of particles, $N$, in agreement with simulations. Yet, these theories become ill-posed for degenerate frequency profiles, as is the case in the harmonic potential, where all particles share the exact same mean orbital frequency. Using an exact collision-driven 1D integrator, we investigate numerically the self-consistent relaxation of 1D harmonic self-gravitating systems. We show that harmonic systems relax on a timescale that grows quadratically with $N$. We show that systems that are only partially degenerate display the same quadratic scaling for low $N$, but transition to the linear, non-degenerate behaviour for larger $N$. The larger the fraction of degenerate orbits, the larger the value of $N$ at which this transition of dynamical regime occurs. Finally, we explore the dynamics of fully non-degenerate systems, albeit with finite radial support: we confirm that their relaxation time scales linearly with $N$, though with a substantially larger prefactor than in non-compact systems. Astrophysically, this investigation should offer some new clues on the dynamics of density cores, as in the center of dwarf galaxies.

</details>

### [109] [Cut and project schemes in the Poincaré disc: From cocompact Fuchsian groups to chaotic Delone sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11311)
*Richard A. Howat,Tony Samuel,Ayşe Yıltekin-Karataş*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究基于双曲空间（hyperbolic space）中紧余Fuchsian群（cocompact Fuchsian groups）的切割投影方案（cut and project scheme），证明所得集合是混沌Delone集（chaotic Delone set），其瓦片长度集（tile lengths）可数无限，并将结果应用于三角形群（triangle groups）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在回应Davies等人提出的问题：通过开发新的切割投影模型（cut and project models），其中晶格非方形或曲线非线性，能否生成性能更好的梯度超材料（graded metamaterials）？研究聚焦于双曲空间（hyperbolic space）中紧余Fuchsian群（cocompact Fuchsian groups）的自然构造方案。

Method: 采用基于庞加莱圆盘模型（Poincaré disc model）中紧余Fuchsian群作用的切割投影方案，分析群基本域（fundamental domain）——双曲多边形（hyperbolic polygon）的条件，确保所得切割投影集为混沌Delone集，并研究其瓦片长度集（tile lengths）的性质。

Result: 建立了基本域条件使所得切割投影集S⊂ℝ成为混沌Delone集，证明其瓦片长度集ℒ_S可数无限，并将结果应用于紧余Fuchsian三角形群（cocompact Fuchsian triangle groups），验证所得切割投影集具有混沌Delone性质。

Conclusion: 研究证实了基于双曲空间Fuchsian群的切割投影方案能产生混沌Delone集，扩展了López等人的工作，为梯度超材料设计提供了新的数学框架和构造方法。

Abstract: A question raised by Davies et al [Phys. Rev. Lett. 131, 2023] is: "Can developing new cut and project models, where the lattice is not square or the curve is non-linear, generate better performing graded metamaterials?" In this article, we study a natural construction of such a cut and project scheme, namely, cut and project schemes in relation to cocompact Fuchsian groups acting on the Poincaré disc model of hyperbolic space. We present a condition on the fundamental domain (a hyperbolic polygon) of the group so that the resulting cut and project set $S \subset \mathbb{R}$ is a chaotic Delone set. We also investigate the set of tile lengths of $S$, namely $\mathcal{L}_{S} = \{ z - y : z,y \in S, \, z > y \; \text{and} \; (y,z) \cap S = \emptyset \}$, and show that this set is countably infinite. Finally, we apply our results to cocompact Fuchsian triangle groups and show that the resulting cut and project sets are chaotic Delone, complementing and extending the work of López et al. [Discrete Contin. Dyn. Syst. 41, 2021].

</details>

### [110] [Pattern stability in reaction-diffusion systems depends on path entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11192)
*Eric R. Heller,David T. Limmer*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种非平衡瞬子框架（nonequilibrium instanton framework），用于高效计算远离热力学平衡的反应扩散系统中亚稳态空间图案之间的转变速率。该框架通过单条最优转变路径及其涨落实现计算，并揭示了路径空间有效熵（effective entropy in path space）在有限粒子数下能定性改变图案稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 远离热力学平衡的反应扩散系统（reaction-diffusion systems）可支持多种持久空间图案，但这些亚稳态相（metastable phases）的稳定性由连接它们的转变路径决定，而非热力学因素。有限粒子数下的内在随机性（intrinsic stochasticity）导致图案间的稀有转变，使得连续平均场描述不足，而精确随机模拟在空间扩展系统中计算成本过高。

Method: 研究开发了一种非平衡瞬子框架，能够从单条最优转变路径（optimal transition path）及其涨落高效计算亚稳态图案间的转变速率。该理论框架通过分析路径空间的有效熵来研究有限粒子数下的稳定性变化。

Result: 研究表明，路径空间的有效熵能通过增加亚稳态图案的退出速率（exit rates）来定性改变有限粒子数下的稳定性。通过对不同复杂度的模型进行研究，该工作确立了路径熵（path entropy）作为非平衡图案形成的关键组织原则（organizing principle）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立的非平衡瞬子框架为计算远离平衡系统中亚稳态图案间的转变速率提供了高效方法，并证明路径熵是非平衡图案形成的重要组织原则，能够显著影响有限粒子数下的系统稳定性。

Abstract: Reaction-diffusion systems driven far from thermodynamic equilibrium through the injection of energy can support multiple distinct spatial patterns that persist as long-lived dynamical phases. The stability of these metastable phases is not determined by thermodynamics, but by the transition paths connecting them. At finite particle numbers, intrinsic stochasticity induces rare transitions between competing patterns, rendering continuum mean-field descriptions insufficient, while exact stochastic simulations become computationally prohibitive in spatially extended systems. Here, we develop a nonequilibrium instanton framework that enables efficient computation of transition rates between metastable patterns from a single optimal transition path and its fluctuations. Using this theoretical framework, we show that an effective entropy in path space can qualitatively alter stability at finite particle numbers by increasing the exit rates of metastable patterns. By studying models of varying complexity, this work establishes path entropy as a key organizing principle for nonequilibrium pattern formation.

</details>


### [111] [What is a minimum work transition in stochastic thermodynamics?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11995)
*Paolo Muratore-Ginanneschi,Julia Sanders*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究重新评估了经典随机有限时间热力学中最小功转变的概念，表明最小功优化控制问题的良定义表述必须考虑控制协议的速度限制，这具有重要的定性影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于重新评估经典随机有限时间热力学（classical stochastic finite-time thermodynamics）中最小功转变的概念，特别关注当系统动力学由扩散过程（diffusion process）建模时的情况。

Method: 研究方法基于扩散过程建模，通过分析最优控制问题（optimal control problem）的良定义表述，特别强调必须考虑控制协议（control protocols）的速度限制（speed limits）。

Result: 研究结果表明：1）速度限制的考虑允许区分最优快速工程平衡（optimal swift engineered equilibration）和最小功转变；2）当速度限制被移除时，只有由广义薛定谔桥（generalized Schrödinger bridges）指定的转变才具有一致的物理解释。

Conclusion: 该研究通过一个高斯移动陷阱中悬浮粒子的简单模型问题（levitating particle in a Gaussian moving trap）阐明了这些观点，强调了速度限制在最小功转变理论中的关键作用。

Abstract: We reassess the concept of transition at minimum work in classical stochastic finite-time thermodynamics, when the system dynamics is modelled by a diffusion process. We show that a well-posed formulation of the optimal control problem corresponding to the minimization of the mean work done on the system during a finite-time transition necessarily requires taking into account speed limits on control protocols. This fact has major qualitative consequences. First, it permits to discriminate between optimal swift engineered equilibration and transitions at minimum work. Second, it shows that in the limit when speed limits are removed, only transitions specified by generalized Schrödinger bridges admit a consistent physical interpretation. To illustrate these points, we focus on the simplest model problem: a levitating particle in a Gaussian moving trap.

</details>


### [112] [Unraveling anomalous relaxation effects in the thermodynamic limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11326)
*Emilio Pomares,Víctor Martín-Mayor,Antonio Lasanta,Gabriel Álvarez*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究解决了异常姆彭巴弛豫（anomalous Mpemba-like relaxations）理论中的两个核心问题：将其扩展到一维以上空间维度，并在热力学极限下建立一致的理论框架。通过研究外磁场作用下反铁磁伊辛模型（antiferromagnetic Ising model）的相变行为，揭示了弛豫过程中连续时间尺度谱的出现，并建立了与平衡态热力学量（如序参量磁化率）的理论联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在解决异常姆彭巴弛豫理论中的两个核心开放问题：将其扩展到一维以上空间维度，并在热力学极限下建立一致的理论描述框架。这些问题的解决对于理解复杂系统中的非平衡弛豫现象至关重要。

Method: 采用外磁场作用下的反铁磁伊辛模型（antiferromagnetic Ising model）作为理论框架，该模型具有丰富的相图，包含温度和磁场两个控制参数。通过理论分析结合蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）进行验证，并采用谱投影方法（spectral projector）分析最慢时间尺度。

Result: 研究发现，对于具有标准涨落的强度可观测量，单一主导指数弛豫的标准假设是不一致的；随着系统尺寸增大，会出现连续的时间尺度谱。在相变附近，最慢时间尺度的谱投影器可以用平衡态热力学量——亚稳态相序参量的磁化率（susceptibility）来有效表征。

Conclusion: 该理论框架能够对涉及温度和磁场同时变化的各种异常弛豫现象（包括直接和逆姆彭巴效应、冷却-加热不对称性、预冷诱导的更快加热等）提供定性和半定量预测。经过最小化后优化，可将理论指导的协议转化为完全最优协议，使异常弛豫现象以最显著形式呈现。

Abstract: We address two central open problems in the theory of anomalous Mpemba-like relaxations: their extension beyond one spatial dimension and their consistent formulation in the thermodynamic limit. Our framework is the antiferromagnetic Ising model on a square lattice under an externally applied magnetic field, which enables us to work in the presence of a phase transition. The rich phase diagram contains two control parameters: temperature and magnetic field. We demonstrate that the standard assumption of relaxation dominated by a single leading exponential is inconsistent for intensive observables exhibiting standard fluctuations. Instead, as the system size increases, a continuous spectrum of time scales emerges. Nevertheless, we make the ansatz that, in the vicinity of the phase transition, the spectral projector onto the slowest time scales can be effectively characterized in terms of an equilibrium thermodynamic quantity: the susceptibility associated with the order parameter of the metastable phase. Combined with the richness of the phase diagram, this ansatz yields qualitative and semi-quantitative predictions for optimal protocols leading to a variety of anomalous relaxation phenomena involving simultaneous variations of temperature and magnetic field. These include direct and inverse Mpemba effects, cooling-heating asymmetries, and faster heating induced by precooling. Careful Monte Carlo simulations validate our theoretical predictions. Furthermore, minimal post-optimization suffices to convert our analytically guided protocols into fully optimal ones that display anomalous relaxations in their most pronounced form.

</details>


### [113] [Time irreversibility and entropy production in non-Hermitian Model A field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11450)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用随机路径积分形式，执行受控的小噪声展开，计算熵产生率和涨落耗散定理违反；分析表明局域熵产生率完全由线性化朗之万方程的非厄米部分决定。

Conclusion: 研究结果为非厄米标量场理论中的时间反演对称性破缺提供了普适特征描述，所建立框架适用于分析非互易伊辛模型等粗粒化尺度系统。

Abstract: We develop a systematic framework to quantify irreversibility in scalar Model A field theories with a generic non-Hermitian term driving the dynamics. Using the stochastic path-integral formalism, we perform a controlled small-noise expansion, allowing the computation of the entropy production rate (EPR) and violations of the fluctuation-dissipation theorem (FDT). We show that the local EPR is entirely determined by the anti-Hermitian part of the linearised Langevin equation. Around steady states, the non-Hermitian component produces linear corrections to FDT violations and contributes quadratically to the EPR. As an illustration of the applicability of our approach, we analyse a minimal non-Hermitian extension of the Ginzburg-Landau $ψ^4$ theory describing a non-reciprocal Ising model at coarse-grained scales, for which we obtain explicit expressions of the local EPR, showing that it localises at interfaces in non-uniform states. Our results provide a general characterisation of TRS breaking in non-Hermitian scalar field theories.

### [114] [Third-order transitions in Ising and Potts models on Watts--Strogatz small-world networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11522)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究二维伊辛和波茨模型中的三阶相变现象，特别是在正则晶格和瓦茨-斯特罗加茨小世界网络（Watts-Strogatz small-world networks）拓扑结构下，这些相变的特征温度层次结构及其对网络重连概率的响应。

Method: 采用团簇观测量（cluster observables）追踪临界后边界重组（post-critical boundary reorganization）和临界前团簇破裂（pre-critical cluster breakup）。对于伊辛模型，通过宾德累积量交叉（Binder-cumulant crossings）和磁化率峰值（susceptibility peaks）独立校准临界温度；对于小世界网络上的波茨模型，则通过 $\mathrm d\langle P\rangle/\mathrm dT$ 的主临界峰值（dominant critical peak）操作性地识别临界温度。

Result: 在晶格和小世界拓扑结构中均发现稳健的温度排序 $T_{\mathrm{ind}}<T_c<T_{\mathrm{dep}}$。增加重连概率（rewiring probability）会使所有三个特征温度上移，并增强临界后相变（post-critical transition）的可见度。这种效应在波茨模型中尤为明显，其中基于周长的观测量（perimeter-based observables）对多态边界涨落（multistate boundary fluctuations）更为敏感。

Conclusion: 特征温度层次结构在不同拓扑结构和有限尺寸下的系统性持续存在，反驳了将这些特征解释为偶然的有限尺寸不规则性（incidental finite-size irregularities）的观点。相反，研究结果支持将其解释为真正的三阶相变，其结构可探测性（structural detectability）可通过网络拓扑结构得到增强。

Abstract: We study third-order transitions in the two-dimensional Ising and Potts model on regular lattices and Watts--Strogatz small-world networks. Cluster observables are used to track post-critical boundary reorganization and pre-critical cluster breakup. For the Ising model, the critical temperature $T_c$ is calibrated independently from Binder-cumulant crossings and susceptibility peaks, whereas for the Potts model on small-world networks it is identified operationally from the dominant critical peak of $\mathrm d\langle P\rangle/\mathrm dT$. The independent and dependent third-order transitions are identified from the isolated-spin peak and the post-critical structural extremum, respectively. For both lattice and small-world topologies, we find the robust ordering $T_{\mathrm{ind}}<T_c<T_{\mathrm{dep}}$. Increasing the rewiring probability shifts all three characteristic temperatures upward and enhances the visibility of the post-critical transition. The effect is especially clear in the Potts model, where perimeter-based observables are more sensitive to multistate boundary fluctuations. The systematic persistence of the characteristic temperature hierarchy across topologies and finite sizes argues against interpreting these features as incidental finite-size irregularities. Instead, our results support their interpretation as genuine third-order transitions whose structural detectability can be amplified by network topology.

</details>


### [115] [Skyrmion-Bimeron Transformation in Bilayer Chiral Magnets with Competing Magnetic Anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11585)
*Gülşen Doğan,Ümit Akıncı*

TL;DR: 通过蒙特卡洛模拟研究了双层手性磁体中的拓扑自旋纹理，揭示了包括斯格明子晶格、半子-反半子晶体相在内的多种磁构型，并构建了标度手征性映射以表征系统拓扑特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究双层手性磁体中拓扑自旋纹理（topological spin textures）的涌现机制，重点关注双层几何结构如何通过层间交换耦合（interlayer exchange coupling）稳定拓扑构型，为纳米尺度自旋电子学系统提供新的平台。

Method: 采用经典自旋模型的蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations），模型包含交换相互作用（exchange interaction）、Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）、磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）和外磁场（external magnetic field）。通过构建(K/J, h/J)参数空间中的标度手征性映射（scalar chirality map）来表征系统拓扑特性。

Result: 研究揭示了多种磁构型，包括迷宫结构（labyrinth structures）、斯格明子晶格（skyrmion lattices）、铁磁态（ferromagnetic states）和半子-反半子晶体相（meron-antimeron crystal phases）。特别发现从易轴到易面各向异性（easy-axis to easy-plane anisotropy）的转变驱动了从斯格明子纹理到双半子型构型（bimeron-type configurations）的连续转变。

Conclusion: 双层几何结构引入了额外的稳定机制，层间交换耦合使两层中的拓扑核心相互关联，增加了缺陷坍塌的能量成本。这些发现为双层手性磁体提供了系统的拓扑纹理映射，并突显耦合磁层作为稳定纳米尺度自旋电子学系统中双半子型自旋纹理的有前景平台。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the emergence of topological spin textures in a ferromagnetically coupled bilayer chiral magnet by means of Monte Carlo simulations of a classical spin model including exchange interaction, Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction, magnetic anisotropy, and an external magnetic field. To characterize the topology of the system, we construct a scalar chirality map in the $(K/J,h/J)$ parameter space.
  Our results reveal several magnetic configurations, including labyrinth structures, skyrmion lattices, ferromagnetic states, and meron-antimeron crystal phases. In particular, we show that the transition from easy-axis to easy-plane anisotropy drives a continuous transformation from skyrmion textures to bimeron-type configurations. The bilayer geometry introduces an additional stabilization mechanism, where interlayer exchange coupling correlates the topological cores in the two layers and increases the energetic cost of defect collapse.
  These findings provide a systematic topological texture map for bilayer chiral magnets and highlight coupled magnetic layers as a promising platform for stabilizing bimeron-type spin textures in nanoscale spintronic systems.

### [116] [Weak integrability breaking perturbations in classical integrable models on the lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11712)
*Sara Vanovac,Catherine McCarthy,Federica Maria Surace,Olexei I. Motrunich*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种系统构建经典格点可积模型中弱可积性破坏扰动（WIBs）的框架，并将其应用于Ishimori模型、Toda链和简谐振子链（HOC）。特别地，证明了alpha-FPUT模型中的立方非线性相互作用是真正的WIB扰动，并构造了相应的准守恒量层次结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子系统中的弱可积性破坏扰动（weak integrability breaking perturbations, WIBs）已被广泛研究，因其能延迟热化和扩散输运的发生时间。然而，量子模型的长时动力学计算具有挑战性，因此需要利用经典可积格点模型作为补充平台来探究WIBs下的输运和长时动力学行为。

Method: 作者将通用框架专门化，为Ishimori模型、Toda链和简谐振子链（Harmonic Oscillator Chain, HOC）构建了多个WIBs家族。特别地，利用Toda晶格的运动积分（integrals of motion, IoMs）显式构造了HOC运动积分层次结构的修正，从而获得了alpha-FPUT链的无限塔状准守恒量。

Result: 证明了立方非线性（alpha-FPUT相互作用）是真正的WIB扰动。识别出相应的绝热规范势（adiabatic gauge potential, AGP）在实空间中表现为非平凡的三局域生成元。更一般地，任何立方、平移不变、动量守恒的HOC扰动都允许此类生成元，因此都是WIBs。

Conclusion: 该研究为弱可积性破坏提供了一个统一的经典框架，可用于诊断近可积哈密顿格点系统中的异常热化和输运现象。结合输运和AGP方差研究，该框架为理解近可积系统中的动力学行为提供了系统工具。

Abstract: We show how to systematically construct weak integrability breaking perturbations (WIBs) for classical integrable models on the lattice. These perturbations, which allow quasi-conserved quantities, have mostly been explored in quantum systems, where they are expected to delay the onset of thermalization and diffusive transport to timescales far exceeding those predicted by Fermi's golden rule. However, accessing such long-time dynamics in quantum models is computationally challenging. Classical integrable lattice models offer a complementary setting for probing transport and long-time dynamics under WIBs. In this work, we specialize our general framework to construct several families of WIBs for the Ishimori model, the Toda chain, and the Harmonic Oscillator Chain (HOC). Such constructions can help quantify how WIBs contribute to anomalous transport and serve as a benchmark for thermalization studies in perturbed integrable models. An important example is the Fermi-Pasta-Ulam-Tsingou (FPUT) model: Starting from the HOC, we show that the cubic nonlinearity (the alpha-FPUT interaction) is a genuine WIB perturbation. Using the integrals of motion (IoMs) of the Toda lattice, we explicitly construct corrections to the entire hierarchy of the HOC IoMs, thereby obtaining an infinite tower of quasi-conserved quantities for the alpha-FPUT chain. We further identify the corresponding adiabatic gauge potential (AGP) as a nontrivial trilocal generator in real space, and show that, more generally, any cubic, translationally invariant, momentum-conserving perturbation of the HOC admits such a generator and is therefore a WIB. Together with our transport and AGP-variance studies, our results provide a unified classical framework for weak integrability breaking and for diagnosing anomalous thermalization and transport in nearly integrable Hamiltonian lattice systems.

</details>


### [117] [Quantum Many-Body Mpemba Effect through Resonances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11788)
*Shion Yamashika,Ryusuke Hamazaki*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文为理解封闭量子多体混沌系统中的量子姆潘巴效应（quantum Mpemba effect）提供了一个通用框架，通过将局部子系统的平衡过程重新表述为Ruelle-Pollicott共振，揭示了抑制初始态与主导共振模式重叠可加速平衡，并发现通过初始态的完全平移对称性破缺可实现强量子姆潘巴效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子姆潘巴效应（quantum Mpemba effect, QME）的微观起源尚不清楚，而近期可控量子平台的发展为探索其量子类似物提供了机会。本文旨在为理解封闭量子多体混沌系统中的QME提供一个通用框架。

Method: 通过将局部子系统的平衡过程重新表述为Ruelle-Pollicott（RP）共振，建立了理解QME的理论框架。使用典型的受踢伊辛链（kicked Ising chain）和受数论启发的实验相关初始态来验证理论预测。

Result: 研究表明，抑制初始态与主导Ruelle-Pollicott共振模式的重叠可以加速子系统平衡，从而产生量子姆潘巴效应。进一步发现，通过初始态的完全平移对称性破缺可以实现一种新型的强量子姆潘巴效应。

Conclusion: 这些发现将封闭多体系统中的量子姆潘巴效应纳入了一个与开放系统类似物相统一的框架，并为最先进的量子平台提供了实验可观测的特征。

Abstract: Relaxation towards equilibrium is often assumed to be slower when a system starts farther from equilibrium, but this intuition fails in the Mpemba effect. Recent advances in controllable quantum platforms have enabled the exploration of its quantum analogue, the quantum Mpemba effect (QME), yet its microscopic origin remains largely unclear. Here we provide a general framework for understanding the QME in closed quantum many-body chaotic systems by reformulating the equilibration process of local subsystems in terms of Ruelle-Pollicott (RP) resonances. We show that suppressing the initial-state overlap with the dominant RP resonant mode accelerates subsystem equilibration and thereby yields the QME. We further uncover that a novel type of strong QME can occur via complete translation-symmetry breaking of initial states. We substantiate our predictions using the prototypical kicked Ising chain and exotic yet experimentally relevant initial states inspired by number theory. These findings cast the QME in closed many-body systems into a unified framework with open-system analogues and provide experimentally accessible signatures on state-of-the-art quantum platforms.

</details>


### [118] [A Universality Emerging in a Universality: Derivation of the Ericson Transition in Stochastic Quantum Scattering and Experimental Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12068)
*Simon Köhnes,Jiongning Che,Barbara Dietz,Thomas Guhr*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文在通用海德堡方法（universal Heidelberg approach）中推导了向埃里克森区域（Ericson regime）的转变，证明了散射矩阵元素的普适高斯分布，并获得了分布矩的显式公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子混沌多体、无序或一般随机系统中，共振在较高能量下重叠，最终达到埃里克森区域（Ericson regime），此时散射截面表现为随机函数。六十多年来，这种在普适系统随机性之上出现的额外鲁棒普适行为一直缺乏简洁的分析处理。

Method: 采用通用海德堡方法（universal Heidelberg approach），通过适当的渐近展开推导向埃里克森区域的转变，并证明散射矩阵元素的普适高斯分布。

Result: 成功推导了向埃里克森区域的转变，证明了散射矩阵元素遵循普适高斯分布，并获得了分布矩的显式公式。通过与微波实验和数值模拟的比较验证了理论结果。

Conclusion: 该研究为埃里克森区域的出现提供了简洁的分析处理，证明了散射矩阵元素的普适高斯分布特性，并通过实验和数值模拟验证了理论推导的有效性。

Abstract: At lower energies, the resonances in scattering experiments are often isolated. In quantum chaotic many-body, disordered or generically stochastic systems, the resonances overlap at larger energies. Eventually, the Ericson regime is reached in which the cross section behaves like a random function. The scattering matrix elements then follow a universal Gaussian distribution. For more than sixty years, the emergence of this robust additional universal behavior on top of the universal system stochasticity awaits a concise analytical treatment. We derive the transition to the Ericson regime in the universal Heidelberg approach and prove the universal Gaussian distribution by a proper asymptotic expansion. We also obtain explicit formulae for the moments of the distributions. We compare with microwave experiments and numerical simulations.

### [119] [Spatiotemporal Characterization of Active Brownian Dynamics in Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12080)
*Yanis Baouche,Mathis Guéneau,Christina Kurzthaler*

TL;DR: 该研究分析了受限活性布朗粒子（ABP）在边界处的积累现象，通过Siegmund对偶性建立了吸收边界与硬壁边界问题之间的直接映射，揭示了活性运动如何影响首次通过时间和空间分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用分析预测方法研究受限活性布朗粒子（ABP）在吸收边界和硬壁边界条件下的行为。利用Siegmund对偶性建立了两类边界问题传播子之间的直接映射，并在低活性和高活性区域（量化了相对于扩散的持续运动）分析系统。

Result: 研究表明，活性运动结合有利的初始取向通常能降低相对于被动扩散的平均首次通过时间（mean first-passage time）。硬壁间的全时变传播子通过Siegmund对偶性趋近于由分裂概率导数给出的壁积累稳态。

Conclusion: Siegmund对偶性为理解活性布朗粒子在边界处的积累现象提供了理论框架，揭示了活性运动对首次通过特性和空间分布的定量影响，特别是硬壁边界条件下的壁积累稳态行为。

Abstract: Accumulation at boundaries represents a widely observed phenomenon in active systems with implications for microbial ecology and engineering applications. To rationalize the underlying physics, we provide analytical predictions for the first-passage properties and spatial distributions of a confined active Brownian particle (ABP). We show that ABPs with absorbing and hard-wall boundary conditions are Siegmund duals, yielding a direct mapping between the propagators of the two problems. We analyze the system across low and high activity regimes -- quantifying persistent motion relative to diffusion -- and show that active motion, together with a favorable initial orientation, typically lowers the mean first-passage time relative to passive diffusion. Notably, the full time-dependent propagator between hard walls approaches a wall-accumulated stationary state given by the derivative of the splitting probability as a consequence of Siegmund duality.

### [120] [Direct Boltzmann inversion method from particle configurations at arbitrary state points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12081)
*Olivier Coquand,Davide Paolino,Ludovic Berthier*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种直接玻尔兹曼反演方法，用于从任意状态点的粒子构型推断相互作用势，无需迭代模拟，计算成本低且易于实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统迭代玻尔兹曼反演方法需要在迭代过程的每一步执行新的蒙特卡洛模拟，计算成本高昂。本文旨在开发一种无需迭代模拟、计算效率更高的相互作用势推断方法。

Method: 该方法通过强制两个独立的对关联函数估计之间的一致性来推断相互作用势：一个基于粒子间距离，另一个基于成对力。该方法仅依赖于粒子间力的表达式，因此计算成本低且易于实现。

Result: 该方法在多种测试势的计算机模拟中进行了性能基准测试，显示出良好的表现。由于仅依赖于粒子间力表达式，该方法适用于任何状态点，包括高密度情况，而替代方法可能在此失效。

Conclusion: 由于其简单性和普适性，该方法应具有广泛的应用前景，从粗粒度相互作用势的构建到非平衡系统中有效相互作用的推断。

Abstract: We introduce a direct Boltzmann inversion method to infer the interaction potential in particle systems using as input particle configurations generated at an arbitrary state point of the system. Unlike iterative Boltzmann inversion, the proposed method does not require performing a new Monte Carlo simulation at each step of the iteration process. It relies instead on enforcing consistency between two independent estimates of the pair correlation function, respectively obtained from interparticle distances and from pairwise forces. As a result, the approach is computationally inexpensive and straightforward to implement. Because it relies on the sole expression of interparticle forces, our method naturally applies to any state point, including when the density is large and alternative methods may fail. Here we present the basic principles of the method and benchmark its performance on a diverse set of test potentials studied using computer simulations. Practical aspects and detailed implementation of the method are also discussed. Owing to its simplicity and generality, the method should be broadly applicable, from the construction of coarse-grained interaction potentials to the inference of effective interactions in non-equilibrium systems.

### [121] [Non-Markovian Entropy Dynamics in Living Systems from the Keldysh Formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12184)
*Feiyi Liu,Min Guo,Hongwei Tan,Yang Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究基于Keldysh泛函形式主义和随机热力学，为非平衡生物系统的熵动力学建立了非马尔可夫理论框架，揭示了活性生物涨落的直接热力学特征及其与系统发育、衰老和死亡的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生命系统是开放的非平衡系统，持续与环境交换能量、物质和信息，导致具有记忆和活性涨落的随机动力学。需要建立能够自然整合有色环境噪声、记忆相关耗散和多体相互作用的理论框架。

Method: 基于Keldysh泛函形式主义（Keldysh functional formalism）和随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics），发展了非马尔可夫理论框架。该方法自然整合了有色环境噪声（colored environmental noise）、记忆相关耗散（memory-dependent dissipation）和多体相互作用（many-body interactions），产生了广义朗之万动力学（generalized Langevin dynamics）和非马尔可夫主方程（non-Markovian master equations）。

Result: 推导了熵产生率（entropy production rate）的精确频域表达式，表明涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relation）的违反提供了活性生物涨落的直接热力学特征。环境记忆增强了低频涨落和熵产生，导致动力学不稳定性附近的临界慢化（critical slowing down）。

Conclusion: 这些结果为生命系统的熵"浴缸"图景（entropy "bathtub" picture）提供了微观物理基础，并将熵演化与非平衡动力学中的发育、衰老和死亡联系起来。

Abstract: Living systems are open nonequilibrium systems that continuously exchange energy, matter, and information with their environments, leading to stochastic dynamics with memory and active fluctuations. In this study, we develop a non-Markovian theoretical framework for the entropy dynamics of living systems based on the Keldysh functional formalism and stochastic thermodynamics. The approach naturally incorporates colored environmental noise, memory-dependent dissipation, and many-body interactions, yielding generalized Langevin dynamics and non-Markovian master equations. Within this framework we derive an exact frequency-domain expression for the entropy production rate and show that violations of the fluctuation-dissipation relation provide a direct thermodynamic signature of active biological fluctuations. We further demonstrate that environmental memory enhances low-frequency fluctuations and entropy production, leading to critical slowing down near dynamical instability. These results provide a microscopic physical foundation for the entropy "bathtub" picture of living systems and connect entropy evolution with development, aging, and death in nonequilibrium dynamics.

</details>

### [122] [Statistical Mechanics of Density- and Temperature-Dependent Potentials: Application to Condensed Phases within GenDPDE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11203)
*Giuseppe Colella,Allan D. Mackie,James P. Larentzos,Fernando Bresme,Josep Bonet Avalos*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究在广义耗散粒子动力学能量守恒（GenDPDE）框架内开发了局部热力学（LTh）模型，用于描述凝聚相，并通过氩的液态和超临界条件验证了模型准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粗粒化拉格朗日方法（如耗散粒子动力学）适合描述包含热涨落的介观流体系统，但使用这些方法进行液体的真实模拟仍是一个长期存在的问题。

Method: 在广义耗散粒子动力学能量守恒（Generalized Dissipative Particle Dynamics with Energy Conservation, GenDPDE）框架内开发局部热力学（local thermodynamic, LTh）模型，该模型在介观尺度上明确考虑了热膨胀系数和等温压缩率。

Result: 通过氩在液态和超临界条件下的平衡模拟验证了LTh模型的准确性，模型在参考状态附近的热力学条件范围内有效，能够正确描述密度和温度存在空间变化的系统物理特性。

Conclusion: LTh模型使GenDPDE成为通过粗粒化技术分析凝聚相的可靠且多功能的工具，即使在平均场水平上，准确捕捉局部粒子排列对于从介观数据预测宏观热力学性质也至关重要。

Abstract: Coarse-grain Lagrangian methods, such as Dissipative Particle Dynamics ( Hoogerbrugge et al., EPL, 1992), are suitable for describing mesoscopic fluid systems that include thermal fluctuations. However, the realistic simulation of liquids using these methods represents a longstanding problem. In this work, we develop a local thermodynamic (LTh) model for the description of condensed phases within the framework of the Generalized Dissipative Particle Dynamics with Energy Conservation (GenDPDE) method (Bonet Avalos et al., PCCP 2019). Such a model is appropriate for the analysis of liquids, due to the explicit account of the thermal expansion coefficient and isothermal compressibility at the mesoscale. We demonstrate the accuracy of the LTh model by examining the thermodynamic properties of argon at both liquid and supercritical conditions, through equilibrium simulations performed around two key reference states (125.7 K, 85.31 MPa, 1419.7 kg/m3 for liquid Ar, and 418.8 K, 85.31 MPa, 695.99 kg/m3 for supercritical Ar). Remarkably, we show that the model is also valid over a range of thermodynamic conditions near the reference states, allowing a correct description of the physics of systems with spatial variations in density and temperature. We further derive analytical expressions for the macroscopic pressure and energy equations of state based on the model parameters, discussing their validity and limitations. We demonstrate that, even at the mean-field level, accurately capturing local particle arrangements is essential for predicting macroscopic thermodynamic properties from mesoscopic data. We also assess the applicability of the HNC approximation in predicting the radial distribution function of the GenDPDE system, exploring its strengths and limitations. With the LTh model, GenDPDE offers a dependable and versatile tool for analysing condensed phases through coarse-grain techniques.

</details>


### [123] [Gelation dynamics of charged colloidal rods: critical behaviour and time-connectivity superposition principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11366)
*Lise Morlet-Decarnin,Thibaut Divoux,Sébastien Manneville*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了纤维素纳米晶（CNCs）作为典型带电棒状胶体在盐溶液中的凝胶化动力学，通过时间分辨力学谱揭示了明确的临界凝胶点，并建立了凝胶与吸引玻璃态之间的相边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管球形胶体的凝胶化已被广泛研究，但对各向异性胶体（如棒状胶体）的凝胶化动力学了解甚少。本研究以纤维素纳米晶（CNCs）为原型，探究高电荷棒状胶体在静电屏蔽条件下的自组装凝胶网络形成机制。

Method: 采用时间分辨力学谱（time-resolved mechanical spectroscopy）研究CNC悬浮液在强剪切后的力学恢复动力学。通过改变CNC重量分数和盐浓度，分析流变学观测量的变化，包括凝胶点的弹性模量和粘性模量及其高频幂律指数。

Result: 研究揭示了明确的液-固转变临界凝胶点，演化粘弹性谱可重标到主曲线上，证明了时间-连通性叠加原理（time-connectivity superposition principle）和临界动力学。通过分析动态临界指数和超标度关系，发现凝胶前与凝胶后动力学之间存在显著不对称性，且动态指数具有非普适性。

Conclusion: 该研究突出了高电荷棒状胶体特有的凝胶化机制，识别了凝胶与吸引玻璃态（attractive glass states）之间的相边界，并指出需要补充微观结构表征和理论建模来进一步理解这些机制。

Abstract: Charged colloidal particles can self-assemble into gel networks upon screening of electrostatic repulsion by added salt. While gelation of spherical colloids has been extensively studied, much less is known about the gelation dynamics of anisotropic colloids. Here, we focus on cellulose nanocrystals (CNCs) as prototypical rigid, highly charged rod-like colloids. In aqueous solution with salt, CNCs display a rich phase diagram ranging from gel at low solid content to glassy phases at higher concentrations. Building on our previous work [Morlet-Decarnin et al., ACS Macro Lett., 2023, 12, 1733], we present an extensive study of the mechanical recovery dynamics of CNC suspensions following a strong shear. Time-resolved mechanical spectroscopy reveals a liquid-to-solid transition characterized by a well-defined critical gel point. The evolving viscoelastic spectra can be rescaled onto master curves, demonstrating a time-connectivity superposition principle and critical dynamics on both sides of the gel point. By varying the CNC weight fraction and salt concentration, we identify a boundary between gel and attractive glass states marked by clear changes in rheological observables, including the elastic and viscous moduli at the gel point and their high-frequency power-law exponents. Analysis of dynamic critical exponents and hyperscaling reveals pronounced asymmetry between pre-gel and post-gel dynamics and non-universal values of the dynamic exponent. These findings highlight gelation mechanisms specific to highly charged rod-like colloids and call for complementary microstructural characterization and theoretical modeling.

### [124] [Using the force landscape of an active solid to predict plastic deformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11425)
*Tyler Hain,Edan Lerner,M. Lisa Manning*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非活性无序固体中的准局域激发（quasilocalized excitations）控制着塑性行为，类似于晶体缺陷。本研究旨在探索这一概念能否扩展到活性物质（active matter）领域，特别是自驱动棒（self-propelled rods）的密堆积系统。

Method: 研究将非线性激发（nonlinear excitations）的定义推广到包含主动、非保守力（active, non-conservative forces）的力景观（force landscapes）中。通过分析自驱动棒密堆积系统的力基三次激发（force-based cubic excitations），评估其对塑性事件的预测能力。

Result: 研究发现力基三次激发能够稳健地预测未来的塑性事件（plastic events）。这种预测能力使得对活性固体（active solids）的控制成为可能。

Conclusion: 非活性无序固体中准局域激发的概念可以成功扩展到活性物质系统。基于力的非线性激发分析为理解和控制活性固体的塑性行为提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Non-active disordered solids feature quasilocalized excitations that control plasticity, similar to crystal lattice defects, and these excitations can be identified via harmonic or anharmonic analyses of the potential energy landscape. Here we explore whether such ideas can be extended to active matter, focusing on dense packings of self-propelled rods. We generalize the definition of nonlinear excitations to force landscapes that incorporate active, non-conservative forces and find that force-based cubic excitations robustly predict future plastic events, enabling control of active solids.

### [125] [Effect of flow kinematics on extensional viscosity of dilute polymer solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11518)
*Yusuke Koide,Takato Ishida,Takashi Uneyama,Yuichi Masubuchi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过耗散粒子动力学模拟，探究了流动运动学对稀聚合物溶液拉伸粘度的影响，揭示了在不同拉伸流动类型（单轴、平面、双轴）下，聚合物构象变化与纯运动学效应之间的竞争关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在阐明流动运动学（flow kinematics）对稀聚合物溶液拉伸粘度（extensional viscosity）的影响机制。当前对于不同拉伸流动类型下粘度行为的定量差异及其物理起源尚不完全清楚。

Method: 采用耗散粒子动力学（dissipative particle dynamics）模拟方法，在单轴（uniaxial）、平面（planar）和双轴（biaxial）拉伸流动条件下进行研究。同时基于单链模型（single-chain model）推导出连接拉伸粘度与聚合物构象的分析表达式。

Result: 在高拉伸速率下，稀聚合物溶液在所有流动类型中均表现出应变硬化（strain hardening），但定量行为取决于流动类型。当聚合物几乎不受扰动时，粘度差异主要由纯运动学效应决定；当聚合物被拉伸时，拉伸方向上的回转半径（gyration radius）成为主导因素，该方向的拉伸程度差异导致相应的粘度变化。

Conclusion: 拉伸粘度的流动运动学依赖性源于聚合物构象变化与纯运动学效应之间的相互作用。该分析框架成功分离了流动诱导的聚合物构象变化贡献和由速度梯度张量（velocity gradient tensor）结构决定的纯运动学贡献。

Abstract: We investigate the effect of flow kinematics on the extensional viscosity of dilute polymer solutions by conducting dissipative particle dynamics simulations under uniaxial, planar, and biaxial extensional flows. At high extension rates, dilute polymer solutions exhibit strain hardening under these flows, while the quantitative behavior depends on the flow type. To elucidate the physical origin of this flow-kinematics dependence, we relate the extensional viscosity to polymer conformation using an analytical expression derived from a single-chain model. The resulting relation allows us to separate the contribution of flow-induced polymer conformational changes and the purely kinematic contribution determined by the structure of the velocity gradient tensor. When polymers remain almost unperturbed by extensional flows, differences in the extensional viscosity are governed primarily by the purely kinematic effects. In contrast, as polymers are stretched, the gyration radius in the extensional direction becomes the dominant factor, and differences in the stretching degree in this direction lead to corresponding variations in the extensional viscosity.

</details>

*Jose M. G. Vilar,J. Miguel Rubi,Leonor Saiz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 熵力在纳米尺度现象中起基础作用，从胶体自组装到生物分子解聚。然而，对于系绳介导（tether-mediated）的纳米丝束分离，熵力的具体作用机制尚不完全清楚，需要建立精确理论来揭示其基本规律。

Method: 本文发展了精确的解析理论（exact analytical theory），推导出熵分离的一般标度律（general scaling laws），并通过布朗动力学模拟（Brownian dynamics simulations）验证理论预测。

Result: 研究发现单个无量纲参数——排除体积半径（excluded-volume radius）与系绳长度（tether length）的比值——决定丝束是被推开还是被拉近。意外地发现了熵力促进聚集的反常机制，挑战了熵力总是促进解聚的传统观点。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了熵力可以维持丝束处于吸引性亚稳态（attractive metastable states）的条件，为生物物理学、软物质物理学和纳米技术应用提供了预测性见解。

Abstract: Entropic forces play a fundamental role in nanoscale phenomena, from colloidal self-assembly to biomolecular disaggregation. Here, we develop an exact analytical theory and find general scaling laws for the entropic separation of tether-mediated nanofilament bundles, revealing that a single dimensionless parameter--the ratio of the excluded-volume radius to the tether length--dictates whether filaments are pushed apart or, contrary to the usual expectation, pulled together. This unexpected regime challenges the view that entropic forces invariably promote disaggregation, instead uncovering conditions under which the bundles can remain in attractive metastable states. Brownian dynamics simulations confirm this paradoxical effect, offering predictive insights for applications in biophysics, soft matter physics, and nanotechnology.

### [127] [Metadensity functional learning for classical fluids: Regularizing with pair correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11973)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索和利用神经元密度泛函理论描述非均匀流体物理的潜力。该理论对势的依赖关系与软物质设计和Henderson反演相关，并允许在预测阶段动态改变对势。

Conclusion: 该研究成功利用神经元密度泛函理论探索了获取体流体对关联结构的"元直接"途径，为软物质设计和Henderson反演问题提供了基于第一性原理的新方法，避免了传统Ornstein-Zernike反演的局限性。

Abstract: We investigate and exploit consequences of the recent neural metadensity functional theory [Kampa et al., Phys. Rev. Lett. 134, 107301 (2025), 10.1103/PhysRevLett.134.107301] for describing the physics of inhomogeneous fluids. The metadensity dependence on the pair potential is relevant for soft matter design and Henderson inversion and it allows one to change the pair potential on the fly at prediction stage. Here we consider one-dimensional systems with short-ranged (truncated) interparticle forces and draw on the functional pair potential dependence to investigate 'metadirect' routes towards the bulk fluid pair correlation structure. Classical density functional theory provides the required functional relationships. Efficient variational calculus is implemented by neural functional line integration and automatic differentiation. We regularize local learning of neural functionals by comparing the pair structure from different routes. Thereby results from metadirect functional differentiation are matched against accurate test particle data from an initial locally trained metadensity functional. Accessing the pair structure via the metadensity functional dependence circumvents Ornstein-Zernike inversion and it is based on first principles.

### [128] [Spatiotemporal crystallization of an active fluid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12079)
*Olga Bantysh,Ramon Reigada,Rodrigo C. V. Coelho,Pau Guillamat,Jordi Ignés-Mullol,Francesc Sagués*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究展示了混沌活性向列相（active nematic）能够自组织形成时空晶体（spatiotemporal crystal），在无外力作用下产生具有空间和时间平移对称性破缺的规则晶格结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解决远离平衡态物理中的核心挑战：如何从内在混沌中产生长程时空有序性。活性流体（如驱动细胞运动的细胞骨架网络）中自发生成的流动通常产生缺乏平移对称性的"活性湍流（active turbulence）"。

Method: 实验采用与层状液晶（lamellar liquid crystal）界面接触的微管/驱动蛋白（microtubule/kinesin）活性向列相，并将其限制在微流控通道中。同时使用连续介质向列流体动力学（continuum nematohydrodynamics）模拟来支持实验解释。

Result: 观察到在没有外部强迫的情况下，混沌活性向列相能够自组织形成稳健的时空晶格，产生密度、取向和涡度的规则晶格结构。这种有序性源于内在流动不稳定性的自发同步（spontaneous synchronization），通过限制以及活性层与被动各向异性界面之间的反馈机制实现。

Conclusion: 该研究调和了活性物质（active matter）中的混沌与结晶性，为在自驱动、远离平衡态的软材料中工程化有序结构提供了策略。研究强调了内在长度和时间尺度如何塑造活性晶体。

Abstract: The emergence of long-range spatiotemporal order from intrinsic chaos is a central challenge in far-from-equilibrium physics. In active fluids, such as cytoskeletal networks driving cellular motion, self-generated flows typically produce "active turbulence", lacking translational symmetry. Here we show that a chaotic active nematic can self-organize into a spatiotemporal crystal, forming a regular lattice of density, orientation, and vorticity that breaks both spatial and temporal translational symmetry. Using a microtubule/kinesin active nematic interfaced with a lamellar liquid crystal and confined in microfluidic channels, we observe robust spatiotemporal lattices without external forcing. The ordering emerges from spontaneous synchronization of intrinsic flow instabilities, mediated by confinement and feedback between the active layer and the passive anisotropic interface. Continuum nematohydrodynamics simulations support our interpretation, highlighting how intrinsic length and time scales shape the active crystals. These results reconcile chaos and crystallinity in active matter and provide a strategy for engineering order in self-driven, far-from-equilibrium soft materials.

### [129] [Arrested coalescence drives helical coiling and networking of filamentous smectic condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12124)
*Christopher A. Browne,Paul G. Severino,Yvonne Zagzag,Jacob Z. Cloutier,Aaron C. Boyd,Yihao Chen,Arjun G. Yodh,Chinedum O. Osuji*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了液晶-液相分离中丝状凝聚体自发组装成稀疏网络的机制，发现丝状连接由界面能最小化和近晶相序约束驱动的受阻聚结（arrested coalescence）所介导，最终形成双螺旋结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 液晶-液相分离（liquid-liquid crystal phase separation, LLCPS）在工业和生物环境中广泛存在，其中近晶相（smectic phases）凝聚形成的丝状凝聚体能够自发组装成具有丰富类生命动力学的稀疏网络。研究旨在揭示这些独特网络形成过程中丝状连接和构象变化的底层机制。

Method: 采用显微技术观察丝状连接过程，结合偏振光学显微镜（polarized optical microscopy）、理论建模和模拟分析，研究界面能最小化和近晶相序约束对丝状连接的影响。

Result: 研究发现丝状连接由受阻聚结（arrested coalescence）驱动，该过程依赖于界面能最小化和近晶相序约束。丝状体自发缠绕成双螺旋结构以减少界面面积和近晶相畸变，从而驱动网络紧凑化。研究提出了与这一解释一致的微观结构，能够定量预测受阻聚结的程度。

Conclusion: 这些发现为液晶中网络形成提供了一条通用途径，有助于理解其他工程或生物材料中凝聚体网络的形成机制。研究揭示了在缺乏分子手性或中间相转变的情况下，丝状体通过受阻聚结形成双螺旋结构的自组装过程。

Abstract: Liquid-liquid crystal phase separation (LLCPS) occurs in many industrial and biological settings. To date the states of the separated condensed liquid crystals have been found to be nematic, columnar, or smectic phases. Interestingly, when smectic phases condense out of the liquid, they can form filamentous condensates that spontaneously assemble into sparse networks with rich life-like dynamics. Here, we study the underlying process of filament linking and conformational changes that mediates formation of these unique networks. Microscopy reveals that new linkages between filaments are initiated by an adhesive interaction between straight filaments; the filaments snap into contact and then rapidly wind into helical coils, despite the absence of molecular chirality or transitions between mesophases. Using polarized optical microscopy, theoretical modeling, and simulation, we show that filament linking into ribbon structures is driven by arrested coalescence that depends on both interfacial energy minimization and the constraints of smectic order. The linked filaments spontaneously coil into double helices to reduce interfacial area and smectic distortion, thus driving compaction into networks. We propose a microstructure consistent with this interpretation, which quantitatively predicts the extent of arrested coalescence. In total, these findings suggest a generic pathway for network formation in liquid crystals that provides insight about the formation of condensate networks in other engineered or biological materials.

</details>

### [130] [Warm Inflation Beyond the Markovian Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11629)
*Mayukh R. Gangopadhyay,Nilanjana Kumar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了超越马尔可夫极限的暖暴胀（warm inflation），分析了有限关联时间（finite correlation time）对原初标量功率谱（primordial scalar power spectrum）的影响，发现记忆效应会抑制标量谱并建立了非马尔可夫效应与背景热动力学参数的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统暖暴胀研究通常假设随机力源是马尔可夫过程，但实际热系统具有有限弛豫时间，会产生具有非零关联时间的有色噪声（colored noise）。本研究旨在探索超越马尔可夫极限的暖暴胀，确定有限关联时间如何修正原初标量功率谱。

Method: 研究在暖暴胀框架下超越马尔可夫近似，考虑具有有限关联时间的有色噪声，分析记忆效应对暴胀场涨落的影响。通过建立背景热动力学参数与修正效应的直接联系，推导了标量功率谱的修正表达式。

Result: 研究发现记忆效应会抑制标量功率谱相对于标准白噪声结果，推导出了用背景热动力学参数表示的简单修正表达式。特别地，将非马尔可夫效应的大小直接与浴温度（bath temperature）和哈勃尺度（Hubble scale）的热比值联系起来，建立了暖暴胀背景量与马尔可夫近似有效性之间的透明联系。同时推导了张标比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）、标量谱指数（scalar spectral index）及其跑动（running of the scalar spectral index）的相应修正。

Conclusion: 研究结果为识别暖暴胀模型构建中有限关联时间效应何时变得相关提供了简单实用的诊断工具，建立了热动力学参数与马尔可夫近似有效性之间的直接联系，对暖暴胀模型的精确构建具有重要意义。

Abstract: Warm inflation is commonly studied under the assumption that the stochastic force sourcing inflaton fluctuations is Markovian. Realistic thermal systems, however, possess finite relaxation times and can therefore generate colored noise with non-zero correlation time. In this work, we investigate warm inflation beyond the Markovian limit and determine how finite correlation time modifies the primordial scalar power spectrum.
  We show that memory effects suppress the scalar spectrum relative to the standard white-noise result and derive a simple expression for this correction in terms of the background thermal dynamics. In particular, we relate the size of the non-Markovian effect directly to the thermal ratio between the bath temperature and the Hubble scale, thereby establishing a transparent link between warm-inflation background quantities and the validity of the Markovian approximation. We also derive the corresponding modification of the tensor-to-scalar ratio and the induced shifts in the scalar spectral index and the running of the scalar spectral index.
  Our results provide a simple and practical diagnostic for identifying when finite correlation-time effects become relevant in warm-inflation model building.

</details>


### [131] [Cosmological gravity on all scales V: MCMC forecasts combining large scale structure and CMB lensing for binned phenomenological modified gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11895)
*Sankarshana Srinivasan,Shreya Prabhu,Kai Lehman,Ajiv Krishnan V.,Jochen Weller*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种快速模拟方法，用于在修正引力（modified gravity）参数化框架下模拟非线性尺度的物质功率谱（matter power spectrum），并在LSST和CMB透镜联合观测的模拟数据中预测了对修正引力参数的约束能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着宇宙学进入数据主导阶段，特别是第四阶段大尺度结构巡天（stage IV large scale structure surveys）的到来，非线性尺度的建模成为重要挑战，尤其是在分析超越wCDM模型时。需要开发能够快速模拟修正引力效应的方法来应对这一挑战。

Method: 采用现象学参数化方法描述修正引力，其中随时间变化的有效引力常数μ和引力滑移η在红移上分箱处理。开发了快速模拟器来模拟物质功率谱，相对于COLA（COmoving Lagrangian Acceleration）模拟的精度优于1%。使用模拟的LSST Y10-like 3×2pt数据向量和LSST Y10 × Simons Observatory CMB透镜的6×2pt数据向量进行约束能力预测。

Result: 模拟器在修正引力增强因子方面达到<1%的精度。恢复了先前在Fisher预测中识别的μ和η之间的特征简并性，证明最佳约束方向对应于控制透镜势的组合Σ=μ(1+η)/2。大尺度结构对低红移的结构增长敏感，而CMB透镜将敏感性扩展到更高红移范围。

Conclusion: 非线性修正引力效应的快速模拟使得能够使用真实巡天数据向量和天体物理系统误差对模型无关的引力参数化进行完整的贝叶斯分析。这为未来大规模巡天数据的分析提供了重要工具。

Abstract: As cosmology rapidly approaches the data-dominated phase of stage IV large scale structure surveys, the modelling of nonlinear scales has become a serious challenge that faces the community, particularly when analysing models beyond $w$CDM. In this work, we emulate the matter power spectrum in a phenomenological parameterisation of modified gravity in which a time-varying effective gravitational constant $μ$ and a gravitational slip $η$ are binned in redshift. We are able to achieve accuracy $<1\%$ in the modified gravity boost relative to COLA (COmoving Lagrangian Acceleration) simulations. We forecast the constraining power for each bin using a simulated $3\times 2$pt LSST Y10-like data vector and a $6\times 2$pt LSST Y10 x Simons Observatory cosmic microwave background (CMB) lensing data vector. We recover the characteristic degeneracy between $μ$ and $η$ previously identified in Fisher forecasts and demonstrate that the best-constrained direction corresponds to the combination $Σ=μ(1+η)/2$ which governs the lensing potential. We show that while large scale structure is sensitive to growth of structure at low redshift, CMB lensing extends the sensitivity to a higher redshift range. These results demonstrate that fast emulation of nonlinear modified-gravity effects enables full Bayesian analyses of model-agnostic gravity parameterisations with realistic survey data vectors and astrophysical systematics.

### [132] [The Targeted Standard Siren Cosmology with Pulsar Timing Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12168)
*Shubhit Sardana,Boris Goncharov,Jacob Cardinal Tremblay*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究提出通过目标搜索而非全天盲搜来利用脉冲星计时阵列探测的超大质量黑洞双星作为标准汽笛，解决其大定位误差对宇宙学应用的制约问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）探测的超大质量黑洞双星（SMBHBs）通常具有约10-100平方度的定位误差，这一大定位误差长期以来阻碍了将这些源作为标准汽笛（standard sirens）用于精确宇宙学研究。

Method: 研究提出采用目标搜索（targeted searches）而非全天盲搜（all-sky blind searches）的方法，并基于当前PTA观测数据构建模拟数据集，应用于中国脉冲星计时阵列（CPTA）进行验证。

Result: 模拟结果显示，仅使用中国脉冲星计时阵列（CPTA）即可将哈勃常数（Hubble constant）的测量精度推至2 km/s/Mpc，该独立宇宙学探针的精度可为解决哈勃张力（Hubble tension）提供决定性支持。

Conclusion: 该方法可应用于多个同时观测的超大质量黑洞双星（SMBHBs），且在真实观测场景中，对源宿主星系间的混淆问题表现出良好的鲁棒性（robustness）。

Abstract: The sky localisation of about $10$ to $100~\text{deg}^2$, which is expected to be achieved in all-sky blind searches for gravitational waves from supermassive black hole binaries (SMBHBs) with Pulsar Timing Array (PTA) experiments, has long been posed as a prohibitive factor in utilising these sources as standard sirens for precision cosmology. We propose a solution to this problem, which makes use of targeted searches rather than all-sky blind searches for SMBHBs. Using our simulated data informed by current PTA observations, we show that the Chinese Pulsar Timing Array (CPTA) alone could infer the Hubble constant with a precision of 2~km/s/Mpc. Such precision in an independent cosmological probe could provide decisive support in the resolution of the Hubble tension. We demonstrate the application of our method to several simultaneously observed SMBHBs, as well as the method's robustness against confusion between the host galaxies of SMBHB sources in realistic observing scenarios.

### [133] [Scale-Dependent Loop Corrections to the Inflationary Power Spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12216)
*Matteo Braglia,Sebastián Céspedes,Lucas Pinol*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个适用于强破坏德西特对称性的暴胀背景的重整化程序，证明了紫外发散和tadpole项可通过有限个局域抵消项消除，并首次明确展示了由局域特征产生的一圈重整化功率谱在大尺度和小尺度均趋于零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于引力的非线性本质，原初关联函数的圈修正不可避免。先前工作主要针对（近）德西特（de Sitter）背景，缺乏适用于强破坏德西特对称性并产生尺度依赖特征的暴胀背景的一致重整化程序。

Method: 在暴胀涨落的有效场论（Effective Field Theory, EFT）框架内进行分析，允许威尔逊系数（Wilson coefficients）具有任意时间依赖性。针对共振特征（resonant features）和尖锐特征（sharp features）两种具体实现，在小特征振幅极限下精确计算。

Result: 证明了紫外发散（ultraviolet divergences）和tadpole项尽管具有强时间和尺度依赖性，仍可通过与EFT对称性兼容的有限个局域抵消项（local counter-terms）消除。首次明确展示了由暴胀轨迹上局域特征产生的一圈重整化功率谱（renormalised one-loop power spectrum）在大尺度和小尺度均趋于零。

Conclusion: 尺度依赖重整化框架表明，用于拟合CMB残差的原初特征模型与微扰性界限一致，并为研究标量诱导引力波（scalar-induced gravitational waves）和原初黑洞（primordial black holes）等更复杂场景中的圈修正打开了系统研究之门。

Abstract: Loop corrections to primordial correlation functions are unavoidable due to the non-linear nature of gravity. Previous works have established a robust framework for computing the renormalised one-loop power spectra of scalar and tensor modes, but primarily in (near) de Sitter backgrounds. In this work, we develop a consistent renormalisation procedure applicable to inflationary backgrounds that strongly break de Sitter symmetries and generate scale-dependent features in the primordial spectra. Our analysis is performed within the Effective Field Theory (EFT) of inflationary fluctuations, allowing for arbitrary time dependence of the Wilson coefficients. We show that both ultraviolet divergences and tadpoles of the theory, despite their strong time and scale dependence, can be cancelled by a finite set of local counter-terms compatible with the EFT symmetries. Importantly, this result only relies on the existence of an initial phase of adiabatic evolution continuously related to the Bunch-Davies vacuum and holds independently of the precise time dependence of the background and of the free-field mode functions. We then study two concrete realisations, corresponding to resonant and sharp features. In both cases, all calculations are carried out exactly in the limit of small feature amplitude. We analyse perturbativity and provide the first explicit demonstration that the renormalised one-loop power spectrum generated by a localised feature along the inflationary trajectory vanishes both at large and small scales. Our scale-dependent renormalisation framework implies that models of primordial features used to fit CMB residuals are consistent with perturbativity bounds, and opens the door to systematic studies of loop corrections in more complicated scenarios relevant for scalar-induced gravitational waves and primordial black holes.

</details>

### [134] [Nonlinear potential field in contact electrification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11144)
*Benjamin J. Kulbago,James Chen*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过原子场理论（AFT）和分子动力学（MD）模拟，揭示了接触起电（contact electrification）中电子转移的部分驱动力来源于接触过程中表面偶极诱导电位，并在碳-二氧化硅界面发现了非线性电位场和分离依赖的势垒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 接触起电中的电子转移机制是当前最具争议的物理问题之一。研究旨在探究表面偶极诱导电位是否在接触过程中驱动电子转移，以增进对接触起电基本机制的理解。

Method: 采用原子场理论（atomistic field theory, AFT）与分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟相结合的方法。选择碳-二氧化硅接触系统作为代表性研究对象，因其具有优异的摩擦隧穿功率输出性能。

Result: 研究结果揭示了接触界面存在非线性电位场以及分离依赖的势垒（separation dependent potential barrier）。这些发现为理解摩擦电荷转移（triboelectric charge transfer）的可能机制提供了关键证据。

Conclusion: 表面偶极诱导电位是驱动接触起电中电子转移的部分因素。研究结果对于理解接触起电的基本机制至关重要，为解释摩擦电荷转移现象提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: The cause of electron transfer in contact electrification is one of the most hotly debated physical problems today. In this study, the electron transfer is hypothesized to be partly driven by the surface dipole induced potential during contact. This phenomena is demonstrated by a combination of atomistic field theory (AFT) and molecular dynamics (MD) simulation. A representative contact system of carbon and silicon dioxide was chosen for its excellent tribo-tunneling power output performance. The results reveal the existence of a nonlinear potential field as well as the existence of a separation dependent potential barrier at the contact interface. Possible scenarios of triboelectric charge transfer are discussed in light of these results. These results are critical to the fundamental understanding of contact electrification.

</details>


### [135] [Mpemba Effect in Many-Body Systems Near Equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11707)
*Philippe Ben-Abdallah*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect）可在多体系统的线性响应（linear-response）区域内出现，无需非线性或远离平衡态（far-from-equilibrium）动力学。在可逆系统中，通过快慢模式的谱分离（spectral separation）产生均匀姆潘巴效应；打破可逆性则使弛豫算子非正规（non-normal），实现严格的分量式姆潘巴效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 姆潘巴效应通常与非线性或远离平衡态动力学相关，本研究旨在探索该效应是否能在多体系统的线性响应区域内出现，从而扩展对该现象的理论理解。

Method: 研究采用线性响应理论（linear-response theory）分析多体系统的弛豫行为。通过分析可逆（reciprocal）系统与非可逆系统的弛豫算子特性，特别是谱分离和非正规性（non-normality）的作用。

Result: 在可逆系统中，当自由度（degrees of freedom）为三个或以上时，通过快慢模式的谱分离可产生均匀姆潘巴效应。打破可逆性使弛豫算子变为非正规，实现严格的分量式姆潘巴效应，即较热状态在每个单独自由度上都弛豫更快。

Conclusion: 姆潘巴效应不仅限于非线性或远离平衡态区域，也可在线性响应区域内出现。可逆性条件决定了效应的表现形式：可逆系统产生均匀效应，非可逆系统实现严格的分量式效应。

Abstract: The Mpemba effect, in which a system initially farther from equilibrium relaxes faster than a closer one, is often associated with nonlinear or far-from-equilibrium dynamics. We show that this effect can arise entirely within the linear-response regime of many-body systems. In reciprocal systems, a uniform Mpemba effect emerges for three or more degrees of freedom via spectral separation of fast and slow modes. Breaking reciprocity renders the relaxation operator non-normal, enabling a strict componentwise Mpemba effect, with the hotter state relaxing faster even in every individual degree of freedom.

</details>

### [136] [Matlantis-PFP v8: Universal Machine Learning Interatomic Potential with Better Experimental Agreements via r2SCAN Functional](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11063)
*Chikashi Shinagawa,So Takamoto,Daiki Shintani,Yong-Bin Zhuang,Yuta Tsuboi,Katsuhiko Nishimra,Kohei Shinohara,Shigeru Iwase,Yuta Tanaka,Ju Li*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出PFP v8通用机器学习原子间势能（uMLIP），通过训练于r2SCAN meta-GGA数据而非传统PBE-GGA数据，显著提升了零样本预测实验数据的准确性，在晶体、分子和表面模拟中优于PBE-DFT计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通用机器学习原子间势能（universal Machine Learning Interatomic Potentials, uMLIPs）大多基于Perdew-Burke-Ernzerhof（PBE）广义梯度近似（generalized gradient approximation, GGA）数据训练，其精度受限于PBE水平。需要开发能够超越PBE功能限制、更好预测实验结果的uMLIPs。

Method: 提出PFP v8 uMLIP，在Matlantis服务中可用。该方法通过训练于正则化恢复的强约束适当范数（regularized-restored strongly constrained and appropriately normed, r2SCAN）meta-GGA势能面数据，覆盖广泛的化学领域，克服了PBE功能的内在限制。

Result: 无需领域特定微调，PFP v8在晶体、分子和表面模拟中系统性地改善了与实验数据或高精度参考的吻合度，优于基于PBE的密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算。在长时间分子动力学模拟中，预测熔点的平均误差约为130K，相比PBE训练模型误差减半。

Conclusion: uMLIPs能够超越其训练近似的限制，在不同化学领域中实现与实验数据显著改善的一致性，进一步缩小了模拟与现实之间的差距。PFP v8的成功表明将零样本预测实验作为明确设计目标是可行的。

Abstract: Universal Machine Learning Interatomic Potentials (uMLIPs) enable atomistic simulations and high-throughput screening at scales far beyond those accessible with density functional theory (DFT). However, most existing uMLIPs are trained on Perdew--Burke--Ernzerhof (PBE) generalized gradient approximation (GGA) data and are therefore fundamentally limited by PBE-level accuracy. In this paper, we argue that better zero-shot predictions versus experiments must be an explicit design target for uMLIPs and present PFP v8, a uMLIP available on the Matlantis service that overcomes the inherent limitations of the PBE functional by being trained to reproduce the regularized-restored strongly constrained and appropriately normed (r2SCAN) meta-GGA potential-energy surface across a wide range of chemical domains. Without requiring domain-specific fine-tuning, PFP v8 delivers systematically improved agreement with experimental data or high-accuracy references for crystals, molecules, and surfaces, outperforming PBE-based DFT calculations. Crucially, in long-time molecular dynamics simulations that are computationally impractical with DFT, PFP v8 predicts melting points with an average error of approximately 130 K, halving the error relative to PBE-trained models. These results establish that uMLIPs can move beyond the limitations of their training approximations and achieve substantially improved agreement with experiment across diverse chemical domains, further narrowing the gap between simulation and reality.

</details>


### [137] [Micropatterning photopolymerizable hydrogels for diffusion studies using pillar arrays or photomasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11065)
*Sevgi Onal,Edmondo Battista,Hilal Nasir,Fabio Formiggini,Valentina Mollo,Raffaele Vecchione,Paolo Netti*

Method: 开发了两种平台：第一种采用多通道微流控设计，通过柱阵列分离相邻通道，引导定制制备的光聚合水凝胶流动，实现光聚合的定位。第二种通过微铣削250微米厚PMMA基板并结合铂涂层，制作具有不透明和透明区域的光掩模，用于PEGDA-PEG水凝胶的光基聚合。

Abstract: In situ polymerization and micropatterning of hydrogels on-chip opens the potential for many applications such as tracking and controlling the diffusion of molecules, stimulants, inhibitors, as well as nutrients and drugs, from their source to a target. In the first platform that we introduce here, the design has multiple adjacent microfluidic channels separated with pillar arrays shaping the flow of our custom-prepared photopolymerizable hydrogels and thus enabling the localization of photopolymerization. In the second platform, a photomask formation has been achieved by coupling the micro-milling of 250-\textmu m thickness of PMMA substrate with Platinum (Pt)-coating onto the PMMA mask. In this way the design was obtained to have opaque and transparent regions for light-based polymerization of the PEGDA-PEG hydrogels. The developed method of in situ polymerization of the hydrogel on-chip through photomask has enabled direct transfer of the design of interest to the pre-hydrogel in channel. Next, the developed platforms will be further used to test various compositions of photopolymerizable hydrogels and track and control the diffusion of molecules across hydrogel interfaces. The micropatterning methods and platforms developed here could be tailored to device design and development needs in various application fields from molecular transport to biosensing to electronic devices.

### [138] [ChemFit: A concurrent framework for model parametrization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11769)
*Moritz Sallermann,Amrita Goswami,Hannes Jónsson,Elvar Ö. Jónsson,Jorge R. Espinosa*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: ChemFit是一个用于计算化学和物理中参数优化的Python框架，能够处理昂贵、噪声、不可微或异质的目标函数，支持大规模并发评估并与梯度无关的黑盒优化算法协同工作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算化学和物理中的参数优化常面临目标函数评估昂贵、有噪声、不可微或由独立模拟产生的异质贡献等问题。现有模拟引擎与参数优化库的接口通常繁琐，特别是在需要并发运行昂贵模拟时。

Method: ChemFit框架提供了异质目标项（heterogeneous objective terms）、基于文件和内存的量值评估、以及对目标组件和参数猜测的显式并发控制等抽象。该框架设计用于与梯度无关的黑盒优化算法（gradient-free and black box optimization algorithms）协同工作。

Result: 通过两个应用案例展示了ChemFit的通用性：(1) 使用分子动力学模拟（molecular-dynamics simulations）根据液态氩在温度和压力范围内的实验密度数据确定Lennard-Jones参数；(2) 基于密度泛函理论计算（density functional theory calculations）得到的小冰团簇结构，参数化H2O的极化力场（polarizable force-field）。

Conclusion: ChemFit框架实现了可扩展、可重复且与优化器无关的参数拟合，为计算化学和物理中的复杂优化问题提供了灵活的解决方案。

Abstract: Parameter optimization in computational chemistry and physics often involves objective functions that are expensive to evaluate, noisy, non-differentiable, or composed of heterogeneous contributions originating from separate simulations. Gradient-free and black box optimization algorithms are powerful tools which are particularly well-suited to solving such optimization problems. However, interfacing simulation engines and parameter optimization libraries can be cumbersome, especially if simulations are expensive and need to be run concurrently. Here, we introduce ChemFit, a flexible Python framework for the definition, composition, and massively concurrent evaluation of simulation-based objective functions, which is designed to operate in conjunction with these algorithms. This framework provides abstractions for heterogeneous objective terms, file-based and in-memory quantity evaluation, and explicit control over concurrency across both objective components and parameter guesses. We demonstrate the versatility of ChemFit for different applications such as: (i) determination of Lennard-Jones parameters for liquid Argon from experimental density data over a range in temperature and pressure, using molecular-dynamics simulations, and (ii) the parameterization of a polarizable force-field for H2O against the structure of small ice clusters obtained from density functional theory calculations. These examples illustrate how ChemFit enables scalable, reproducible, and optimizer-agnostic parameter fitting.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.supr-con'></div>
