### [139] [Progress of ambient-pressure superconductivity in bilayer nickelate thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11235)
*Wenyuan Qiu,Dao-Xin Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文综述了双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇薄膜在常压超导性方面的最新进展，重点关注外延应变工程如何实现常压超导、实验表征、Tc提升以及理论研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该综述旨在总结双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇薄膜在常压超导性方面的最新进展，这是在块体La₃Ni₂O₇高压超导性发现后的重要突破。研究关注如何通过外延应变工程实现常压超导，为探索高温超导性提供可调控平台。

Method: 采用外延应变工程（epitaxial strain engineering）技术，通过SrLaAlO₄等衬底施加压缩应变来稳定La₃Ni₂O₇薄膜的超导性。同时综述了包括角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）在内的实验表征方法，以及相关的理论研究进展。

Result: 压缩应变成功实现了La₃Ni₂O₇薄膜的常压超导性，但ARPES测量显示存在相互矛盾的费米面拓扑结构。研究在提高超导转变温度Tc方面取得进展，并通过理论研究探讨了电子结构和配对对称性。

Conclusion: 这些进展确立了双层镍酸盐薄膜作为探索高温超导性的高度可调控且前景广阔的平台。综合研究表明，应变工程是实现常压超导的关键因素，为未来高温超导研究提供了新的材料体系。

Abstract: This review summarizes recent progress of ambient-pressure superconductivity in bilayer nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ thin films, a major advancement following the discovery of high-pressure superconductivity in bulk La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$. First, we explain how epitaxial strain engineering enables ambient-pressure superconductivity in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ thin films, with compressive strain from substrates like SrLaAlO$_4$ stabilizing superconductivity. Next, we review experimental characterizations of related systems, with particular emphasis on ARPES measurements that have shown conflicting Fermi surface topologies. We then discuss progress in increasing the superconducting transition temperature $T_c$. Finally, we summarize theoretical studies of the electronic structure and pairing symmetry of La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ thin films. Together, these advances establish bilayer nickelate thin films as a highly tunable and promising platform for exploring high-$T_c$ superconductivity.

</details>


### [140] [Pseudo Point Nodal Superconducting Gap in Spin-Triplet UTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11278)
*S. Hosoi,K. Imamura,M. M. Bordelon,E. D. Bauer,S. M. Thomas,F. Ronning,P. F. S. Rosa,R. Movshovich,I. Vekhter,Y. Matsuda*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过高分辨率热导率测量揭示了UTe₂超导体的能隙结构，发现其具有完全能隙态（fully gapped state）与赝点节点结构（pseudo point-nodal structure），排除了非幺正配对对称性混合（non-unitary mixing of pairing symmetries）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: UTe₂作为罕见的自旋三重态配对（spin-triplet pairing）超导体，其能隙结构（gap structure）特别是点节点（point nodes）存在相互矛盾的报道，阻碍了对序参量对称性（order parameter symmetry）和拓扑性质的理解。

Method: 研究采用高分辨率热导率测量（high-resolution thermal conductivity measurements）技术，在低至约50 mK的温度下对高质量UTe₂单晶进行体相定向输运（bulk directional transport）分析，重点关注b轴热导率κ_b/T的行为。

Result: b轴热导率κ_b/T在T→0时表现出可忽略的剩余电导率，其温度依赖性与沿b轴的小超导能隙一致。磁场下κ_b/T仅显示弱场致增强，且在H∥a时低场处出现阈值场（threshold field），其特征为表征准粒子输运变化的扭折（kink）。

Conclusion: 测量特征强烈表明UTe₂具有完全能隙态与赝点节点结构，其中能隙最小值接近但不为零。估算沿b轴的最小能隙Δ_min/Δ_0∼0.1，该不寻常能隙结构为理解自旋三重态超导体的配对机制和拓扑性质提供了关键见解。

Abstract: The unconventional superconductor UTe$_2$ represents a rare example of spin-triplet pairing with potentially topologically protected quantum states. However, conflicting reports on its gap structure, particularly regarding point nodes, have hindered understanding of the order parameter symmetry and topological properties. Here we report high-resolution thermal conductivity measurements on high-quality UTe$_2$ single crystals down to ~50 mK that resolve the gap anisotropy through bulk directional transport. The $b$-axis thermal conductivity $κ_b/T$ exhibits negligible residual conductivity as $T \to 0$, and its temperature dependence is consistent with a small superconducting energy gap along the $b$-axis. Under magnetic fields, the residual $κ_b/T$ shows only weak field-induced enhancement. Remarkably, a threshold field emerges at low fields for $H \parallel a$, characterized by a kink that signals a change in quasiparticle transport normal to the field. Below the threshold, $κ_b/T$ remains isotropic for all field orientations, whereas strong anisotropy between transport along and normal to the field develops above it. These signatures strongly suggest that UTe$_2$ exhibits a fully gapped state with a pseudo point-nodal structure, where gap minima approach but never reach zero. We estimate the minimal gap $Δ_{min}/Δ_0 \sim 0.1$ along the $b$-axis, where $Δ_0$ is the characteristic superconducting gap. This unusual gap structure provides crucial insights into the pairing mechanism and topology of this spin-triplet superconductor and excludes non-unitary mixing of pairing symmetries.

</details>


### [141] [Quantum Oscillations and Superconductivity in YPtBi Under Pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11464)
*Jared Z. Dans,Prathum Saraf,Lillian Jirousek,Carsyn L. Mueller,Chandra Shekhar,Claudia Felser,Johnpierre Paglione*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过高压磁输运和舒布尼科夫-德哈斯效应测量，发现压力导致YPtBi向更绝缘行为转变，表明能带反转减弱和拓扑性质可能被调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: YPtBi作为拓扑半金属（topological semimetal）因其新颖的超导和正常态性质受到关注。其强自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）导致的能带反转（band inversion）允许费米能级附近存在j=3/2准粒子，这些准粒子可能形成角动量高于单重态或三重态的库珀对（Cooper pairs）。

Method: 对高质量YPtBi样品进行高达P=2.08 GPa的高压磁输运（high-pressure magnetotransport）和舒布尼科夫-德哈斯效应（Shubnikov-de Haas effect）测量。

Result: 随着压力增加，观察到低温电阻率趋向更绝缘行为，同时量子振荡（quantum oscillation）振幅被抑制。上临界场（upper critical field）降低和丁格尔温度（Dingle temperature）显著增加，这些变化表明能带反转减弱和YPtBi拓扑性质可能被调控。

Conclusion: 压力诱导的变化指向能带反转减弱和YPtBi拓扑性质的潜在调控，表明压力是理解其他相关半赫斯勒化合物（half-Heusler compounds）拓扑性质的有用工具。

Abstract: The topological semimetal YPtBi has attracted considerable attention, owing to its novel superconducting and normal state properties. A strong band inversion from spin-orbit coupling allows the existence of $j=3/2$ quasiparticles near the Fermi level, which form Cooper pairs with angular momentum potentially higher than single or triplet states. In this report, we present high-pressure magnetotransport and Shubnikov-de Haas effect measurements on high-quality YPtBi up to $P = 2.08$ GPa. As a function of pressure, we observe a trend toward more insulating resistivity at low temperatures concomitant with a suppression of quantum oscillation amplitude. Together with a decrease of the upper critical field and significant increase in the Dingle temperature, the pressure-induced changes point to a weakening of the band inversion and potential tuning of the topological nature of YPtBi, suggesting pressure as a useful tool for understanding the nature of topology in other related half-Heusler compounds.

</details>


### [142] [Double-twisted surface spectrum from hybridized Majorana Kramers pairs and wallpaper fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11637)
*Kaito Yoda,Ai Yamakage*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该理论研究具有p4g壁纸群对称性的拓扑非对称晶体绝缘体中壁纸费米子的超导表面态，发现A1u表示下壁纸费米子与两对马约拉纳克拉默斯对共存，产生双扭曲表面态和四个态密度峰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究壁纸费米子（wallpaper fermions）——受p4g壁纸群保护的拓扑非对称晶体绝缘体表面准粒子——的超导表面态特性，旨在理解其独特的对称性约束和拓扑性质。

Method: 基于空间群P4/mbm（No. 127）的紧束缚模型进行理论分析，结合壁纸群p4g的对称性分析和一维拓扑不变量计算，系统研究允许的四种在位配对势。

Result: 对于A1u表示，壁纸费米子与两对马约拉纳克拉默斯对（Majorana Kramers pairs）共存，其杂化产生双扭曲表面态（double-twisted surface state）并在表面态密度中形成四个峰；镜像陈数（mirror Chern number）为零，表明系统实现了无镜像螺旋性表面态。

Conclusion: 超导壁纸费米子展现出独特的无镜像螺旋性表面态，这使其区别于其他超导拓扑（晶体）绝缘体如Cu_xBi_2Se_3和Sn_{1-x}In_xTe，揭示了壁纸群对称性在塑造拓扑超导表面态中的关键作用。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the superconducting surface states of wallpaper fermions, which are surface quasiparticles of topological nonsymmorphic crystalline insulators protected by a wallpaper group $p4g$ symmetry, based on a tight-binding model for the space group $P4/mbm$ (No. 127). A symmetry-based analysis shows that four types of on-site pair potentials are allowed. Using the symmetries of the wallpaper group $p4g$ and the one-dimensional topological invariants, we clarify that for the $\mathrm{A_{1u}}$ representation, wallpaper fermions and two Majorana Kramers pairs coexist, and hybridization between them give rise to a double-twisted surface state and produces four peaks in the surface density of states. We further find that the mirror Chern number vanishes, indicating that our system realizes mirror-helicity-free surface states. This distinguishes superconducting wallpaper fermions from the other superconducting topological (crystalline) insulators, such as $\mathrm{Cu}_x\mathrm{Bi}_2\mathrm{Se}_3$ and $\mathrm{Sn}_{1-x}\mathrm{In}_x\mathrm{Te}$.

</details>


### [143] [Theoretical proposal of superconductivity in hole-doped reduced bilayer nickelate La3Ni2O6: a manifestation of orbital-space bilayer model with incipient bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11771)
*Shu Kamiyama,Reo Kohno,Yuto Hoshi,Kensei Ushio,Daiki Nakaoka,Hirofumi Sakakibara,Kazuhiko Kuroki*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究提出双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₆可作为轨道空间双层模型（OSBM）描述的超导体候选材料，其s±波超导性由轨道间相互作用驱动，在空穴掺杂条件下实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索多轨道Hubbard模型与双层Hubbard模型之间的对应关系，并寻找可由轨道空间双层模型（orbital-space bilayer model, OSBM）描述的新型超导体候选材料。

Method: 基于第一性原理计算构建紧束缚模型（tight-binding model），获得Ni d轨道间的能级偏移ΔE；采用涨落交换近似（fluctuation exchange approximation）计算超导性质；同时研究原子替代和压力下晶体结构的能量与动力学稳定性。

Result: La₃Ni₂O₆中由于缺少外层顶端氧原子，导致Ni dₓ²₋ᵧ²轨道与其他d轨道间存在大的能级偏移ΔE；计算表明在初生带（incipient-band）情况下，轨道间相互作用驱动s±波超导性出现，超导能隙函数在dₓ²₋ᵧ²与其他d轨道带间改变符号。

Conclusion: La₃Ni₂O₆可作为OSBM描述的超导体候选材料，其配对机制与La₃Ni₂O₇完全不同，展示了轨道空间双层模型在新型超导体设计中的潜力。

Abstract: A correspondence exists between the multi-orbital Hubbard model and the bilayer Hubbard model, in which superconductivity is optimized in an incipient-band regime in both cases. In the multi-orbital system, the orbital level offset $ΔE$ plays a role analogous to the interlayer hopping in bilayer systems, and superconductivity is enhanced for large $ΔE$. We refer to such a multi-orbital model as an orbital-space bilayer model (OSBM). In this study, we theoretically propose that a reduced bilayer nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_6$ can be a candidate for a superconductor described by OSBM when an appropriate amount of holes is doped. By constructing a tight-binding model based on first-principles calculations, a large $ΔE$ between the Ni $d_{x^2-y^2}$ and the other $d$ orbitals is obtained due to the absence of outer apical oxygens. Furthermore, our fluctuation exchange approximation calculations indicate the emergence of $s\pm$-wave superconductivity driven by interorbital interactions in an incipient-band situation, where the superconducting gap function changes its sign between the $d_{x^2-y^2}$ and other $d$ orbital bands. We also investigate the energetic and dynamical stability of the crystal structure under atomic substitution and pressure. Although La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ and La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_6$ share a similar chemical formula, our study shows that an entirely different pairing mechanism can take place in the latter.

</details>


### [144] [Multiple Magnetic Transitions in the Trilayer Nickelate Pr$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$ Revealed by Muon-Spin Rotation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11823)
*Rustem Khasanov,Thomas J. Hicken,Zurab Guguchia,Shangxiong Huangfu,Hubertus Luetkens,Ekaterina Pomjakushina,Vladimir Pomjakushin,Andreas Schilling,Igor Plokhikh,Dariusz J. Gawryluk*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过μ子自旋转动/弛豫（μSR）技术，在三层Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐Pr₄Ni₃O₁₀中发现了三个磁相变，并研究了静水压力对这些相变的影响。自旋密度波（SDW）有序在压力下被线性抑制，表明压缩会逐渐削弱该不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究三层Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐Pr₄Ni₃O₁₀的磁有序行为，特别是在环境压力和静水压力下的磁相变特性。通过μ子自旋转动/弛豫（μSR）技术探索该材料的复杂磁相图。

Method: 采用μ子自旋转动/弛豫（μSR）技术，在环境压力下以及高达2.2 GPa的静水压力下对Pr₄Ni₃O₁₀样品进行研究。通过弱横向场测量探测磁相变的热滞后现象。

Result: 在环境压力下识别出三个磁相变：自旋密度波（SDW）有序起始于T_SDW ≈ 158 K，中间温度转变T* ≈ 90-100 K，以及低温转变T_SDW^Pr ≈ 25-27 K。T_SDW^Pr转变伴随着磁结构的显著重构。静水压力线性抑制T_SDW，抑制速率为dT_SDW/dp = -4.9(1) K/GPa，同时降低有序Ni磁矩，速率为dlnM/dp = -2.0(5)×10⁻² GPa⁻¹。

Conclusion: 静水压力导致自旋密度波（SDW）不稳定性逐渐减弱。T_SDW转变表现出弱一级相变特征，具有有限的热滞后现象。Pr亚晶格的有序化增强了层间相干性，导致低温下磁结构的重构。

Abstract: A muon-spin rotation/relaxation ($μ$SR) study of the trilayer Ruddlesden--Popper nickelate Pr$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$ was performed at ambient pressure and under hydrostatic pressure up to 2.2 GPa. Three magnetic transitions were identified at ambient pressure: the onset of spin-density-wave (SDW) order at $T_{\rm SDW} \simeq 158$ K, an intermediate-temperature transition at $T^{\ast} \simeq 90$--100 K, and a low-temperature transition at $T_{\rm SDW}^{\rm Pr} \simeq 25$--27 K. While the intermediate transition at $T^{\ast}$ induces only minor changes in the internal-field distribution, the transition at $T_{\rm SDW}^{\rm Pr}$ is accompanied by a pronounced reconstruction of the magnetic structure, consistent with previous reports attributing enhanced interlayer coherence to the ordering of the Pr sublattice. The high-temperature transition at $T_{\rm SDW}$ is characterized by the sharp development of static internal magnetic fields with a narrow transition width of $0.65(4)$ K. Weak-transverse-field measurements reveal a finite thermal hysteresis of $0.27(6)$ K, with $T_{\rm SDW}^{\rm warming} > T_{\rm SDW}^{\rm cooling}$, indicating weakly first-order-like behavior. Hydrostatic pressure suppresses $T_{\rm SDW}$ linearly and reduces the ordered Ni magnetic moment $M$, with corresponding rates of ${\rm d}T_{\rm SDW}/{\rm d}p = -4.9(1)$ K/GPa and ${\rm d}\ln M/{\rm d}p = -2.0(5)\times10^{-2}$ GPa$^{-1}$, respectively, thereby demonstrating a gradual weakening of the spin-density-wave instability under compression.

</details>


### [145] [Phase stiffness in flat-band superconductors with nodal pairing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11986)
*A. A. Zyuzin,A. Yu. Zyuzin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 研究双带系统中动量依赖杂化（momentum-dependent hybridization）对Bogoliubov准粒子谱的影响，发现平带准粒子谱中可能出现抛物线节点，导致超导相刚度在低温下呈现二次温度依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有动量依赖杂化的双带系统中Bogoliubov准粒子谱的特性，特别关注色散带与平带之间的相互作用对超导性质的影响。

Method: 分析具有动量依赖杂化的双带系统，其中包含色散带与平带之间的杂化以及带内Cooper配对（intraband Cooper pairing）的相互作用。

Result: 发现平带准粒子谱中可能出现抛物线节点（parabolic node），导致超导相刚度（superconducting phase stiffness）在低温下呈现二次温度依赖关系；非磁性无序（nonmagnetic disorder）会诱导Machida-Shibata深亚能隙共振（deep subgap resonances）。

Conclusion: 平带超导性对无序敏感，动量依赖杂化与带内Cooper配对的相互作用能够产生独特的准粒子谱特征，影响超导相刚度的温度依赖行为。

Abstract: We study Bogoliubov quasiparticle spectrum in a two-band system with momentum-dependent hybridization between a dispersive band and a flat band. The interplay between the interband mixing and intraband Cooper pairing may give rise to a parabolic node in the spectrum of flat band quasiparticles, resulting in a quadratic temperature dependence of the superconducting phase stiffness at low temperatures. We also comment that nonmagnetic disorder induces Machida-Shibata deep subgap resonances suggesting the sensitivity of flat-band superconductivity to disorder.

</details>


### [146] [Quantum interference in a twisted high-Tc SQUID senses emergent interfacial order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12092)
*Amit Basu,Samrat Ash,Ritajit Kundu,Neha Bhatia,Sakshi Nema,Tejaswini Gawade,Khushabu Agrawal,Abhishek Das,Joydip Sarkar,Amit Shah,Ruta Kulkarni,Digambar A. Jangade,Arijit Kundu,A. Thamizhavel,Mandar M. Deshmukh*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过构建基于扭曲铜氧化物超导体界面的超导量子干涉器件（SQUID），首次观测到界面手性超导序的π相位差，并实现了接近77K的高性能磁通传感器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过扭曲和堆叠范德华材料构建人工系统已成为探索涌现量子现象的重要平台。高质量扭曲界面的制备为研究扭曲铜氧化物超导体中尚未充分探索的界面超导序提供了独特机会。

Method: 研究团队制备了利用Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊δ（一种高温铜氧化物超导体）扭曲界面的超导量子干涉器件（SQUID）。通过测量开关电流和微分电阻的磁场调制，分析SQUID两个约瑟夫森结臂之间的相位关系。

Result: 观测到SQUID两个约瑟夫森结臂之间存在π相位差，反映了手性超导序（chiral superconducting order）的存在。同时发现库珀对（Cooper pairs）的协同隧穿和时间反演对称性破缺的涌现超导序。该SQUID在接近77K时实现了约1.5 μΦ₀/√Hz的磁通噪声灵敏度。

Conclusion: 利用扭曲界面稳定新型超导序并通过量子干涉进行探测，为理解非常规超导体的微观起源开辟了新途径。该SQUID架构适用于研究其他系统界面处的电荷输运机制和超导序对称性，展示了超越铜氧化物超导体的广泛应用前景。

Abstract: Engineering artificial systems by twisting and stacking van der Waals materials has proven to be an excellent platform for exploring emergent quantum phenomena that can be significantly different from the constituents. Recent advances in the fabrication of high-quality twisted interfaces provide a unique opportunity to study the little-explored interfacial superconducting order in twisted cuprate superconductors. In our work, we fabricate superconducting quantum interference devices (SQUID) that utilize the twisted interface of $\mathrm{Bi_2Sr_2CaCu_2O_{8+δ}}$, a high-Tc cuprate superconductor. By measuring the magnetic field modulation of switching current and differential resistance, we find a $\mathrmπ$ phase difference between the two Josephson junction arms of the SQUID reflecting chiral superconducting order -- a crucial aspect inaccessible to single Josephson junction devices of the past. Our observations also indicate co-tunneling of the Cooper pairs and a time-reversal symmetry-broken emergent superconducting order. Additionally, these SQUIDs are well suited for use as state-of-the-art flux sensors close to 77 K, achieving a flux noise sensitivity of $\sim$1.5 $\mathrm{μΦ_0/\sqrt{Hz}}$. Stabilizing new superconducting orders using twisted interfaces and probing them using quantum interference opens new avenues to understanding the microscopic origin of unconventional superconductors. Our SQUID architecture is suitable for investigating the charge transport mechanisms and the symmetry of superconducting order at the interfaces of other systems, reflecting the broad applicability beyond cuprate superconductors.

</details>


### [147] [A superconducting half-dome in bilayer nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12196)
*Yidi Liu,Bai Yang Wang,Jiarui Li,Yaoju Tarn,Lopa Bhatt,Michael Colletta,Yi-Ming Wu,Cheng-Tai Kuo,Jun-Sik Lee,Berit H. Goodge,David A. Muller,Zhi-Xun Shen,Srinivas Raghu,Harold Y. Hwang,Yijun Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究报道了在压缩应变双层镍酸盐薄膜中，通过连续调控氧化学计量比，观察到了超导半穹顶结构，揭示了氧间隙与氧空位对超导性的不同调控机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解关联电子系统中超导性的产生与崩溃是凝聚态物理的核心挑战。双层镍酸盐作为高温超导体家族的新成员，其氧化学计量比的显著敏感性为调控电子相提供了有效控制参数。

Method: 研究采用压缩应变双层镍酸盐薄膜，通过连续调控氧化学计量比（oxygen stoichiometry）作为控制参数，系统研究不同稀土组合及有无碱土金属掺杂样品的超导行为。

Result: 观察到超导半穹顶结构：从最佳超导态开始，增加氧化学计量比逐渐抑制超导性向金属相转变，而减少氧化学计量比则驱动颗粒超导体-绝缘体转变，同时保持超导起始温度不变。该半穹顶结构源于氧间隙与氧空位的不同作用机制。

Conclusion: 超导半穹顶结构在不同稀土组合及有无碱土金属掺杂的样品中均一致出现，揭示了双层镍酸盐相图的普遍特征，为理解关联电子系统中的超导调控机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: Understanding how superconductivity emerges and collapses in correlated electron systems remains a central challenge in condensed matter physics. As a recently discovered member of the high temperature superconductor family, bilayer nickelates provide a new opportunity for examining this problem. Their pronounced sensitivity to oxygen stoichiometry, while posing challenges for stabilizing superconductivity, simultaneously offers an effective control parameter for tuning electronic phases. Here we report a superconducting half-dome in compressively strained bilayer nickelate thin films as a function of continuous tuning of oxygen stoichiometry. Starting from an optimally superconducting state, increasing oxygen stoichiometry gradually suppresses superconductivity toward a metallic phase, whereas decreasing oxygen stoichiometry drives a granular superconductor-to-insulator transition while leaving the superconducting onset intact. This half-dome structure can be understood to arise from the contrasting roles played by interstitial oxygen versus oxygen vacancies - namely the dominance of doping versus scattering. Notably, the half-dome emerges consistently across samples with different rare-earth combinations, with or without alkaline-earth doping, revealing a general feature of the bilayer nickelate phase diagram.

### [148] [Integrable Free and Interacting Fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11172)
*Zhao Zhang*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一维量子系统中自由费米子与相互作用费米子的可积性条件，定义了比Maassarani的"自由费米子代数"更广义但比精确可解量子模型中自由费米子更特殊的自由费米子概念，并建立了从局域哈密顿量构造自由费米子R矩阵的迭代求解方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在建立一维量子系统中自由费米子与相互作用费米子的可积性条件，提供比现有定义更精确的自由费米子概念框架，并探索如何通过变形操作从自由系统构造可积的相互作用系统。

Method: 通过要求R矩阵同时满足Yang-Baxter方程和Shastry的装饰星三角关系来定义自由费米子，提出迭代求解自由费米子R矩阵的实用程序，并利用共轭算子对自由哈密顿量进行变形以描述相互作用系统。

Result: 发现自由费米子R矩阵具有差分形式和共轭对称性，建立了判断变形后系统是否保持可积性的进一步准则，并以Hubbard模型和纵向场中的XY模型为例展示了该方法的应用。

Conclusion: 论文成功建立了更精确的自由费米子定义框架，提供了从局域哈密顿量构造自由费米子R矩阵的系统方法，并阐明了通过共轭变形从自由系统生成可积相互作用系统的条件，为研究一维量子系统的可积性提供了新工具。

Abstract: Integrability conditions on local Hamiltonians for one-dimensional quantum systems to be free and interacting fermions are introduced. The definition of free fermion is the simultaneous satisfaction of the Yang-Baxter equation and Shastry's decorated star-triangle relation by the $R$-matrix, which is more general than the previous `free-fermion algebra' by Maassarani and more special than free fermions as in the context of exactly solvable quantum models or integrable classical two-dimensional vertex models dual to quantum spin chains. Free fermionic $R$-matrices are of the difference form and have a conjugation symmetry. These free Hamiltonians may sometimes be deformed by the conjugation operator to describe an integrable interacting system with non-relativistic $R$-matrices, as are the cases of the Hubbard model and the XY model in a longitudinal field. A further criterion is obtain on precisely when such deformations remain integrable. A practical procedure is proposed to iteratively solve the free fermionic $R$-matrices from local Hamiltonians, which can be used to construct non-relativistic $R$-matrices if the conditions are met.

### [149] [Quantitative 3D imaging of highly distorted micro-crystals using Bragg ptychography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11584)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 布拉格相干衍射成像（BCDI）在具有强应变不均匀性的微晶中无法可靠地恢复相位，这限制了其应用范围。需要开发能够处理大晶格畸变的新方法。

Method: 采用三维布拉格叠层成像（three-dimensional Bragg ptychography, 3DBP）方法，通过实验测量与数值测试相结合的方式，比较了3DBP与BCDI两种方法的性能极限。

Result: 3DBP能够容忍的晶格畸变程度超过BCDI六倍以上。对于弱畸变晶体，3DBP能产生更平滑的振幅和相位场，并减少短长度尺度的伪影。

Abstract: Bragg coherent diffraction imaging (BCDI) fails to reliably retrieve phases in micro-crystals exhibiting strong strain inhomogeneities, which restricts its applicability. Here we show that three-dimensional Bragg ptychography (3DBP) overcomes this limitation by enabling stable inversion for large lattice distortions. Using a combination of experimental measurements and numerical tests, we compare the performance limits of the two approaches and demonstrate that 3DBP tolerates lattice distortions more than six times larger than BCDI. We also establish the sensitivity of both methods on a weakly distorted crystal, for which 3DBP yields smoother amplitude and phase fields with reduced short-length-scale artifacts. 3DBP thus provides a reliable route for imaging micro-crystals with large lattice distortions, expanding the scope of coherent X-ray Bragg microscopy to strongly deformed systems.

### [150] [Hidden Light Scalars in Heavy-Ion Collisions: A Phenomenological Resolution to High-$p_T$ Quarkonium Anomalies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11097)
*Yi Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出通过引入质量为9.40 GeV的暗标量粒子（dark scalar φ）来解释重离子碰撞中Υ(1S)态在高横动量下出现的异常平台现象，该机制能同时解释核修正因子平坦化、椭圆流消失、夸克偶素极化难题，并规避历史低横动量双μ子搜索。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出引入质量为约9.40 GeV的暗标量粒子φ，该粒子位于严格的运动学合并窗口内。研究表明，硬散射暗标量与相对论性QCD（Non-Relativistic QCD, NRQCD）色八重态产生共享p_T^{-4}渐近碎裂标度，从而在高动量下提供恒定的理论暗分数。

Result: 从异常R_AA平台提取的暗分数约为13.8%，这一单一参数能一致地解释多个现象：R_AA平坦化、包容性v_2向零稀释、缓解长期存在的夸克偶素极化难题，并通过动态探测器分辨率阈值自然规避历史低p_T双μ子搜索。

Abstract: The suppression of heavy quarkonia in heavy-ion collisions is a well-established signature of Quark-Gluon Plasma (QGP) formation. However, recent LHC measurements of the $Υ(1S)$ state exhibit an anomalous high-$p_T$ plateau in the nuclear modification factor ($R_{AA}$) and a vanishing elliptic flow ($v_2$), challenging standard QCD transport models. We propose a viable mechanism to account for these observations by introducing a minimal dark scalar $φ$ situated within a strict kinematic merging window ($m_φ\approx 9.40$~GeV). We demonstrate that the shared $p_T^{-4}$ asymptotic fragmentation scaling between the hard-scattered dark scalar and Non-Relativistic QCD (NRQCD) color-octet production provides a constant theoretical dark fraction at high momenta. By extracting this fraction ($C_φ\approx 13.8\%$) from the anomalous $R_{AA}$ plateau, we establish a consistent phenomenological correlation: a single parameter addresses the $R_{AA}$ flattening, dilutes the inclusive $v_2$ toward zero, mitigates the long-standing quarkonium polarization puzzle, and naturally evades historical low-$p_T$ dimuon searches via a dynamic detector resolution threshold. We emphasize that future high-precision measurements of the dimuon mass lineshape at extreme transverse momenta are crucial for testing this paradigm.

Conclusion: 功能量子色动力学方法为理解QCD相结构，特别是高密度区域的新相现象提供了有价值的框架，能够预测新相的出现位置和实验特征，并与格点QCD结果进行系统校准。

Abstract: We provide a short review of the progress made in the past decade with functional QCD in the description of the phase structure of QCD. We summarise the most important technical aspects of the framework, discuss strategies for truncations and address the problem of systematic error estimates. We detail efforts to gauge the approach systematically with lattice QCD at zero chemical potential, also including the physics of the Columbia plot at non-physical quark masses. Our main focus is, however, the high density regime of QCD. We address the predictive power of the functional approach for the appearance of new phases beyond the chiral crossover regime for chemical potentials $μ_B/T\geq 4.5$. The onset of this regime may be signalled by a critical end point of the crossover line but may also involve a moat regime or the emergence of an instability that indicates an inhomogeneous phase. Respective results include estimates for the location of the onset of new phases, and predictions for their experimental signatures.

In the first section, we use state-of-the-art machine learning methods, such as deep neural networks and the Particle Transformer model architecture, to predict baryon masses directly from their quantum numbers, based on experimental information on hadrons from the Particle Data Group (PDG). The results obtained from both approaches demonstrate strong agreement with experimental data where available and make predictions for a number of unobserved states, including higher radial excitations. ### [154] [Quantum tomography of $H \to ZZ, WW$ beyond leading order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11288)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究结果表明，无论是有效自旋分析能力还是光子否决都不足以使朴素构造的自旋密度算符保持物理性，必须扣除高阶修正才能进行一致的量子层析成像。同时发现，与当前实验数据的不确定性相比，这些修正相对较小。

Conclusion: 研究结论强调，进行一致的量子层析成像必须扣除高阶修正，并指出在H→WW过程中观测宇称破坏效应（parity-violating effects）的显著可能性。

Abstract: We revisit quantum tomography of $H \to ZZ$ and $H \to WW$ in the presence of higher-order corrections. We verify that neither the use of an effective spin analysing power (only for $ZZ$) or a photon veto are sufficient to render the naively-constructed spin density operators physical. A subtraction of higher-order corrections is thus necessary to perform consistent quantum tomography. Such corrections are small when compared to expected experimental uncertainties with current data. As a by-product, we point out the striking possibility to observe parity-violating effects in $H \to WW$.

### [155] [Unified Flavor: Lattice Quantization, Chain Locality, and a Dynamical Origin of Hierarchical Yukawas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11341)
*Vernon Barger*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Unified Flavor (UF) 框架将B-晶格味层次结构与TeV能标矢量费米子链的动态实现相结合，通过离散晶格指数和多重信使结构自然产生夸克质量层次、CKM混合和CP破坏，同时解决强CP问题并扩展到轻子扇区。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在统一解释标准模型中的味物理（flavor physics）问题，包括夸克质量层次、CKM混合矩阵（Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa mixing）和CP破坏（CP violation）的起源。同时框架试图将这些问题与强CP问题（strong CP problem）的解决相统一。

Method: 提出Unified Flavor (UF)框架，基于B-晶格味层次结构（B-lattice flavor hierarchy），通过TeV能标矢量费米子链（vectorlike fermion chains）动态实现。Yukawa耦合由离散晶格指数生成，有效Yukawa矩阵元作为最近邻矢量夸克链的代数路径和（algebraic path sums）。采用多重信使结构（multi-messenger structure），每个Yukawa矩阵元接收多个链构型的相干贡献。

Result: 成功再现所有六个夸克质量，其O(1)系数基本为1。CKM混合层次和CP相位结构自然从晶格指数代数和多重信使干涉中涌现。链局域性（chain locality）同时抑制了危险的味改变中性流（FCNCs）并满足电弱精度约束。框架扩展到轻子扇区，再现带电轻子质量层次、正序中微子谱（normal-ordered neutrino spectrum）和PMNS混合。

Conclusion: Unified Flavor框架通过离散规范对称性统一了味物理、CP破坏和强CP问题，同时保护了Peccei-Quinn轴子质量。矢量夸克质量在multi-TeV范围，可在HL-LHC探测。轻子扇区预测的二分位相-δ关联可在DUNE和Hyper-Kamiokande实验检验。

Abstract: We present Unified Flavor (UF), a framework that synthesizes the $B$-lattice flavor hierarchy with a dynamical realization based on TeV-scale vectorlike fermion (VLF) chains. Hierarchical Yukawa couplings arise from discrete ninths-quantized lattice exponents enforced by a single flavon $Φ$ with $ε\equiv\langleΦ\rangle/Λ=1/B$, $B=75/14$. Effective Yukawa entries are generated as algebraic path sums along nearest-neighbor chains of vectorlike quarks (VLQs), factorizing into entry, chain-propagation, and exit amplitudes controlled by the discrete gauge charges. A multi-messenger structure -- in which each Yukawa entry receives coherent contributions from several chain configurations -- generates O(1) complex coefficients whose phases are the physical origin of CP violation. We derive a general chain-inversion theorem, perform systematic perturbative diagonalization of both up- and down-type Yukawa textures, and show that the Cabibbo--Kobayashi--Maskawa (CKM) mixing hierarchy and CP-phase structure emerge naturally from the lattice exponent algebra and multi-messenger interference. All six quark masses are reproduced with O(1) coefficients that are essentially unity. The chain locality simultaneously suppresses dangerous flavor-changing neutral currents (FCNCs) and satisfies electroweak precision constraints, while requiring VLQs with masses in the multi-TeV range accessible at the High-Luminosity Large Hadron Collider (HL-LHC). The same discrete gauge symmetry that enforces the lattice structure also protects the Peccei--Quinn axion quality, unifying flavor, CP violation, and the strong CP problem. The framework extends to the lepton sector, reproducing charged-lepton mass hierarchies, the normal-ordered neutrino spectrum, and PMNS mixing with a predictive two-branch octant--$δ$ correlation testable at DUNE and Hyper-Kamiokande.

</details>

*Germán Rodrigo*

Result: 论文识别了对撞机物理中适合量子模拟的关键计算挑战，并提出了具体应用方向。特别指出多圈真空振幅的因果结构识别与图论（graph theory）有深刻联系，而高维函数积分采样是实现能够在高微扰阶次（high perturbative orders）运行的完整量子事件生成器（quantum event generator）的初步步骤。

Conclusion: 对撞机物理为量子模拟提供了丰富的应用场景，从数据分析到基础计算挑战。论文展示的具体应用案例表明，量子计算技术有望显著提升对撞机物理研究的计算效率和能力，特别是在处理复杂微扰计算和事件生成方面具有重要潜力。

Abstract: High-energy colliders, exemplified by the CERN's Large Hadron Collider (LHC), constitute genuine quantum machines. In alignment with Richard Feynman's foundational vision for quantum computing, collider physics emerge therefore as a prime candidate for quantum simulations. Prospective applications include Quantum Machine Learning for collider data analysis, accelerated evaluation of complex multiloop Feynman diagrams, efficient jet clustering, enhanced parton shower simulations, and related computational challenges. We discuss two specific applications: the identification of causal structures in multiloop vacuum amplitudes, a fundamental component of the Loop-Tree Duality exhibiting deep connections to graph theory; and high-dimensional function integration and sampling. The latter constitutes an initial step toward realizing a fully fleged quantum event generator capable of operating at high perturbative orders.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigate the particle production in proton-antiproton ($p\bar{p}$) collisions using the PACIAE 4.0 model. The pseudorapidity density distributions ($dN_{\text{ch}}/dη$) and transverse momentum ($p_T$) spectra of charged particles from nonsingle diffractive (NSD) $p\bar{p}$ collisions agree well with the experimental data when using model parameters previously determined from nonsingle diffractive proton-proton ($pp$) collisions. Furthermore, we systematically compare results from both inelastic (INEL) and nonsingle diffractive $p\bar{p}$ and $pp$ collisions at the same energy to study the effect of the initial state (matter vs. antimatter) on the transverse momentum spectra of identified particles. Our results show that the net baryon-number difference in the initial state significantly enhances nucleon production at low collision energies, while its effect becomes negligible for high-multiplicity particles or at high collision energies, as expected. These findings further prove that the PACIAE 4.0 model is a versatile and reliable tool for studying high-energy collision physics.

Method: 采用暗色技术色范式（Dark Technicolour paradigm），引入扩展最吸引通道假说（Extended Most Attractive Channel hypothesis）。模型包含三个禁闭规范扇区：技术色、暗色技术色和中间QCD-like扇区，通过扩展规范对称性连接。

Result: 扩展最吸引通道假说揭示了凝聚体的层次结构，其中具有更高净手征性（net chirality）的通道变得更具吸引力。在低能下，暗色技术色范式自然地简化为Froggatt-Nielsen或标准层次真空期望值模型（Standard Hierarchical Vacuum Expectation Value model）。

Conclusion: 该框架由剩余离散对称性支配，为标准模型味道问题提供了令人信服的解决方案，实现了传统技术色动力学在暗色技术色范式中的复兴。

Abstract: We discuss that conventional Technicolour dynamics can be revitalized within the Dark Technicolour paradigm by invoking the Extended Most Attractive Channel hypothesis. The model incorporates three confining gauge sectors, Technicolour, Dark Technicolour, and an intermediate QCD-like sector, linked through extended gauge symmetries. The Extended Most Attractive Channel hypothesis reveals a hierarchical structure of condensates, where channels with higher net chirality become increasingly attractive. At low energies, the Dark Technicolour paradigm naturally reduces to the Froggatt-Nielsen or Standard Hierarchical Vacuum Expectation Value model, governed by residual discrete symmetries, offering a compelling resolution to the Standard Model Flavor Problem.

### [159] [Transverse Structure of the Kaon: A light-front Hamiltonian Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11599)
*Yuanqi Lu,Zhimin Zhu,Jiangshan Lan,Chandan Mondal,Xingbo Zhao,James P. Vary*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究采用基矢光前量子化（BLFQ）框架计算了K介子的领头扭度（twist-2）和次领头扭度（twist-3）横动量依赖部分子分布函数（TMDs），首次理论预测了包含Fock分量干涉效应的K介子次领头扭度TMDs。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于计算K介子的领头扭度和次领头扭度TMDs，特别是关注次领头扭度TMDs中超越概率解释的夸克-夸克-胶子关联效应，这些效应通常被Wandzura-Wilczek近似所忽略。

Method: 采用基矢光前量子化（Basis Light-Front Quantization, BLFQ）框架，通过对角化包含夸克-反夸克（|q\bar{q}\rangle）和夸克-反夸克-胶子（|q\bar{q}g\rangle）Fock分量以及三维禁闭势的光前QCD哈密顿量来获得光前波函数。利用QCD运动方程将twist-3 TMDs分解为twist-2贡献和真正的twist-3项。

Result: 研究提供了首个明确考虑Fock分量干涉效应的K介子次领头扭度TMDs理论预测。真正的twist-3贡献来源于|q\bar{q}\rangle和|q\bar{q}g\rangle分量之间的干涉效应。此外，K介子的twist-2和twist-3共线部分子分布函数（PDFs）结果显示，twist-2 PDFs与JAM合作组最近的全局分析结果吻合良好。

Conclusion: 该工作首次实现了对K介子次领头扭度TMDs的理论预测，明确考虑了Fock分量干涉效应，揭示了超越Wandzura-Wilczek近似的夸克-夸克-胶子关联在次领头扭度TMDs中的重要性。

Abstract: We employ the Basis Light-Front Quantization (BLFQ) framework to compute the leading-twist (twist-2) and subleading-twist (twist-3) transverse-momentum-dependent parton distribution functions (TMDs) of the kaon. The light-front wave functions are obtained by diagonalizing a light-front QCD Hamiltonian that includes quark-antiquark (|q\bar{q}\rangle) and quark-antiquark-gluon (|q\bar{q}g\rangle) Fock components together with a three-dimensional confinement. Using the QCD equations of motion, the twist-3 TMDs are decomposed into twist-2 constributions and genuine twist-3 terms, the latter encoding quark-quark-gluon correlations beyond the probabilistic picture. These genuine twist-3 constributions arise from the interference between the |q\bar{q}\rangle and |q\bar{q}g\rangle sectors, which are usually negelected in the Wandzura-Wilczek approximation. This work provides the first theoretical predictions of kaon subleading-twist TMDs that explicitly account for Fock-sector interference. In addition, we present results for the kaon's twist-2 and twist-3 collinear parton distribution functions (PDFs). The twist-2 PDFs are found to be in good agreement with the recent global analysis by the JAM collaboration.

### [160] [Schwinger Model with a Dynamical Axion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12194)
*Gabriel Rouxinol,Tom Magorsch,Jesse J. Osborne,Nora Brambilla,Jad C. Halimeh*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过哈密顿格点规范理论（Hamiltonian lattice gauge theory）将量子化轴子（axion）场耦合到具有拓扑θ项（topological θ-term）的大质量施温格模型（Schwinger model），首次在完全动力学的格点规范理论中非微扰地（nonperturbatively）展示了轴子解决强CP问题（strong CP problem）的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型（Standard Model）中的强CP问题是主要未解之谜之一：量子色动力学（Quantum Chromodynamics）允许CP破坏的拓扑θ项，但实验约束其值极小。Peccei-Quinn机制通过将θ角提升为动力学场——引入轴子——来解决此问题，但其在完全动力学量子场论中的实现需要验证。

Method: 采用哈密顿格点规范理论框架，将量子化轴子场耦合到具有拓扑θ项的大质量施温格模型。使用无限矩阵乘积态（infinite matrix product state）技术计算基态性质，分析轴子动力学如何弛豫有效θ角。

Result: 计算显示轴子动力学将有效θ角弛豫到真空能最小值，使基态能量独立于θ，在完全动力学格点规范理论中展示了轴子介导的强CP问题解决方案。进一步分析了CP恢复（CP restoration）并从拓扑敏感性（topological susceptibility）和激发谱中提取了轴子质量。

Conclusion: 该研究为轴子动力学提供了非微扰证明，展示了轴子机制在量子格点规范理论中的实现，且该框架适合在现代量子硬件（quantum hardware）上进行研究。

Abstract: One of the major open puzzles in the Standard Model of particle physics is the strong CP problem: although Quantum Chromodynamics allows a CP-violating topological $θ$-term, experiments constrain its value to be extremely small. The Peccei--Quinn mechanism resolves this problem by promoting the $θ$-angle to a dynamical field-introducing the axion -- whose dynamics relax the effective angle $θ_\text{eff}$ to a CP-conserving minimum. Here, we investigate the resulting axion physics in a Hamiltonian lattice gauge theory (LGT) by coupling a quantized axion field to the massive Schwinger model with a topological $θ$-term. Using infinite matrix product state techniques, we compute the ground-state properties of the resulting theory and demonstrate that the axion dynamically relaxes $θ_\text{eff}$ to the minimum of the vacuum energy. Consequently, the ground-state energy becomes independent of $θ$, demonstrating the axion-mediated solution to the strong CP problem within a fully dynamical LGT. We further analyze CP restoration and extract the axion mass from the topological susceptibility and excitation spectrum. Our results provide a nonperturbative demonstration of axion dynamics in a quantum LGT amenable to investigation on modern quantum hardware.

### [161] [Bayesian Model Calibration with Integrated Discrepancy: Addressing Inexact Dislocation Dynamics Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11960)
*Liam Myhill,Enrique Martinez Saez,Sez Russcher*

Main category: stat.ME

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种贝叶斯模型校准（Bayesian model calibration）新方法，重新诠释了Kennedy和O'Hagan（KOH）的传统模型差异定义。该方法将δ_θ(x_i)高斯过程（Gaussian processes, GPs）集成到模拟器中，并通过GP代理模型（surrogate model）确保计算可行性。应用于分子动力学（Molecular Dynamics, MD）和离散位错动力学（Discrete Dislocation Dynamics, DDD）模拟的临界应力预测校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统KOH方法将模型差异（model discrepancy）视为与模拟器解耦的"万能"误差来源，而新方法旨在重新诠释这一概念。动机在于开发一种更合理的校准方法，假设模拟器在校准后能充分预测观测趋势，且所有模型形式误差（model-form errors）可归因于输入参数的不确定性。

Method: 方法的核心创新在于将δ_θ(x_i)高斯过程（GPs）集成到模拟器内部，而非像KOH方法那样将其作为外部独立项。为确保计算可行性，该方法使用高斯过程代理模型（GP surrogate model）来近似模拟器。通过重新定义常用的差异高斯过程（discrepancy Gaussian process），实现了与KOH方法的差异化。

Result: 该方法成功应用于分子动力学（MD）观测的临界应力驱动位错偶极子（dislocation dipoles）预测，以及离散位错动力学（DDD）模拟器的等效预测校准。DDD模拟器对底层物理机制的粗粒度物理解释需要基于MD观测进行校准。研究提供了与KOH方法的基准比较（benchmark against KOH）。

Conclusion: 本文提出了关于新方法适用场景的哲学论证（philosophical argument），并展望了未来扩展该方法的方向。通过重新定义模型差异的概念框架，为贝叶斯模型校准提供了新的理论视角和实践方法，特别适用于模拟器能充分预测观测趋势但存在参数不确定性的场景。

Abstract: In this work, a novel approach to Bayesian model calibration routines is developed which reinterprets the traditional definition of model discrepancy as defined by Kennedy and O'Hagan (KOH). The novelty lies in the integration of $δ_θ(x_i)$ GPs within the simulator, which is approximated as a GP surrogate model to ensure computational tractability. This approach assumes that the utilized simulator sufficiently predicts observed trends when calibrated with respect to the application domain, and that all model-form errors can be attributed to uncertainty in the input parameters. In contrast, the KOH method assumes discrepancy to be inherently decoupled from the simulator, acting as a 'catch-all' for various sources of model error. The new method is applied to Molecular Dynamics observations of the critical stress to drive dislocation dipoles, and equivalent predictions using a Discrete Dislocation Dynamics simulator whose coarse-grained physical interpretation of the underlying physical mechanisms requires calibration against MD observations. We present an overview of similar state-aware calibration routines; differentiate the provided approach through redefining the commonly used discrepancy Gaussian process and benchmark against KOH. A philosophical argument as to when application of the proposed method is appropriate is provided, and future directions for expanding upon this methodology are proposed.

### [162] [Pre-Lie Structures for Semisimple Lie Algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11218)
*Xerxes D. Arsiwalla,Fernando Olivie Méndez Méndez*

Main category: math.RA

TL;DR: 该论文研究了与给定李代数（特别是复半单李代数）相关的预李结构（pre-Lie structures）的可容许性（admissibility）问题。重点分析了五类非结合李可容许代数（Lie-admissible algebras）中的反柔性代数（AFAs），并探讨了A₃-结合与S₃-结合类型，最终证明S₃-结合代数是所有复李代数的通用预李结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决与给定李代数（特别是复半单李代数）相关的预李结构（pre-Lie structures）的可容许性（admissibility）问题。该研究关注李可容许代数（Lie-admissible algebras）这一非结合代数类，其交换子括号满足雅可比恒等式（Jacobi identity）。

Method: 研究从分析由二阶置换(1 3)生成的子群对应的代数类——反柔性代数（anti-flexible algebras, AFAs）入手。论文讨论了AFAs的性质，提供了有限维表示（finite-dimensional representations）的例子，计算了AFAs的李可容许性准则（Lie-admissibility criteria），并确定了几类简单的解。此外，还探讨了剩余的两类非结合李可容许代数：A₃-结合（A₃-associative）和S₃-结合（S₃-associative）类型。

Result: 研究发现可解李代数（solvable Lie algebras）容许AFAs。对于半单李代数（semisimple Lie algebras），论文给出了一个显式反例，证明sl(2, ℂ)容许一个AFA。最终，论文证明了S₃-结合代数是任何复李代数（包括半单李代数）的通用预李结构（universal pre-Lie structures）。

Conclusion: S₃-结合代数被证明是所有复李代数（包括半单李代数）的通用预李结构。这一结论扩展了我们对李可容许代数及其与李代数关系的理解，特别是在预李结构可容许性方面取得了重要进展。

Abstract: We address the problem of admissibility of pre-Lie structures associated with a given Lie algebra, particularly, semisimple Lie algebras over ${\mathbb C}$. Such structures are collectively referred to as Lie-admissible algebras, which are a class of nonassociative algebras such that the commutator bracket over these algebras satisfies the Jacobi identity. Among the five classes of nonassociative Lie-admissible algebras, left-symmetric algebras (LSAs) and right-symmetric algebras (RSAs), are known to be non-admissible by semisimple Lie algebras of finite dimension $n \geq 3$. Here, we examine the remaining classes starting with those corresponding to the subgroup generated by permutations of order 2: $(1 \; 3)$. These appear in the literature as anti-flexible algebras (AFAs). We discuss properties of AFAs and provide examples of finite-dimensional representations. AFAs geometrically correspond to richer structures than the flat torsion-free affine connections associated with left-symmetric algebras (LSAs) or right-symmetric algebras (RSAs). We compute Lie-admissibility criteria for AFAs and determine a few simple solution classes. Not surprisingly, solvable Lie algebras admit AFAs. Concerning semisimple ones, we report an explicit counterexample demonstrating an AFA admissible by ${\mathfrak sl(2, \, {\mathbb C})}$. We then discuss the remaining two classes of nonassociative Lie-admissible algebras, the $A_3$-associative and $S_3$-associative types. Finally, we prove that $S_3$-associative algebras are universal pre-Lie structures for any Lie algebra over ${\mathbb C}$, including semisimple ones.

</details>

### [163] [Searching solo for the invisible at Compact Muon Solenoid (CMS)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11070)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管标准模型（Standard Model, SM）取得了成功，但仍存在若干未解决的基本问题，如暗物质（dark matter, DM）的本质，这推动了对新物理的探索。本文旨在通过"单-X"末态搜索来探测可能的新物理场景。

Method: 研究使用紧凑μ子螺线管（Compact Muon Solenoid, CMS）探测器在欧洲核子研究中心大型强子对撞机（CERN Large Hadron Collider, LHC）记录的质子-质子碰撞数据，质心能量为√s=13 TeV。方法聚焦于"单-X"（mono-X）末态，其特征是单个可见SM粒子（X）反冲产生大的横向动量不平衡。具体分析了铅笔喷注（低多重数喷注）、单光子（mono-photon）和单顶夸克（mono-top）三种末态，使用的数据集对应积分亮度为138 fb⁻¹。

Result: 未观察到超出标准模型预测的显著事件超出（excess of events）。研究结果被用于为各种新物理场景设定严格的排除限（exclusion limits），包括简化暗物质模型（simplified DM models）和大额外时空维度模型（models of large extra spacetime dimensions）。

Conclusion: 基于CMS Run 2数据的"单-X"末态搜索未发现新物理存在的证据。研究结果为相关理论模型提供了重要的实验约束，特别是对暗物质候选者和大额外维度模型设定了严格的限制。

Abstract: Despite the success of the Standard Model (SM), several fundamental questions remain unanswered, such as the nature of dark matter (DM), motivating searches for new physics. This paper summarizes three recent searches for new physics in proton-proton collisions at a center-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV, using data recorded with the Compact Muon Solenoid (CMS) detector at the CERN Large Hadron Collider (LHC). The searches focus on "mono-X" final states, characterized by a large imbalance in transverse momentum recoiling against a single visible SM particle ($X$), and serve as powerful probes of new physics scenarios. Results are presented for searches in the pencil-jet (low-multiplicity jet), mono-photon, and mono-top final states, using CMS Run 2 data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. No significant excess of events beyond SM predictions is observed, and the results are used to set stringent exclusion limits on various new physics scenarios, including simplified DM models and models of large extra spacetime dimensions.

</details>


### [164] [Measurement of the cosmic muon flux at the Stawell Underground Physics Laboratory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11981)
*G. Fu,M. Mews,F. Scutti,P. Urquijo,E. Barberio,V. Bashu,L. J. Bignell,I. Bolognino,A. Cools,F. Dastgiri,A. R. Duffy,L. Einfalt,M. Froehlich,T. Fruth,M. Gerathy,M. Hancock,R. James,S. Kapoor,S. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为即将开展的SABRE South实验建立μ子否决系统（muon veto system），需要精确测量Stawell地下物理实验室的宇宙μ子通量，以验证模拟预测并优化实验设计。

Method: 使用八个EJ200塑料闪烁体面板（plastic scintillator panels），每个面板两端配备Hamamatsu R13089光电倍增管对（PMT pairs），这些组件构成了SABRE South实验的μ子否决系统。

Result: 测得μ子通量为f = (6.33 ± 0.04_stat ± 0.35_sys) × 10^{-8} s^{-1} cm^{-2}，相对不确定度比建模不确定度小一个数量级，与模拟结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 首次成功测量了Stawell地下物理实验室的地下宇宙μ子通量，测量结果验证了模拟预测的准确性，为SABRE South实验的μ子否决系统提供了关键基准数据。

Abstract: We report the first measurement of the underground cosmic muon flux at the Stawell Underground Physics Laboratory. The measurement uses eight EJ200 plastic scintillator panels, equipped with Hamamatsu R13089 PMT pairs at the ends, which are the primary components of the muon veto system for the upcoming SABRE South experiment. The measured muon flux is f = (6.33 +/- 0.04_stat +/- 0.35_sys) x 10^{-8} [s^{-1} cm^{-2}]. This measurement is in excellent agreement with simulations, with a relative uncertainty an order of magnitude smaller than the modelling uncertainty.

### [165] [Search for displaced decays of long-lived particles in events with missing transverse momentum in $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV $pp$ collisions with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12051)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究利用ATLAS探测器在大型强子对撞机（LHC）Run 2期间收集的137 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据，通过搜索具有显著横向动量缺失和至少一个位移顶点的事件来寻找长寿命粒子。研究未发现显著超出背景的信号，并据此对四种超出标准模型（BSM）物理模型设定了95%置信水平上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于寻找超出标准模型（Beyond-the-Standard Model, BSM）的长寿命粒子（long-lived particles），这些粒子可能产生具有显著横向动量缺失（missing transverse momentum）和位移顶点（displaced vertex）的特征信号。此类信号可能揭示新物理的存在。

Method: 方法包括使用两种不同的次级顶点重建算法（secondary vertexing algorithms）识别位移顶点，其中一种是专门为识别重夸克（heavy quarks）位移衰变优化的新型"模糊"顶点算法（"fuzzy" vertexing algorithm）。对每种算法分别进行搜索，并使用数据驱动方法（data-driven procedure）独立估计每种搜索的标准模型（Standard Model）背景。

Result: 在两种算法的情况下均未观察到显著超出背景的信号。研究结果被用于设定95%置信水平（95% confidence-level）上限，以限制可能产生该末态的超出标准模型物理。

Conclusion: 结论部分将结果在四种模型的背景下进行解释：形成R-强子（R-hadrons）后衰变的长寿命胶微子（long-lived gluinos）、在Bino-Wino协同湮灭模型（Bino-Wino coannihilation model）中通过希格斯介导道衰变的中性微子（neutralinos）、衰变为轴微子（axinos）的长寿命希格斯微子（long-lived Higgsinos），以及预测轻赝标量（light pseudoscalars）位移衰变的奇异希格斯门户模型（exotic Higgs portal model）。

Abstract: A search for long-lived particles in events with significant missing transverse momentum and at least one displaced vertex is presented. This analysis is performed using 137 $\text{fb}^{-1}$ of $pp$ collision data collected between 2016--2018 during Run 2 of the Large Hadron Collider by the ATLAS detector. Displaced vertices are identified using two different secondary vertexing algorithms, including a novel ``fuzzy'' vertexing algorithm optimized for identifying displaced decays of heavy quarks. Separate searches are performed using each algorithm, and the expected Standard Model background is independently estimated for each search using a data-driven procedure. No significant excess is observed over the background in either case. The results are used to set 95% confidence-level limits on potential beyond-the-Standard Model physics that could produce this final state. Results are interpreted in the context of four models: long-lived gluinos that form $R$-hadrons before decaying, neutralinos decaying via Higgs-mediated channels in the Bino-Wino coannihilation model, long-lived Higgsinos decaying to axinos, and an exotic Higgs portal model predicting displaced decays of light pseudoscalars.

### [166] [Why urban heterogeneity limits the 15-minute city](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12122)
*Marc Barthelemy*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过结合城市几何结构和经验观测的企业规模分布，推导出通勤时间的理论下限，揭示了当就业足够集中时，任何空间重组都无法确保统一的短通勤时间，挑战了"15分钟城市"的普遍可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: "15分钟城市（15-minute city）"作为城市规划的核心范式，强调在短出行时间内提供工作和基本服务的普遍可达性，但其可行性（特别是通勤可行性）很少被定量检验。研究旨在探讨城市经济内部结构对通勤可达性的根本约束。

Method: 结合城市几何结构（urban geometry）与经验观测的企业规模分布（firm-size distributions），推导出独立于规划选择或交通技术的通勤时间下限。该方法揭示了当就业足够集中时，即使是最优工作地点布局也无法确保统一的短通勤。

Result: 研究发现了急剧的转变（sharp transition）：当就业足够集中时，任何工作场所的空间重组都无法确保统一的短通勤。应用于巴黎及其近郊的案例表明，实现普遍的15分钟通勤需要显著的经济重组或差异化的移动策略。

Conclusion: 关键问题不是"x分钟城市"是否可实现，而是在给定城市经济结构和空间尺度下，最小可行的x是多少。研究强调了城市经济结构对通勤可达性的根本约束，挑战了单纯空间规划解决通勤问题的假设。

Abstract: The `15-minute city' has emerged as a central paradigm in urban planning, promoting universal access to work and essential services within short travel times. Its feasibility-particularly for commuting to work-has however rarely been examined quantitatively. Here, we show that proximity to employment is fundamentally constrained by the internal structure of urban economies. Combining urban geometry with empirically observed firm-size distributions, we derive a lower bound on commuting times that holds independently of planning choices or transport technologies. This bound reveals a sharp transition: when employment is sufficiently concentrated, no spatial rearrangement of workplaces can ensure uniformly short commutes, even under optimal placement. Applied to Paris and its near suburbs, we find that achieving universal 15-minute commutes would require substantial economic restructuring or differentiated mobility strategies. The relevant question is therefore not whether an $x$-minute city is achievable, but what the minimal feasible $x$ is given a city's economic structure and spatial scale.

### [167] [Biology and Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11234)
*Stuart A. Newman,Sahotra Sarkar*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出生物学与物理学的关系应理解为前者是后者的子学科而非特例，通过将生物物理学（biological physics）重新定义为研究生命物质（living matter）的科学，区别于传统生物物理学（classic biophysics）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在重新界定生物学与物理学的关系，反对将生物学视为物理学的特殊案例。作者认为需要建立一种新的理论框架来理解生命物质的独特性，特别是细胞尺度上非单一性（nonunitary）的生命物质特征。

Method: 采用"物质形式"（forms of matter）的视角，将生命物质分为三类：通用型（generic）、生物通用型（biogeneric）和非通用型（nongeneric）。该方法论植根于恩格斯的辩证唯物主义（dialectical materialism）和纽拉特的多层次物理主义（multilevel physicalism）。

Result: 提出了生物物理学作为研究生命物质科学的新定义，识别了生命物质在细胞尺度上的非单一性特征，以及多细胞形式中三类不同的物理过程。该框架与信息主义（informationism）和遗传还原论（genetic reductionism）形成对比。

Conclusion: 生物学应被视为物理学的子学科而非特例，生命物质具有独特的物质形式特征。该观点为理解尚未完全表征的生命物质形式提供了新的理论框架，并指出了相关开放性问题。

Abstract: This article frames the relation between biological and physics by characterizing the former as a subdiscipline rather than a special case of the latter. To do this, we posit biological physics as the science of living matter in contrast to classic biophysics, the study of organismal properties by physical techniques. At the scale of the individual cell, living matter is nonunitary, i.e., not composed of aggregated subunits, and has features (e.g., intracellular organizational arrangements and biomolecular condensates) that are unlike any materials of the nonliving world. In transiently or constitutively multicellular forms (social microorganisms, animals, plants), living matter sustains physical processes that are generic (shared with nonliving matter, e.g., subunit communication by molecular diffusion in cellular slime molds), biogeneric (analogous to nonliving matter but realized through cellular activities, e.g., subunit demixing in animal embryos) or nongeneric (pertaining to sui generis materials, e.g., budding of active solids in plants). This "forms of matter" perspective is philosophically situated in the dialectical materialism of Engels and Hessen and the multilevel physicalism of Neurath and the logical empiricists. We counterpose this view to informationism and to genetic and other hierarchically reductionist physical theories of biological systems and highlight open questions regarding incompletely characterized and enigmatic forms of living matter.

</details>

### [168] [From Embeddings to Dyson Series: Transformer Mechanics as Non-Hermitian Operator Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11322)
*Po-Hao Chang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于算子理论的框架，将Transformer架构重新表述为多体物理（many-body physics）语言，将自注意力（self-attention）解释为非厄米相互作用算子（non-Hermitian interaction operator），网络深度对应算子有序组合，为理解深度Transformer的稳定性、表示饱和等经验性质提供了结构性解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer架构通常以算法和统计术语描述，缺乏物理理论研究者熟悉的结构性语言。本文旨在弥合这一鸿沟，通过建立算子理论框架，将Transformer机制重新表述为多体物理领域熟悉的语言。

Method: 从将词元（token）视为无内在几何的离散索引出发，嵌入（embedding）对应到连续表示空间的基变换（basis transformation）。建立参考基后，自注意力自然承担非厄米相互作用算子的角色，网络深度实现这些相互作用的有序组合（ordered composition）。

Result: 在该框架下，深度Transformer的若干经验性质——包括大深度下的稳定性、表示饱和（representational saturation）以及多头分解（multi-head decomposition）的有效性——获得了作为受调控算子组合（regulated operator composition）结果的自然结构解释。谱几何（spectral geometry）、通道分解（channel factorization）和归一化（normalization）作为组织性结构逻辑而非孤立架构选择出现。

Conclusion: 该视角不依赖事后类比，而是遵循构造性路径，每个并行性都源自前序结构步骤。通过用算子语言重新表述Transformer机制，该框架通过共享数学结构降低了深度学习与多体物理之间的概念障碍，使两个领域的工具和直觉更易于相互理解。

Abstract: Transformer architectures are typically described in algorithmic and statistical terms, leaving their internal mechanics without a familiar structural language for researchers trained in physical theories. To bridge this gap, we develop a complementary operator-theoretic framework that recasts their mechanics in a language familiar to many-body physics. Beginning from the token as a discrete index without intrinsic geometry, we show that embedding corresponds to a basis transformation into a continuous representation space. Once such a reference basis is established, self-attention naturally assumes the role of a non-Hermitian interaction operator, and network depth implements an ordered composition of these interactions. Within this formulation, several empirical properties of deep Transformers -- including stability at large depth, representational saturation, and the effectiveness of multi-head decomposition -- find natural structural interpretations as consequences of regulated operator composition. Together, spectral geometry, channel factorization, and normalization emerge as organizing structural logic rather than isolated architectural choices. This perspective does not rely on post-hoc analogy, but follows a constructive path in which each parallel arises from the preceding structural step. By recasting Transformer mechanics in operator language, the framework lowers the conceptual barrier between deep learning and many-body physics through shared mathematical structure, making tools and intuitions from each domain more readily legible to the other.

</details>


### [169] [Machine Learning of Topological Insulator and Anderson Insulator in One-Dimensional Extended Su-Schrieffer-Heeger Chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11688)
*Zhekai Yin,C. K. Ong*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究使用基于无系统约化关联矩阵训练的卷积神经网络，预测扩展SSH模型中无序系统的绕数相图，发现机器学习可作为量子物质对称性保护本质的灵敏探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究扩展Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型中的无序效应，探索机器学习在探测量子物质对称性保护本质方面的潜力，超越传统分类器功能。

Method: 使用在无系统约化关联矩阵（RCMs）上训练的卷积神经网络（CNN），预测具有非对角和对角无序系统的绕数相图；结合主成分分析（PCA）分析特征空间，并采用逆参与率（IPR）和能谱分析。

Result: 训练后的CNN模型可推广到手征对称性保持的非对角无序系统，但在手征对称性破坏的对角无序系统中失效；PCA显示无系统和对称保持系统共享重叠特征流形，而对称破坏无序导致特征流形发散；IPR和能谱分析表明非对角无序保持拓扑边缘态，而对角无序驱动向安德森绝缘体的转变。

Conclusion: 机器学习不仅是分类器，更是量子物质对称性保护本质的灵敏探针；非对角无序保持拓扑性质，而对角无序破坏手征对称性并诱导安德森局域化。

Abstract: We study disorder effects in the extended Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model using a convolutional neural network (CNN) trained on reduced correlation matrices (RCMs) of disorder-free systems to predict winding number phase diagrams in systems with off-diagonal and diagonal disorder. The trained CNN model generalizes to chiral-symmetry-preserving off-diagonal disorder system but fails in the presence of chiral-symmetry-breaking diagonal disorder system. Using principal component analysis (PCA) of the RCM feature space, we demonstrate that disorder-free and symmetry-preserving systems share overlapping feature manifolds, whereas symmetry-breaking disorder causes them to diverge. Inverse participation ratio (IPR) and energy spectrum analysis further demonstrate that off-diagonal disorder preserves topological edge states, whereas diagonal disorder drives a transition to an Anderson insulator. Our results position machine learning not merely as a classifier, but as a sensitive probe for the symmetry-protected nature of quantum matter.

### [170] [Emergent criticality in the Aubry-André model with periodic modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12085)
*Sitaram Maity,Nilanjan Roy,Tapan Mishra*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究展示了在强周期性调制条件下，Aubry-André模型（AAH模型）中出现的临界相（critical phase），该相具有多重分形本征态和奇异连续谱，属于临界Harper模型的普适类。研究还揭示了周期性势能如何将谱折叠成多个能带并产生多个Hofstadter蝴蝶结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Aubry-André模型（AAH模型）在一维情况下存在金属-绝缘体转变，但在临界点处所有态都是临界或多重分形的。虽然额外的周期性调制通常会破坏这种临界性，但研究旨在探索在强调制条件下是否会出现新的临界现象。

Method: 研究通过分析具有准周期晶格调制的Aubry-André模型，特别关注在强周期性调制强度极限下的行为。采用理论分析探讨了周期性势能对谱结构的影响，特别是周期为N的额外势能如何折叠谱并增强准周期性。

Result: 研究发现强调制临界相（strong-modulation critical phase）表现出多重分形本征态（multifractal eigenstates）和奇异连续谱（singular continuous spectra），属于临界Harper模型（critical Harper model）的普适类。此外，准周期链中的周期势能将谱折叠成N个能带，准周期性增强N倍，在每个能带中产生N个Hofstadter蝴蝶结构。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了一种在准周期系统中工程化稳健临界性和谱复制的一般机制。强调制条件可以产生新的临界相，而周期性势能则能实现谱的折叠和Hofstadter蝴蝶结构的复制，为调控准周期系统的性质提供了新途径。

Abstract: The Aubry-André model describes a system with quasiperiodic lattice modulation. In one dimension the AAH model is known to exhibit a sharp metal to insulator transition at a self-dual critical point at which all the states in the spectrum are critical or multifractal in nature. While such criticality is immediately destroyed by an additional onsite periodic modulation, we show an emergent criticality in the limit of strong periodic modulation strength under proper conditions. The resulting strong-modulation critical phase exhibits multifractal eigenstates and singular continuous spectra, belonging to the universality class of the critical Harper model. Moreover, we reveal that additional periodic potential of period N in the quasiperiodic chain folds the spectrum into N bands with quasiperiodicity being enhanced by a factor of N, producing N numbers of Hofstadter butterflies in each band. Our results reveal a general mechanism for engineering robust criticality and spectral replication in quasiperiodic systems.

</details>


### [171] [Thermalisation as Diffusion in Hilbert Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12234)
*Aleksey Lunkin*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究发展了一种超越标准马尔可夫和费米黄金定则假设的微观热化理论，通过将非相互作用基中的相互作用矩阵元建模为独立随机变量，推导出约化动力学的扩散传播子表达式，并证明弛豫由相互作用诱导的能级展宽分布控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在建立超越标准马尔可夫近似和费米黄金定则假设的微观热化理论，特别关注温度计与多体浴耦合系统的热化过程，以更精确地描述非马尔可夫效应和相互作用诱导的能级展宽效应。

Method: 通过将非相互作用基中的相互作用矩阵元建模为独立随机变量，推导出约化动力学的扩散传播子表达式，并采用精确对角化方法对重尾Lévy耦合、全对全横向场伊辛模型和一维Imbrie模型进行数值验证。

Result: 理论预测热化时间尺度由典型展宽的倒数设定，并得到全局平衡的非马尔可夫推广；精确对角化测试显示理论预测与数值结果良好吻合，表明弛豫确实由相互作用诱导的能级展宽分布控制。

Conclusion: 该研究成功发展了一种超越标准近似的微观热化理论框架，为理解温度计与多体浴耦合系统的非马尔可夫热化动力学提供了新的理论工具和物理洞见。

Abstract: We develop a microscopic theory of thermalisation for a thermometer coupled to a many-body bath beyond standard Markovian and Fermi-golden-rule assumptions. By modeling interaction matrix elements in the non-interacting basis as independent random variables, we derive a diffusion-propagator expression for the reduced dynamics and show that relaxation is controlled by the distribution of interaction-induced level broadenings. The theory predicts a thermalisation timescale set by the inverse typical broadening and yields a non-Markovian generalization of global balance. Exact-diagonalization tests for heavy-tailed L{é}vy couplings, an all-to-all transverse-field Ising model, and the one-dimensional Imbrie model show good agreement with these predictions.

</details>

### [172] [Selective braiding of different anyons in the even-denominator fractional quantum Hall effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11162)
*Jehyun Kim,Amit Shaer,Ravi Kumar,Alexey Ilin,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Ady Stern,David F. Mross,Yuval Ronen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究实现了一种门可调谐的法布里-珀罗干涉仪，用于测量偶分母量子霍尔态中任意子（anyon）的编织相位，观测到π和π/2的统计相位，并直接解析了单个任意子隧穿事件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 偶分母量子霍尔态可以承载多种具有不同交换统计特性的任意子，交换两个准粒子会对多体波函数施加相位甚至将其转变为不同状态。研究旨在解决观测非阿贝尔编织的两个关键挑战之一：实现对局域化和干涉任意子类型的控制。

Method: 实现了一种门可调谐的法布里-珀罗干涉仪（gate-tunable Fabry-Pérot interferometer），其中嵌入反点（antidot）以提供对干涉环内任意子数量的局域控制。通过独立调节磁场、器件各区域的载流子密度以及反点电势，访问局域任意子可重复形成的区域。

Result: 测量到编织相位θ_braid=π和θ_braid=π/2，分别归因于e/2准粒子环绕e/2或e/4准粒子。进一步观察到反点不同任意子占据数随时间切换，直接解析了单个任意子隧穿进入干涉环的事件。在填充因子1/3处观察到类似行为。

Conclusion: 该工作解决了观测非阿贝尔编织的两个关键挑战之一，实现了对局域化和干涉任意子类型的控制，为研究偶分母量子霍尔态中任意子的统计特性提供了重要实验手段。

Abstract: Even-denominator quantum Hall states can host several types of anyons with distinct exchange statistics. Depending on the anyon type, exchanging two quasiparticles can impart a phase to the many-body wave function or even transform it into a different state. Here, we realize a gate-tunable Fabry-Pérot interferometer with an embedded antidot that provides local control over the number of anyons within the interference loop. By independently tuning the magnetic field, carrier densities across the device, and the antidot potential, we access regimes in which localized anyons form reproducibly and measure the associated statistical phases $e^{i θ_\mathrm{braid}}$. We resolve braiding phases of $θ_{\mathrm{braid}}=π$ and $θ_{\mathrm{braid}}=\fracπ{2}$, which we attribute to $e/2$ quasiparticles encircling either $e/2$ or $e/4$ quasiparticles, respectively. We further observe switching between different anyon occupancies of the antidot over time, directly resolving individual anyon tunnelling events into the interference loop. Similar behavior occurs at filling factor one third. Our work addresses one of the two key challenges in observing non-Abelian braiding, which requires control of both localized and interfering anyon types.

</details>


### [173] [Imaging flat band electron hydrodynamics in biased bilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11175)
*Canxun Zhang,Evgeny Redekop,Hari Stoyanov,Jack H. Farrell,Sunghoon Kim,Ludwig Holleis,David Gong,Aidan Keough,Youngjoon Choi,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Martin E. Huber,Ania C. Bleszynski Jayich,Andrew Lucas,Andrea F. Young*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究利用扫描超导磁传感器成像双层石墨烯中的局域电流，在平带（flat band）区域观察到最强的流体动力学输运，电子-电子散射长度约50纳米，为基于线性和非线性电子流体动力学的小型化器件开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流体动力学电子输运（hydrodynamic electron transport）通常受限于电子-电子散射长度较大（数百纳米），限制了基于流体动力学流动的器件小型化。双层菱面体石墨烯（rhombohedral graphene multilayers）的大且可调有效质量为增强流体动力学行为提供了新途径。

Method: 采用扫描超导磁传感器（scanning superconducting magnetic sensor）对双栅双层石墨烯（dual-gated bilayer graphene）中的局域电流进行成像。利用对层流和涡流都敏感的样品几何结构，在载流子密度和位移场构成的完整相空间中识别不同输运区域。

Result: 在完整相空间中识别出三种不同的输运区域：弹道（ballistic）、流体动力学（hydrodynamic）和扩散（diffusive）区域。最强的流体动力学输运出现在平带区域，电子-电子散射长度约50纳米，与费米波长相当。高电流测量揭示了流动模式的显著非线性特征。

Conclusion: 该研究通过双层石墨烯平带区域实现了电子-电子散射长度约50纳米的强流体动力学输运，为基于线性和非线性电子流体动力学（linear and nonlinear electron hydrodynamics）的小型化电子器件发展奠定了基础。

Abstract: Hydrodynamic electron transport arises when carrier kinetics are dominated by interelectron collisions rather than the relaxation of momentum out of the electron system. In recent years, signatures of electron hydrodynamics have been reported in graphene devices owing to the low disorder and weak electron-phonon coupling. However, these experiments have been performed in regimes where the carrier mass is light, and the electron-electron collision length--though smaller than corresponding lengths for phonon or impurity scattering--remains large in absolute terms, typically several hundred nanometers. This restricts hydrodynamic transport phenomena to large length scales, limiting miniaturization of devices based on hydrodynamic flow. The advent of dual-gated rhombohedral graphene multilayers introduces a new route toward enhanced hydrodynamic behavior via their large--and tunable--effective mass. Here, we employ a scanning superconducting magnetic sensor to image local current flow in dual-gated bilayer graphene. Exploiting a sample geometry sensitive to both laminar and vortical flow, we identify three distinct transport regimes--ballistic, hydrodynamic, and diffusive--across the full phase space spanned by carrier density and displacement field. The strongest hydrodynamic transport is observed in the flat band regime, where fitting our results to a unified Boltzmann transport model reveals the electron-electron scattering length to be comparable to the Fermi wavelength of ~50 nm. High-current measurements, meanwhile, reveal striking nonlinearities in the flow pattern. Our results pave the way for miniaturized electronic devices based on linear and nonlinear electron hydrodynamics.

</details>


### [174] [Controlled localization of anyons in a graphene quantum Hall interferometer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11182)
*Christina E. Henzinger,James R. Ehrets,Rikuto Fushio,Junkai Dong,Thomas Werkmeister,Marie E. Wesson,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Ashvin Vishwanath,Bertrand I. Halperin,Amir Yacoby,Philip Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过在双层石墨烯分数量子霍尔干涉仪中心添加栅极控制点/反点，实现了对局域任意子数量的精确调控，观测到数百个受控相位滑移，为观测非阿贝尔任意子的非局域交换统计和构建容错拓扑量子比特奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交换统计（exchange statistics）是量子力学的基本原理，决定了全同粒子波函数的对称性，并由此产生多体量子态的涌现现象。通过电子分数量子霍尔（FQH）干涉仪可以探测阿贝尔和非阿贝尔任意子波函数的交换诱导幺正变换，其中沿干涉FQH边缘传播的准粒子与局域在干涉仪内的准粒子发生编织（braid）。

Method: 在双层石墨烯分数量子霍尔干涉仪腔体中心添加栅极控制点/反点（gate-controlled dot/anti-dot），以调控被包围的任意子数量。通过测量干涉仪对角电导（diagonal conductance）来观测相位滑移（phase slips）。

Result: 观测到数百个受控相位滑移，与局域准粒子数量的离散变化一致。对于阿贝尔任意子，观测到的相位滑移与理论预期值相符。在半填充时，结果表明干涉边缘携带电荷|e*/e| = 1/2的阿贝尔激发，而电荷|e*/e| = 1/4的假定非阿贝尔任意子仍局域在干涉仪腔体内。

Conclusion: 在干涉仪中控制局域e/4任意子数量是观测其非局域交换统计（non-local exchange statistics）和构建基于非阿贝尔任意子操控的容错拓扑量子比特（fault tolerant topological qubit）的重要里程碑。

Abstract: Exchange statistics are a fundamental principle of quantum mechanics, dictating the symmetry of identical particle wavefunctions and thereby enabling emergent phenomena of many-body quantum states. The exchange-induced unitary transformation of both abelian and non-abelian anyonic wavefunctions can be probed using electronic fractional quantum Hall (FQH) interferometers, where quasiparticles propagating along the interfering FQH edge braid with those localized within the interferometer. Here, we add a gate-controlled dot/anti-dot in the center of a bilayer graphene FQH interferometer cavity to tune the number of enclosed anyons. We observe hundreds of controlled phase slips in the diagonal conductance across the interferometer for both abelian and non-abelian states, consistent with discrete changes in the localized quasiparticle population. For abelian anyons, the observed phase slips agree with the theoretically expected value. At half filling, our results suggest the interfering edge carries charge $|e^*/e| = 1/2$ abelian excitations, whereas charge $|e^*/e| = 1/4$ putative non-abelian anyons remain localized in the interferometer cavity. Controlling the population of localized $e/4$ anyons in an interferometer marks a significant milestone towards observing their non-local exchange statistics and building a fault tolerant topological qubit based on non-abelian anyon manipulation.

</details>


### [175] [Hall conductance in a weakly time-reversal invariant open system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11186)
*Alexander Fagerlund,Christopher Ekman,Rodrigo Arouca*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究展示了非平衡效应如何在弱时间反演对称（time-reversal invariant）系统中诱导霍尔物理（Hall physics），即使未施加磁场。关键在于费米子系统通过与玻色子自由度和外部库的相互作用获得时间反演对称破缺的自能（self-energy），从而产生非量子化的霍尔电导（Hall conductance）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子霍尔效应（quantum Hall effect）和量子反常霍尔效应（quantum anomalous Hall effect）都需要时间反演对称性破缺。本研究旨在探索在系统整体保持弱时间反演对称且无外加磁场的条件下，非平衡效应是否仍能诱导出霍尔物理现象。

Method: 研究构建了一个理论模型，其中费米子系统通过与系统内的玻色子自由度以及外部库（external reservoir）的相互作用，获得时间反演对称破缺的自能。该方法强调了波函数重整化（wave-function renormalization）效应在非平衡情况下的关键作用。

Result: 费米子系统在非平衡条件下发展出非量子化的霍尔电导。研究证明，与平衡情况不同，仅存在质量项（mass term）不足以产生霍尔电导，必须考虑波函数重整化效应。

Conclusion: 非平衡效应能够在弱时间反演对称系统中诱导霍尔物理，即使系统整体保持对称且无外加磁场。这一现象源于费米子系统通过相互作用获得时间反演对称破缺的自能，且波函数重整化效应在其中扮演关键角色。

Abstract: The quantum Hall effect and the quantum anomalous Hall effect both require time-reversal invariance to be broken. We show that non-equilibrium effects can cause Hall physics to arise even when the system is weakly time-reversal symmetric and no magnetic field is applied. In our model, this occurs due to a fermionic subsystem breaking time-reversal invariance even if the system as a whole does not. The fermions receive a TRI-breaking self-energy, caused by interactions with bosonic degrees of freedom in the system and with an external reservoir. As a result, the fermions develop a non-quantized Hall conductance. We demonstrate that, unlike in the equilibrium case, the presence of a mass term is insufficient for the Hall conductance to appear, and wave-function renormalization effects have to be included.

</details>


### [176] [Linear response of the Chern insulator MnBi$_2$Te$_4$: A Wannier function approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11268)
*Matthew Albert,Javier Sivianes,Jason G. Kattan,Julen Ibañez-Azpiroz,J. E. Sipe*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究计算了不同层数MnBi₂Te₄薄膜的光学电导率和磁化率，结合密度泛函理论和Wannier函数方法，发现11层薄膜与5层薄膜具有相同陈数（Chern number），与先前报道的"高陈数相"存在差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验和理论预测表明，陈绝缘体（Chern insulator）对有限频率电场的线性响应包含拓扑霍尔项。本研究旨在分析不同层数MnBi₂Te₄薄膜的光学性质和拓扑特性，特别关注11层薄膜的拓扑相。

Method: 结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory）与"单次"Wannier函数（"single-shot" Wannier functions）计算光学电导率和磁化率。使用基于布洛赫能量和速度矩阵元的全局表达式计算二维陈数（two-dimensional Chern number），避免能带交叉处的数值问题。

Result: 11层薄膜与5层薄膜具有相同陈数，与先前报道的"高陈数相"（higher Chern-number phase）存在差异。研究还发现自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）驱动的能带反转可能是这些拓扑相的可能指示器。

Conclusion: 11层MnBi₂Te₄薄膜的拓扑特性与5层薄膜相似，而非先前报道的高陈数相。自旋轨道耦合驱动的能带反转可作为拓扑相的可能识别标志，研究讨论了与其他研究结果差异的可能原因。

Abstract: Recent work demonstrated that in the long wavelength limit the linear response of a Chern insulator to finite-frequency electric fields is the sum of two terms: A general frequency-dependent Kubo contribution that is present irrespective of band topology, and a topological Hall term that vanishes for topologically trivial insulators. Motivated by recent experiments and theoretical predictions, we use these expressions to calculate the optical conductivity and susceptibility of intrinsically magnetic MnBi$_2$Te$_4$ thin films with one, four, five, and eleven septuple layers by combining density functional theory with "single-shot" Wannier functions. To characterize the underlying topology of these systems, we compute the two-dimensional Chern number of these films using recently derived global expressions formulated in terms of Bloch energies and velocity matrix elements; the use of these expressions allows us to circumvent numerical issues at band crossings. Films with eleven septuple layers are of particular interest. We find that they have the same Chern number as five septuple layer films, in contrast to the reported "higher Chern-number phase" of these systems in other studies; we discuss a few possible reasons for the discrepancy. We also identify spin-orbit coupling-driven band inversions as a possible indicator of these topological phases.

</details>


### [177] [Optically Driven Orbital Hall Transport in Floquet Odd-Parity Collinear Altermagnets with High Chern Numbers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11483)
*Yuping Tian,Chen-Hao Zhao,Chao-Bo Wang,Binyuan Zhang,Xiangru Kong,Wei-Jiang Gong*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过对称性分析和有效模型，证明Floquet工程（Floquet engineering）可在二维共线反铁磁多层结构中诱导f波奇宇称altermagnetism，并通过调控圆偏振光（circularly polarized light）实现可调Chern数达±8的非平衡量子反常霍尔效应（quantum anomalous Hall effect），同时调控轨道霍尔效应（orbital Hall effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，非相对论性奇宇称磁性（nonrelativistic odd-parity magnetism）及其在共线altermagnets中的拓扑性质引起了广泛关注。研究旨在探索通过光场调控实现拓扑相变的新途径。

Method: 基于对称性分析（symmetry analysis）和有效模型（effective model），研究采用Floquet工程方法，利用圆偏振光（circularly polarized light）与层自由度（layer degrees of freedom）的耦合来诱导f波奇宇称altermagnetism。同时通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）验证了VSi₂N₄作为实验平台的可行性。

Result: Floquet工程成功诱导了f波奇宇称altermagnetism，并通过调控圆偏振光实现了非平衡量子反常霍尔效应，其Chern数可调至±8。该拓扑相变为轨道霍尔效应的调控提供了有效手段，通过重新分布轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）实现操控。VSi₂N₄被证实为具有显著三角扭曲（trigonal warping）特征的可行实验平台。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一条通往光控拓扑现象（optically controllable topological phenomena）的多功能途径，为拓扑自旋电子学（topological spintronics）和轨道电子学（orbitronics）的未来发展开辟了新机遇。

Abstract: Recent studies have attracted increasing interest in nonrelativistic odd-parity magnetism and its associated topology in collinear altermagnets. Here, based on symmetry analysis and an effective model, we demonstrate that Floquet engineering can induce $f$-wave odd-parity altermagnetism in two-dimensional collinear antiferromagnetic multilayers via the coupling between circularly polarized light (CPL) and layer degrees of freedom. Furthermore, modifying the CPL induces nonequilibrium quantum anomalous Hall effect (QAHE) with tunable Chern numbers up to $C=\pm8$, arising from layer- and valley-dependent band inversions. The induced topological phase transitions provide an efficient means to manipulate the orbital Hall effect (OHE) by redistributing orbital angular momentum. First-principles calculations reveal that experimentally accessible VSi$_2$N$_4$ serves as a viable platform for topological phase diagram of the QAHE and OHE, featuring pronounced trigonal warping. Our findings establish a versatile route toward optically controllable topological phenomena, opening new opportunities for future developments in topological spintronics and orbitronics.

</details>


### [178] [Anomalous Coulomb-Enhanced Charge Transport in Triangular Triple Quantum Dots Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11488)
*Shuo Dong,Junqing Li,Jianhua Wei*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子关联（electron correlation）和量子干涉（quantum interference）在介观输运中至关重要。研究旨在探索三角形拓扑结构中库仑相互作用与量子干涉的独特耦合效应，揭示不同于线性量子点阵列的反常输运特征。

Method: 采用精确的层次运动方程（hierarchical equations of motion, HEOM）形式，理论研究连接费米子库的三角形三量子点（triangular triple quantum dot, TTQD）分子的非平衡输运动力学。

Result: 发现反直觉的输运特征：增加库仑相互作用U显著增强稳态电流，这与线性量子点阵列中典型的抑制行为不同。通过分析谱函数演化，将此增强归因于库仑相互作用诱导的能量移动与三角形拓扑特有的量子干涉效应之间的相互作用。

Conclusion: 研究阐明了三角形拓扑中库仑相互作用与量子干涉的独特耦合机制，揭示了反常电流增强现象。通过构建输运电流随量子点间隧穿（t）和库仑相互作用（U）变化的三维映射图，展示了二者对电流幅值的联合效应及其潜在应用。

Abstract: Electron correlation and quantum interference are pivotal in mesoscopic transport. We theoretically study the nonequilibrium transport dynamics of a triangular triple quantum dot (TTQD) molecule connected to fermionic reservoirs using the exact hierarchical equations of motion (HEOM) formalism. We demonstrate a counter-intuitive transport signature where the stationary current is significantly enhanced by increasing the $U$, a behavior distinct from the suppression typically observed in linear quantum dot arrays. By analyzing the evolution of spectral functions, we attribute this enhancement to the interplay between Coulomb interaction-induced energy shifts and quantum interference effects unique to the triangular topology. We also explore how the circulation of chiral currents and electrode coupling strength modulates these interaction effects. Finally, we present a three-dimensional map of the transport current as a function of inter-dot tunneling ($t$) and Coulomb interaction ($U$), illustrating their combined effect on the current magnitude and its applications.

### [179] [Nonlinear spin-motive force driven by mixed-space quantum geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11499)
*Tomonari Meguro,Hiroaki Ishizuka,Kentaro Nomura*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究超越Thouless泵浦范式，理论分析了自旋动生电动势的非线性效应，发现磁化动力学可诱导直流和二次谐波电流分量，其源于电子能带在混合参数空间$({\boldsymbol k}, {\boldsymbol m})$中的量子几何特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于超越线性响应区域和Thouless泵浦范式，探索磁化动力学诱导电流的非线性效应。当前研究主要关注交流分量，而该工作旨在揭示非线性阶次中可能存在的直流和更高谐波分量。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，基于电子能带在混合参数空间$({\boldsymbol k}, {\boldsymbol m})$中的量子几何特性，构建超越线性响应的理论框架。通过应用该理论到Luttinger模型进行具体计算验证。

Result: 研究发现自旋动生电动势在磁化动力学的非线性阶次中同时获得直流分量和二次谐波分量。在Luttinger模型中，即使在绝缘区域也能产生有限非线性电流，且该电信号可在常规电流测量装置中检测到。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了$({\boldsymbol k}, {\boldsymbol m})$-混合空间量子几何在磁化动力学诱导电流中的关键作用，为利用磁性材料实现交流到直流转换提供了新的工作原理。

Abstract: Spin-motive force, i.e., the electric current induced by magnetization dynamics, is theoretically studied beyond the Thouless-pump paradigm. In contrast to the linear-response regime, where the induced current is purely AC, we show that spin-motive force acquires both a DC component and a second-harmonic component at nonlinear order in magnetization dynamics. We further clarify that both contributions originate from the geometric properties of electronic bands -- quantum geometry defined in the mixed parameter space $({\boldsymbol k}, {\boldsymbol m})$ spanned by electron's momentum ${\boldsymbol k}$ and magnetization ${\boldsymbol m}$. By applying the theory to a Luttinger model, we demonstrate that our mechanism yields a finite nonlinear current even in the insulating regime, and the resulting electrical signal is measurable in a conventional current-measurement setup. Our findings offer a new operating principle of AC-to-DC conversion with magnetic materials, highlighting the pivotal role of the $({\boldsymbol k}, {\boldsymbol m})$-mixed space quantum geometry in magnetization-dynamics-induced electric currents.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用光滑静电势垒在量子点接触结构中工作于正入射条件，在单模区域中，倾斜诱导的谷依赖传输相位产生可控的相对相位偏移Δd = δ_K - δ_{K'}。

Result: 该静电元件实现了可调谐的谷Z旋转，其可达相位范围覆盖99.5%的完整2π区间，同时在宽参数窗口内保持传输平衡度量B高于0.99。结合提供X旋转的固定谷混合元件，可通过Z-X-Z欧拉分解实现通用单量子比特控制。
