Abstract: Valley degrees of freedom in tilted Dirac materials offer a route toward fully electrical quantum control, but previous electrostatic barrier schemes have used the valley index only as a classical filtering resource. Here, we show that a smooth electrostatic barrier operated in a quantum point contact geometry at normal incidence instead realizes coherent valley phase control. In the single-mode regime, both valleys retain near-unit transmission while the tilt-induced valley-dependent traversal phase generates a controllable relative phase shift $Δd = δ_K - δ_{K'}$ between the $|K\rangle$ and $|K'\rangle$ components of the wavefunction. The resulting electrostatic element implements a tunable valley $Z$ rotation whose accessible phase range covers 99.5\% of the full $2π$ interval while maintaining a transmission-balance metric $B$ above 0.99 over a broad parameter window. Combined with a fixed valley-mixing element that supplies an $X$ rotation, this enables universal single-qubit control through a $Z$--$X$--$Z$ Euler decomposition. For realistic parameters, the ballistic gate time is $\sim$50\,fs, with particularly favourable operating windows in 8-$Pmmn$ borophene and WTe$_2$. These results establish tilted Dirac semimetals as a platform for coherent, all-electrical valley manipulation.

### [182] [Primitive-cell-resolved Crystallography for Moiré Bilayers from Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11671)
*Zhidan Li,Xianghua Kong*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种原胞分辨的莫尔晶体学框架，用于从成像数据中精确解码双层莫尔结构的几何构型，解决了现有方法对非对齐几何结构不适用的问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 建立了原胞分辨的莫尔晶体学（primitive-cell-resolved moiré crystallography）框架，引入完整描述符集$\{θ_r,\boldsymbol{\varepsilon},(T_{Mt},T_{Mb}),N_B\}$，其中整数莫尔-层矩阵$(T_{Mt},T_{Mb})$和拍频数$N_B$决定公度原胞。采用混合解析-数值工作流程重建埋层晶格，求解丢番图约束获得$(T_{Mt},T_{Mb})$和$N_B$，并提取$(θ_r,\varepsilon_b,θ_u,\varepsilon_u)$，同时平等处理泊松效应和拉伸/压缩分支。

Result: 重新分析扭曲双层石墨烯（twisted bilayer graphene）时，识别出$N_B=3$的原胞而非$N_B=9$的对齐超胞，将原子基组减少三倍，并修正了莫尔布里渊区（moiré Brillouin-zone）的构建。该框架提供了从成像到原胞分辨的原子模型和多体模型的晶体学一致路径。

Conclusion: 所提出的原胞分辨莫尔晶体学框架为工程量子系统提供了精确的几何解码方法，能够处理一般非对齐几何结构，并建立了从成像数据到原子级模型的晶体学一致路径。

Abstract: Accurate geometric decoding of moiré bilayers from imaging is essential for engineering quantum systems. Existing schemes, limited by identity or aligned assumptions requiring diagonal beating-to-moiré transformations, do not apply to general non-aligned geometries and become underdetermined when buried layers are unresolved. We establish a primitive-cell-resolved moiré crystallography framework that treats the beating-to-moiré relation in full generality and introduces a complete descriptor set $\{θ_r,\boldsymbol{\varepsilon},(T_{Mt},T_{Mb}),N_B\}$, where the integer moiré--layer matrices $(T_{Mt},T_{Mb})$ and the beating number $N_B$ determine the commensurate unit cell. A hybrid analytical--numerical workflow reconstructs buried-layer lattices, solves Diophantine constraints to obtain $(T_{Mt},T_{Mb})$ and $N_B$, and extracts $(θ_r,\varepsilon_b,θ_u,\varepsilon_u)$ with Poisson effects and tensile/compressive branches treated on equal footing. Reanalyzing twisted bilayer graphene, we identify a $N_B=3$ primitive cell rather than a $N_B=9$ aligned supercell, reducing the atomistic basis threefold and correcting the moiré Brillouin-zone construction. The framework provides a crystallographically consistent route from imaging to primitive-cell-resolved atomistic and many-body models.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究通过分析相互作用引起的能量漂移 $\partialε_k/\partial T$ 作为有效驱动力，推导了广义输运关系（generalized transport relation）。该方法将洛伦兹比（Lorenz ratio）偏差直接与热电响应（thermoelectric response）联系起来。

Result: 研究发现温度依赖的电子能带结构重整化是违反WF定律的基本机制。相互作用导致的能量漂移 $\partialε_k/\partial T$ 作为有效驱动力，从根本上解耦了热输运与电荷输运，从而解释了洛伦兹比的偏差。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解相互作用拓扑相（interacting topological phases）中的热输运提供了统一框架，并建议将洛伦兹比作为区分拓扑鲁棒性（topological robustness）与费米液体不稳定性（Fermi liquid instabilities）的探针。

Abstract: The Wiedemann-Franz (WF) law dictates a universal ratio between thermal and electrical conductivities, is widely obeyed by Fermi liquid systems. Here, we identify a fundamental yet often overlooked, thermodynamic mechanism for the violation of WF law: the temperature-dependent renormalization of the electronic band structure. We demonstrate that the interaction-induced energy drift $\partialε_k/\partial T$, acts as an effective driving force that fundamentally decouples heat transport from charge transport. We derive a generalized transport relation linking the Lorenz ratio deviation directly to the thermoelectric response. Our findings provide a unified framework for understanding thermal transport in interacting topological phases and suggest the Lorenz ratio as a probe for distinguishing topological robustness from Fermi liquid instabilities.

These samples were chosen because they exhibit strongly contrasting spectral features -peak frequencies, linewidth, skewness. While analytical expressions of the dispersion relations provide a satisfactory description of the spectra if the modes are in separate frequency domains, the exact dispersion relations and the exact mode profiles are required for a correct description of the spectra not only when mode hybridization is present in the range or near the range of frequencies and wavevector accessed by the experiment. Here, we numerically investigate a strongly-coupled trialyer square artificial spin ice under the effect of interfacial Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction (DMI). We find that the interplay between the non-reciprocity, an applied field, and the stray field within the artificial spin ice results in frequency split additional edge modes. The edge modes are favored by the DMI sign and exhibit destructive and constructive interference depending on both the DMI magnitude and the external magnetic field. Our results demonstrate the non-reciprocity in small nanoislands can affect the long-range states stabilized in the artificial spin ice due to the strong coupling between layers.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过实验研究单耦合和间接耦合两种情况，测量并区分模态衰减率γ与有效衰减率γ_eff。在间接耦合系统中观察相干完美吸收现象，分析其在磁可调失谐范围内的行为特征。

Result: 实验发现：在相干完美吸收时，有效衰减率γ_eff=0导致输出消失和dB尺度光谱变窄，而由2γ决定的本征线宽保持不变。间接耦合系统中CPA在宽磁可调失谐范围内持续存在，与直接耦合的单失谐CPA形成对比。

Conclusion: 研究表明有效衰减率而非物理损耗决定光谱振幅，间接耦合系统中的宽范围CPA特性为实现磁可重构和频率选择性微波吸收器提供了新途径。

Abstract: In this work, we report coherent perfect absorption (CPA) of anti-modes in an indirectly coupled magnon--polariton system. By examining both single and indirectly coupled cases, we experimentally distinguish the modal decay rate $γ$ from the effective decay rate $γ_{\rm{eff}}$. At CPA, $γ_{\rm{eff}} = 0$, leading to a vanishing output and a visually narrow spectrum in the dB-scale, while the intrinsic linewidth set by $2γ$ remains unchanged, demonstrating that the effective decay rate dictates the spectral amplitude rather than the physical loss. Furthermore, in the indirectly coupled system, CPA persists over a broad, magnetically tunable detuning range, in contrast to the single-detuning CPA observed in the directly coupled case, thereby enabling magnetically reconfigurable and frequency-selective microwave absorbers.

</details>


### [188] [Persistent altermagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12223)
*Warlley H. Campos,F. C. Fobasso Mbognou,Anna Birk Hellenes,Joseph Poata,Taikang Chen,Jan Priessnitz,Libor Šmejkal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种由镜面对称性和强交换驱动反铁磁序保护的持久反铁磁自旋极化（PASP）现象，在158个自旋层群和多种代表性材料中存在，并展示了其在全反铁磁结中的自旋过滤应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统具有共线自旋极化的持久自旋纹理通常源于相对论性自旋轨道耦合，导致自旋分裂较弱且自旋相干性脆弱。本研究旨在探索一种由镜面对称性和强交换驱动反铁磁序保护的更稳健的共线自旋极化机制。

Method: 结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）与对自旋和磁层群的系统分类，识别持久反铁磁自旋极化（persistent altermagnetic spin polarization, PASP）现象。在代表性材料V₂Te₂O、La₂CuO₄和VSI₂中进行验证，并理论演示VSI₂中的铁电可切换性。

Result: 识别出PASP存在于158个自旋层群中，并在金属性V₂Te₂O、绝缘性La₂CuO₄和半导体性VSI₂等代表性材料中得到证实。理论证明VSI₂中的PASP具有铁电可切换性，且这种切换能在模型全反铁磁结中导致自旋过滤电导的大幅变化。

Conclusion: 研究结果为在全反铁磁磁性存储器和自旋晶体管器件中应用PASP开辟了可能性，并建立了自旋轨道耦合单层中反铁磁性的普适原理。PASP现象为自旋电子学应用提供了更稳健的平台。

Abstract: Persistent spin textures with collinear spin polarization are promising platforms for spintronics applications. However, their typically relativistic spin-orbit origin leads to weak spin splittings and fragile spin coherence. Here, we demonstrate a previously overlooked class of robust collinear spin polarization protected by mirror symmetry in combination with a strong exchange-driven altermagnetic order, which persists even in the presence of spin-orbit coupling. By combining first-principles calculations with a systematic classification of spin and magnetic layer groups, we identify this phenomenon-termed persistent altermagnetic spin polarization (PASP)-to occur in 158 spin layer groups and in representative materials including metallic V$_2$Te$_2$O, insulating La$_2$CuO$_4$, and semiconducting VSI$_2$. Furthermore, we theoretically demonstrate that PASP is ferroelectrically switchable in VSI$_2$. Finally, we show that this PASP switching can lead to large changes in spin-filtering conductance in a model all-altermagnetic junction. Our results open the possibility of employing PASP in all-altermagnetic magnetic memory and spin-transistor devices and establish universal principles of altermagnetism in spin-orbit-coupled monolayers.

</details>


### [189] [Quantum Inductance as a Phase-Sensitive Probe of Fermion Parity Switching in Majorana Nanowires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12256)
*Binayyak B. Roy,Jay D. Sau,Sumanta Tewari*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析一维半导体-超导体Majorana纳米线与量子点耦合的干涉装置中的量子电感，提出结合量子电容和量子电感测量可可靠区分拓扑非平庸的费米子宇称转换与无序导致的虚假信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管量子电容测量已实验证明可实现快速费米子宇称读取，但无法可靠确认受保护的费米子宇称转换（拓扑非平庸性和Majorana零模存在的关键标志）。实际器件中无序可能导致能级避免交叉或窄双交叉，模拟受保护单宇称转换行为，产生拓扑非平庸行为的假阳性信号。

Method: 研究采用通用Lehmann框架，应用于有效模型和包含无序的完整微观模拟。通过分析一维半导体-超导体Majorana纳米线与量子点耦合的干涉装置中的通量依赖量子电感，探究其对低能谱相位结构的敏感性。

Result: 仅真正的费米子宇称转换产生受保护交叉的特征电感响应，而拓扑平庸的避免交叉或窄双交叉产生的量子电感特征与拓扑非平庸费米子宇称交叉显著不同。量子电感作为互补探针，可直接敏感于低能谱的相位结构。

Conclusion: 量子电容和量子电感的联合测量提供了稳健且实验可实现的识别真正费米子宇称转换的方法，对应非平庸Pfaffian不变量。该方法能可靠区分受保护宇称转换与无序导致的虚假信号。

Abstract: We study the flux-dependent quantum inductance of a one-dimensional (1D) semiconductor-superconductor (SM-SC) Majorana nanowire coupled to a quantum dot in an interferometric setup. Although quantum capacitance in this setup enables fast fermion parity readout, as has been demonstrated experimentally, it cannot by itself reliably confirm a protected fermion parity switch, a key signature of non-trivial topology and the existence of Majorana zero modes (MZMs). In realistic devices, disorder can produce avoided crossings or narrow double crossings between the two parity sectors that can mimic the behavior of a protected single parity switching, leading to false positives for non-trivial topological behavior. We show that quantum inductance provides a complementary probe that is directly sensitive to the phase structure of the low energy spectrum, allowing us to distinguish genuine fermion-parity crossings from avoided crossings or narrow double crossings. Using a general Lehmann framework applied to both effective models and full microscopic simulations with disorder, we demonstrate that only a true fermion-parity switch produces the characteristic inductive response of a protected crossing. In contrast, topologically trivial avoided crossings or narrow double crossings yield quantum inductance signatures that are markedly different from those of topologically nontrivial fermion parity crossings. Therefore, our results show that combined measurements of quantum capacitance and quantum inductance provide a robust and experimentally accessible means to identify true fermion-parity switches, corresponding to a nontrivial Pfaffian invariant.

</details>

### [190] [A counterexample to Fermi isospectral rigidity for two dimensional discrete periodic Schrödinger operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11183)
*Taylor Brysiewicz,Matthew Faust,Wencai Liu*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 通过数值验证，证明了存在非平凡二维周期势能，其离散薛定谔算子与零势能费米等谱，从而否定了二维费米等谱刚性问题，并推翻了关于二维周期势能费米簇不可约性的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决第三作者提出的关于二维费米等谱（Fermi isospectrality）刚性问题，并检验Gieseker、Knörrer和Trubowitz在1990年代提出的猜想：任何非平凡二维实值周期势能的费米簇（Fermi variety）在所有能级都是不可约的。

Method: 采用数值验证（numerical certification）方法，证明存在一个非平凡的二维实值周期势能，其关联的离散薛定谔算子（discrete Schrödinger operator）与零势能费米等谱。

Result: 成功构造了一个非平凡二维周期势能，其离散薛定谔算子与零势能费米等谱，这为二维费米等谱刚性问题提供了否定答案，并推翻了Gieseker等人的猜想。

Conclusion: 二维费米等谱不具有刚性，存在非平凡周期势能与零势能费米等谱；同时，二维周期势能的费米簇在某些能级可能是可约的，这与先前猜想相悖。

Abstract: Using numerical certification, we prove the existence of a nontrivial real-valued two dimensional periodic potential whose associated discrete Schrödinger operator is Fermi isospectral to the zero potential. This provides a negative answer to a question posed by the third author concerning the rigidity of Fermi isospectrality in dimension two. This example also disproves a conjecture of Gieseker, Knörrer, and Trubowitz in the 1990s stating that for any nontrivial real-valued periodic potential in dimension two, the Fermi variety is irreducible at all energy levels.

### [191] [The Einstein condition for quantum irreducible flag manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11786)
*Marco Matassa*

TL;DR: 该论文证明任何量子不可约旗流形（quantum irreducible flag manifold）在量子化参数经典值附近的小开区间内满足爱因斯坦条件的类似物，即里奇张量与度规成比例。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用与这些代数相关的各种规范构造，包括微分计算（differential calculi）和双模连接（bimodule connections），这些构造先前已由多位作者引入。

Result: 证明任何量子不可约旗流形至少在量子化参数经典值附近的小开区间内满足爱因斯坦条件的类似物，表现为里奇张量（Ricci tensor）与度规（metric）之间的比例关系。

Conclusion: 量子不可约旗流形在量子化参数经典值邻域内表现出与经典爱因斯坦条件相似的几何特性，这为量子几何的研究提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We show that any quantum irreducible flag manifold satisfies an analogue of the Einstein condition, expressing proportionality between the Ricci tensor and the metric, at least in a small open interval around the classical value of the quantization parameter. This makes use of various canonical constructions associated to these algebras, such as differential calculi and bimodule connections, which were previously introduced by various authors.

### [192] [Autoparallels and the Inverse Problem of the Calculus of Variations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11581)
*Lavinia Heisenberg*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了与无挠但非度规相容的仿射联络相关的自平行曲线可以从作用量原理推导出来。通过构造作用量泛函并使用标准变分技术，得到了所需的自平行方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自平行曲线在非度规性存在情况下是否具有一致的变分表述，为度量-仿射几何中的粒子运动提供变分框架，并为相对论引力中的测地线原理奠定数学基础。

Method: 基于系统求解变分法的逆问题及相关赫姆霍兹条件，明确构造了作用量泛函，并采用标准变分技术进行推导。

Result: 证明了自平行曲线可以从作用量原理推导，即使在非度规性存在的情况下，自平行的动力学也允许一致的变分表述。

Conclusion: 为度量-仿射几何中的粒子运动提供了变分框架，对相对论引力中测地线原理的数学基础做出了贡献。

Abstract: We prove that autoparallel curves associated with a torsion-free but not necessarily metric-compatible affine connection can be derived from an action principle. We explicitly construct the action functional and show by standard variational techniques that it produces the desired equations. Our analysis is based on systematically solving the inverse problem of the calculus of variation and the associated Helmholtz conditions. This demonstrates that the dynamics of autoparallels admit a consistent variational formulation even in the presence of non-metricity. Our results provide a variational framework for particle motion in metric-affine geometries and thereby contribute to the mathematical foundations of the geodesic principle in relativistic gravity.

### [193] [Systems of partial differential equations describing pseudo-spherical or spherical surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11674)
*Mingyue Guo,Jing Kang,Zhenhua Shi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究描述常曲率曲面的非线性偏微分方程组，基于联络1-形式的平坦条件，对Camassa-Holm型方程组进行分类，并应用于构建新系统和非局部对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究描述常曲率曲面的非线性偏微分方程组（nonlinear partial differential equations），特别是针对Camassa-Holm型方程组的分类问题。通过分析联络1-形式（connection 1-forms）的平坦条件，为这类系统提供系统性的分类框架。

Method: 基于联络1-形式的平坦条件（flatness condition），对具有特定形式的Camassa-Holm型方程组进行分类。该方法适用于描述伪球面（pseudospherical）或球面（spherical）曲面的系统，其中F和G为光滑函数，m,n≥2。同时建立了特殊类型三阶系统的分类结果。

Result: 研究结果提供了Camassa-Holm型方程组的分类，并给出了新的系统实例，包括Song-Qu-Qiao系统、具有三次非线性的双分量Camassa-Holm系统（two-component Camassa-Holm system with cubic nonlinearity）以及修正的Camassa-Holm型系统。此外，从谱参数（spectral parameters）的梯度构造了具有三次非线性的双分量Camassa-Holm系统的非局部对称性（nonlocal symmetry）和非平凡解。

Conclusion: 本文通过联络1-形式的平坦条件成功分类了描述常曲率曲面的Camassa-Holm型方程组，为这类系统提供了新的实例和解析工具。所构建的非局部对称性和非平凡解展示了该方法在求解具体系统中的应用价值。

Abstract: In this paper, we study systems of nonlinear partial differential equations which describe surfaces of constant curvature. From the flatness condition of connection 1-forms, we present a classification of systems of Camassa-Holm-type equations of the form \begin{equation*} \left\{ \begin{aligned} u_{t} - u_{xxt} &= F(x, t, u, u_{x}, \dots, \partial ^{m} u/\partial _x^{m}, v, v_{x}, \dots, \partial ^{n} v/\partial _x^{n}), \\ v_{t} - v_{xxt} &= G(x, t, u, u_{x}, \dots, \partial ^{m} u/\partial _x^{m}, v, v_{x}, \dots, \partial ^{n} v/\partial _x^{n}), \end{aligned} \right. \end{equation*} with $m,n\geq2$, for $F$ and $G$ smooth functions, describing pseudospherical or spherical surfaces. We also establish classification results for a special type of third-order system. Applications of the results provide new examples of such systems, such as the Song-Qu-Qiao system, the two-component Camassa-Holm system with cubic nonlinearity, and the modified Camass-Holm-type system. Moreover, we construct the nonlocal symmetry and a non-trivial solutions for the two-component Camassa-Holm system with cubic nonlinearity from the gradients of spectral parameters.

</details>


### [194] [On Exotic Materials in 3D Linear Elasticity with High Symmetry Classes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12019)
*Nicolas Auffray,Guangjin Mou,Boris Desmorat*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统分类了三维线性弹性框架下的奇异（exotic）弹性结构，即那些在特定载荷下表现出比其固有材料对称性更高对称性的各向异性材料，共枚举出18种高于正交各向异性（orthotropy）对称类的奇异结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇异（exotic）弹性材料在特定载荷下表现出比其固有材料对称性更高的机械响应对称性，这类材料在概念和功能上介于两个不同对称类之间，具有重要的实际应用价值。它们能够实现超材料（metamaterials）的定制设计，以调和原本不相容的机械要求，例如在固有各向异性介质中实现杨氏模量（Young's modulus）的方向性各向同性。

Method: 本研究在三维线性弹性（three-dimensional linear elasticity）框架下对奇异结构进行系统分类。通过详尽分类，枚举出所有高于正交各向异性（orthotropy）对称类的奇异弹性结构。

Result: 分类结果共识别出18种奇异结构，这些结构对应着高于正交各向异性（orthotropy）的对称类。研究还详细分析了奇异弹性行为的代表性示例。

Conclusion: 本研究完成了三维线性弹性框架下奇异弹性结构的系统分类，为设计能够调和不相容机械要求的超材料提供了理论基础，特别是通过枚举18种高于正交各向异性的奇异结构，为材料设计开辟了新途径。

Abstract: An anisotropic elastic material is referred to as exotic when, under specific loadings, its mechanical response exhibits a higher degree of symmetry than that prescribed by its intrinsic material symmetry. Such materials, which may be regarded as lying, conceptually and functionally, between two distinct symmetry classes, are of significant practical relevance. They enable the tailored design of metamaterials capable of reconciling otherwise incompatible mechanical requirements; for example, achieving directional isotropy of the Young's modulus in an intrinsically anisotropic medium. This work focuses on the systematic classification of exotic structures within the framework of three-dimensional linear elasticity. An exhaustive classification is carried out, leading to the enumeration of 18 exotic structures corresponding to symmetry classes higher than orthotropy. Representative examples of exotic elastic behaviours are analysed in detail.

</details>


### [195] [The Euclidean $φ^4_2$ theory as a limit of an inhomogeneous Bose gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12241)
*Cristina Caraci,Antti Knowles,Alessio Ranallo,Pedro Torres Giesteira*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明了在二维量子玻色气体中，当气体密度增大且相互作用范围减小时，其巨正则吉布斯态收敛于具有局域四次自相互作用的复欧几里得场论，并获得了重整化约化密度矩阵的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维量子玻色气体在囚禁势场中的统计力学行为，探索其在高密度和短程相互作用极限下与量子场论的对应关系，解决非均匀囚禁势场带来的新数学挑战。

Method: 通过证明相对配分函数的收敛性，以及在$L^1 \cap L^\infty$空间中重整化约化密度矩阵的收敛性。推导了薛定谔算子及其梯度的格林函数的定量界限，这些界限可能具有独立的研究价值。

Result: 证明了巨正则吉布斯态收敛于具有局域四次自相互作用的复欧几里得场论，该场论由负正则性的分布支撑，需要通过发散的质量和能量抵消项进行重整化。与均匀环面情况不同，抵消项不是有限个标量而是发散的函数。

Conclusion: 二维量子玻色气体在高密度和短程相互作用极限下确实收敛于特定的量子场论，但囚禁势场引入了新的数学复杂性，表现为抵消项成为发散函数而非简单标量，这为相关数学物理问题提供了新的研究视角。

Abstract: We prove that the grand canonical Gibbs state of an interacting two-dimensional quantum Bose gas confined by a trapping potential converges to the complex Euclidean field theory with local quartic self-interaction, when the density of the gas becomes large and the range of the interaction becomes small. We obtain convergence of the relative partition function and convergence in $L^1 \cap L^\infty$ of the renormalised reduced density matrices. The field theory is supported on distributions of negative regularity, which requires a renormalisation by divergent mass and energy counterterms. Unlike previous results in the homogeneous setting of the torus without a trapping potential, the counterterms are not given by a finite collection of scalars but by diverging counterterm functions. This leads to significant new mathematical challenges. For our proof, we also derive quantitative bounds on the Green function of Schrödinger operators and of its gradient, which might be of independent interest.

</details>
